Chapter 451: Nine-Netherworlds Creed Leader Mu Baiyi

When Yun Zhi arrived at Incarceration Peak, the childlike Grand-Shifu was stunned to see two more Transcendent Tribulation souls.

How long has it been since the last Transcendent Tribulation cultivator? And now two more?

Doing the math, four Transcendent Tribulation cultivators have been captured in a year. At this rate, I’ll soon be unable to maintain control over Incarceration Peak. No matter how strong I am, I can’t manage so many Transcendent Tribulation prisoners here. In fact, no one can.

“Actually, there are three. I’ve refined one into an artifact spirit. Little Junior Brother was the one who encountered all three during his outing.”

Grand-Shifu’s cheek twitched. This grand-disciple surpasses even that brat Taciturn in stirring up trouble!

And he’s only at the Golden Core Stage now. What horrors await when he grows stronger?

“I still can’t enjoy peace after retirement,” Grand-Shifu sighed. I’d retired early and thrown all the mess to those nine simply because it was too mentally taxing.

That generation of the Dao-Seeking Sect had produced numerous talents, but nine stood above the rest. Referred to as the “Dao-Seeking Nine,” they were viewed as the hope of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Coincidentally, all nine are my disciples.

When I was sect leader, my days were spent cleaning up their endless messes. Thanks to them, I became acquainted with every major figure in the cultivation world. I’ve desperately cultivated until the Transcendent Tribulation Stage just so that I can discipline these rascals.

As their shifu, if all I can do is watch these little rascals cause chaos without being able to stop them, wouldn’t I die of sheer frustration and anger?

“Had I known, I should’ve swapped with Junior Brother. He can take Incarceration Peak while I stay in the scripture library.” Grand-Shifu sighed as he locked up Wu Youdao and the Azure Lightning Venerable Lord.

~~~

Lu Yang swaggered through the Dao-Seeking Sect as he casually swung the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord’s chained soul, looking like he was asking for a beating. Fortunately, he successfully arrived at Hundred Refinements Peak without getting beaten up.

There, he happened to see Li Haoran sparring with Qin Yanyan.

Qin Yanyan had morphed into a cloud of white mist, ethereal and elusive. Talismans lay concealed within, ready to strike Li Haoran when he least expected it.

Li Haoran was not one to be forced into pure defense. He removed his wig and spun it to disperse the smoke.

Father and daughter clashed, neither gaining a clear advantage.

“Misty Cloud Golden Core?” Lu Yang recognized Qin Yanyan’s golden core. It was a first-grade golden core.

This golden core granted its bearer the ability to transform into mist, tangible yet formless, making it useful for combat, defense, and escape.

All of Li Haoran’s training with his ex-daughter paid off.

“You’ve formed your golden core. Congratulations,” Lu Yang cheered, drawing the father-daughter pair’s attention and prompting them to halt their duel.

“Senior Brother Lu, what brings you here?” Li Haoran was unaware of their trip to Wilderness Province. He simply felt it had been unnervingly quiet without seeing Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou for the past month.

Suffering from a karmic backlash wasn’t exactly glorious, so Meng Jingzhou naturally kept it a secret. The Dao-Seeking Sect’s disciples only knew Qiu Jin’an had ambushed the sect. Beyond that, they were clueless.

“Oh, Old Meng and I made a trip to Wilderness Province. We caught a Transcendent Tribulation Soul, and Big Senior Sister asked me to deliver it to Fifth Elder.” Lu Yang lifted the chain, his tone as casual as bringing back some small souvenirs for his neighbors after returning from a trip.

Despite having almost grown accustomed to Lu Yang’s luck, the father-daughter duo found themselves speechless. Are Transcendent Tribulation souls some roadside cabbages that can be easily encountered?

“Shifu is refining artifacts atop the peak,” Li Haoran directed.

“Alright, I’ll be right back. I happen to have something I’d like to ask you.”

Li Haoran was puzzled but nodded.

At the summit, Lu Yang found Fifth Elder scowling at a wok in deep contemplation, looking extremely conflicted. “Fifth Elder, what are you doing?”

“Since our Heavenly Court Creed partnered with the Nine-Netherworlds Creed by relying on the Automatic Barbecue Array, I was wondering whether we could develop some automatic stir-frying magical treasure.”

“Any success?”

“Not much. I’ve run into many problems. For example, this wok’s offensive power is too high, but I can’t pinpoint why. Anyway, what brings you here...Transcendent Tribulation souls?!” Fifth Elder snapped out of his daze. At the sight of the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord’s soul in Lu Yang’s grasp, his eyes lit up brighter than if he’d seen his wife. He rubbed his hands gleefully with a grin that split from ear to ear.

“Big Senior Sister told me to hand this to you, saying it can be used as an artifact spirit.”

“Just as I hoped!” Fifth Elder accepted the chain as though it was a sacred treasure.

With a Transcendent Tribulation soul, he was confident of forging a Transcendent Tribulation-tier magical treasure. It would be a valuable experience, and the process would be a massive boon in advancing his craft.

Fifth Elder hurled the automatic stir-frying wok to the side. Who cares about researching automatic stir-frying woks when there’s a chance to forge Transcendent Tribulation-tier magical treasures?

Lu Yang bid goodbye to the now-unhearing Fifth Elder and descended the mountain to look for Li Haoran.

“In Wilderness Province, I encountered someone from the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. See if you recognize him?” Lu Yang conjured an image of the white paper-hatted man.

“Mu Baiyi?”[1]

“This person is called Mu Baiyi?”

“I can’t be wrong. It’s definitely Mu Baiyi. In Qin Haoran’s memories, he’s one of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s four vice creed leaders and the youngest among them.”

“He’s now the creed leader.” While Lu Yang couldn’t ascertain whether Mu Baiyi was the creed leader, the combat power he displayed during the battle in Hanshui City confirmed his status as the creed leader.

“He became the creed leader?” Li Haoran was slightly surprised. In terms of seniority or cultivation, Mu Baiyi hadn’t been outstanding. Even Shi Huagu seemed more likely to become the creed leader.

“Could he have made some promise, like building Fengdu Ghost city or whatnot?” Li Haoran mused. With no other advantages, the only possibility is that Mu Baiyi pledged to build the Fengdu Ghost City after becoming the creed leader. That way, the neutral faction would have swayed to him.

“That doesn’t make sense either. The Nine-Netherworlds Creed is so poor. Qin Haoran was chased by debtors every day. Where would he get the construction funds from?” Li Haoran was flummoxed.

“Mu Baiyi excels in cloning and transformation techniques; he can transform into anyone. He said that when he studied in a sect in his youth, his senior and junior brothers were unwilling to go to the learning hall and preferred cultivating by themselves. However, the elder at the learning hall often did roll calls, so they paid Mu Baiyi to answer for them.

“Since Mu Baiyi was from a poor background and lacked spirit stones, he agreed.

“Mu Baiyi was conscientious and took his duties seriously. To avoid detection, he mastered cloning and transformation techniques.”

“Then why did he join the Nine-Netherworlds Creed instead of continuing his studies at the sect?” Lu Yang was curious. “Did the elder find out that he was calling roll for others and expel him from the sect?” Who would abandon studying in a sect to join a diabolic creed?

“That didn’t happen. The sect simply disbanded.”

“Disbanded?” Lu Yang was even more bewildered. Why would a sect suddenly dissolve for no reason?

“The sect also found it strange. Despite many students attending the learning hall with a perfect attendance rate, their final assessment results were disastrous...except for Mu Baiyi’s stellar performance.

“The sect concluded that they weren’t fit as educators, and they disbanded to avoid hampering their disciples’ progress any further.”

Lu Yang, “...”

1. The given name “Baiyi” literally means “white clothes.” The full name sounds like “admire white clothes.” ☜

Chapter 452: This Heavenly Court Creed Is Most Likely a New Diabolic Creed!

In the imperial palace, the Xia Emperor dismissed eunuchs and palace maids, leaving only himself and the representatives of the Five Great Immortal Sects to discuss matters.

“Fellow Daoist Yun, it’s been a while.”

“You’re too courteous, Palace Leader.”

“Fellow Daoist Qiu, I heard you were involved in the Hanshui City incident from start to end?”

“I was lucky to have survived.”

The six exchanged brief pleasantries—except for the abbot of the Hanging Monastery, who remained silent as he was currently practicing the Mouth-Shut Chan Meditation.

Seeing that everyone had arrived, the Xia Emperor cut to the chase. “Regarding the events at Hanshui City, I presume all five of you are generally aware of what transpired. Had it not been for the intervention by an unexpected figure at the end, Great Yu would likely have seized our national fortune’s power.”

Originally, Yun Zhi had intended to convene a meeting among the righteous path. However, after the Xia Emperor learned of the Hanshui City incident, he preemptively summoned the five here.

In terms of outcome, there doesn’t seem to be much difference.

The Xia Emperor’s eyes burned with indignation. It would have been catastrophic if the national fortune had been stolen. The old ancestor might have personally stepped in to reclaim it, which would disrupt all subsequent plans.

“Old Qiu, as someone who had personally gone through the events at Hanshui City, please recount what happened.” The leader of the Prison Suppression Sect spoke up. His burly frame bore glimpses of tattoos on his necks, wrists, and ankles, suggesting that his whole body was covered in battle tattoos—a sign of his major success in the cultivation of battle tattoos.

Qiu Jin’an had already completed dealing with the aftermath in Hanshui City and came to the palace to join the discussion. “My presence in Hanshui City was purely accidental. An evil person schemed against me and cursed me, and I needed the power of the national fortune to erase the curse. Thus, I went to the nearest city, Hanshui City, to seek help from the national fortune.

“At the time, Hanshui City was plagued by ghost calamities. It was the work of Great Yu cultivators, though no one realized it then.

“Shortly after that, Wu Youdao appeared and used his Transcendent Tribulation power of ‘Rules’ to seal off the city and prevent news from leaking out, wreaking havoc within the city.”

“Wu Youdao? The sixth Yu emperor?” interjected Luo Hongxia, the palace leader of the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace.

“Yes, that’s him. He was born with the destiny of a monarch and used Dragon-Tier Qi during the battle, making him an intractable opponent. Provincial Governor Lü and I could barely hold our own even by joining forces.

“When the battle fell into a stalemate, a man in a white paper hat appeared, displaying combat prowess that matched mine.”

“Matched yours?” The Prison Suppression Sect’s leader was slightly surprised. I know Qiu Jin’an’s strength. For that man to be on par with him, he couldn’t have been a nobody.

“Although that person never identified himself, his moves seemed to be from the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. And the only one there who could rival me is their creed leader!

“After the incident, I investigated him and found that he had left traces all across Wilderness Province in recent years. He used cloning techniques to commit crimes and was wanted by the local authorities. However, his crimes relied on wit and didn’t reveal his true cultivation, so the local authorities underestimated his cultivation.

“Just as the three of us were about to defeat Wu Youdao, the Azure Lightning Venerable Lord appeared. Even more devastating was the fact that the Corpse-Driving Sect Leader’s body had been taken over by the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord. This meant that Hanshui City faced the threat of three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators.

“The Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord exploited the Corpse-Driving Sect Leader’s identity and the Wilderness Province’s official seal to temporarily sever Provincial Governor Lü’s control over the national fortune.

“As I prepared for a last stand, a female cultivator appeared, her strength and origins unknown. Calling herself the Supreme Grand Heavenly Sovereign of the Heavenly Court Creed, Dou Heavenly Sovereign, she harnessed the masterless national fortune to crush Wu Youdao’s trio single-handedly, wiping the floor with them!

“Unfortunately, Wu Youdao and the other two still managed to escape after that.”

Although the Xia Emperor had heard Provincial Governor Lü’s report, Qiu Jin’an’s recount still shocked him. To dominate these three opponents at once with such ease implies that Dou Heavenly Sovereign’s true cultivation realm is far above Wu Youdao’s trio.

At minimum, she must be a half-immortal!

“What is this Heavenly Court Creed? Why have I never heard of it?” The Prison Suppression Sect’s leader voiced everyone’s question.

After racking their brains and combing through their memories, all they could recall were fragmented references in ancient texts to a “Heavenly Court,” but the accounts varied so widely that historians had never been able to verify its existence.

What is the relationship between the ancient Heavenly Court and the Heavenly Court Creed?

“I’ve never heard of it either. Judging by the reaction of Wu Youdao’s trio, neither had they heard of the Heavenly Court Creed. But the Nine-Netherworlds Creed Leader’s response indicated he knew of the Heavenly Court Creed.

“When he saw Dou Heavenly Sovereign show up, though he was also startled, he seemed more delighted. He later told me that Dou Heavenly Sovereign was an ineffable puissant personage who could casually play with the stars like they were beans.”

“Play with the stars? Dou Heavenly Sovereign is a figure from ancient times?” The Xia Emperor drummed his fingers on the table.

Everyone present was a high-ranking figure in the cultivation world; few things were secret to them. They all knew that the stars in the sky had vanished, replaced by Yun Zhi’s golden cores. In other words, no one in the current cultivation world could play with the stars like they were beans.

Dou Heavenly Sovereign can only be a figure from ancient times.

With cultivators from the Great Yu and Great Qian dynasties resurfacing, even cultivators from the ancient era are emerging, and an ancient expert at that. But which ancient expert is she? Even if ancient history has many gaps, it wouldn’t have left out the title of such a figure!

“More and more factions are joining this Battle of the Great Era, huh?” the Prison Suppression Sect Leader lamented.

Qiu Jin’an nodded. “My thoughts exactly. I suspect this Heavenly Court Creed is related to the ancient Heavenly Court. Though there are many versions of the ancient Heavenly Court, one thing remains constant—the Heavenly Court was the ruler of the ancient era!”

Drawing on his expertise in ancient knowledge, he made a bold conjecture. “If we deduce further, the Heavenly Court Creed’s objective may be to restore the dominion of the ancient Heavenly Court. This also explains why Dou Heavenly Sovereign attacked Wu Youdao’s faction. It’s because of a conflict of interest.”

Luo Hongxia continued the analysis. “The Nine-Netherworlds Creed Leader is acquainted with Dou Heavenly Sovereign, which points to a connection between the two creeds!”

The Prison Suppression Sect Leader also grasped hold of another clue. “To have a figure like Dou Heavenly Sovereign, the Heavenly Court Creed must be formidable. Yet we know nothing about their existence. This means they have acted covertly until now, making a flashy debut to announce themselves to the world with absolute power!”

The Hanging Monastery’s abbot also wished to speak but couldn’t due to his cultivation of the Mouth-Shut Chan Meditation. Thus, the Xia Emperor stated the conclusion in his stead. “This Heavenly Court Creed is most likely a new diabolic creed! With the Everlasting Immortal Creed annihilated, the Four Great Diabolic Creeds were down to three. Now, with this addition, they’re back to four!”

Everyone nodded in agreement.

Just then, Qiu Jin’an noticed that Yun Zhi had kept silent all this time. “Fellow Daoist Yun, you are the most erudite and possess the highest cultivation among us. What are your thoughts about the Heavenly Court Creed?”

Yun Zhi surveyed and calmly said, “I am the creed leader of the Heavenly Court Creed.”

“!!!”

Chapter 453: The Heavenly Court Creed’s Members All Belong to the Righteous Path, so How Could It Be a Diabolic Creed?

“You’re the Heavenly Court Creed Leader?!” Qiu Jin’an shot to his feet, his eyes wide with belief and his voice jumping an octave.

The others reacted similarly. Even the Hanging Monastery’s abbot broke his composure, fearing that Yun Zhi would smirk ominously and state, “This concerns the Heavenly Court’s million-year plan. No mishaps are permitted,” while eliminating all five of them.

A ripple of confusion surfaced in Yun Zhi’s calm gaze. Weren’t you the ones who asked for my opinion on the Heavenly Court Creed? I answered truthfully, so why do you have such strong reactions?

Their intense reactions were understandable. This was Great Xia’s imperial palace, the stronghold of the righteous path, and everyone present was a leader in their own right. After extensive analysis citing classical texts, they had concluded that the Heavenly Court Creed harbored treasonous ambitions as a new diabolic creed, reforming the new Four Great Diabolic Creeds with the other three diabolic creeds.

Yet you suddenly revealed that you are the Heavenly Court Creed Leader—anyone would have reacted this way.

Most importantly, you are the strongest cultivator among all six present.

Noticing everyone overreacting, Yun Zhi felt there was a need to clarify. “Everyone, you need not worry. The Heavenly Court Creed is an internal organization of the Dao-Seeking Sect—it’s safe and trustworthy. It was formed at the proposal of my Little Junior Brother, Lu Yang, with the purpose of infiltrating the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.”

“Lu Yang?” While Qiu Jin’an and Luo Hongxia were aware of Lu Yang’s existence, the Xia Emperor and the other leaders were unfamiliar with his name.

Lu Yang’s talent was stellar, capable of defeating cultivators who dispersed their cultivation to cultivate anew with sangfroid. He was the undisputed number one among the younger generation, but his cultivation realm was too low to catch the attention of these people at the top.

Of course, if he had leveraged the identity of an ancient history scholar, he could have gained fame easily.

Despite Lu Yang’s meritorious contributions in the destruction of the Everlasting Creed, Yun Zhi’s involvement in the battle prevented others from attributing any of the success to a mere Foundation Establishment cultivator like Lu Yang.

“Lu Yang is our shifu’s newest disciple and my Little Junior Brother. He is exceptionally gifted in spells and cultivation. His role in the eradication of the Everlasting Creed was pivotal.”

Everyone was floored. For Yun Zhi to praise someone’s talent in spells as “exceptional,” just how terrifying must Lu Yang’s talent be?

And what else did Fellow Daoist Yun say? Lu Yang played an integral role in the annihilation of the Everlasting Creed? Could Lu Yang have been the key factor to the creed’s destruction?

But Lu Yang’s cultivation at the time... How could he have achieved that?

“I’ve met Lu Yang. He’s indeed a genius with unconventional thinking,” Qiu Jin’an attested. “He once defeated a reforged Great Yu Fusion cultivator at the same cultivation realm.”

“Defeated a reforged Great Yu Fusion cultivator?!” Luo Hongxia covered her mouth. Everyone here was a prodigy in their youth, but even then, such a feat would have been challenging.

“And not just that.” Qiu Jin’an dropped another bombshell. “During the exchange between the Five-Elements Sect and the Dao-Seeking Sect, the Dao-Seeking Sect even claimed that Lu Yang’s combat prowess was extraordinary, defeating Golden Core, Nascent Soul, and Divine Transfiguration cultivators while still at the Foundation Establishment Stage!” This piece of information was even more shocking than Lu Yang defeating the reforged cultivator.

“Fellow Daoist Yun, is this true?”

After a rare hesitation, Yun Zhi nodded, eliciting gasps.

She realized the conversation had unknowingly gone off track and needed to be steered back. “I am the creed leader of the Heavenly Court Creed. There are nine Heavenly Kings protectors from First Elder to Eighth Elder, plus my shifu, but he is still unaware that he has joined the Heavenly Court Creed.

“Apart from them, we have five disciples recruited from the Dao-Seeking Sect—Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, Tao Yaoye, Man Gu, and Li Haoran.” Yun Zhi didn’t reveal the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s existence.

“Everyone, you may have some misunderstanding about the Heavenly Court Creed. We, the Dao-Seeking Sect, belong to the righteous path, and since the Heavenly Court Creed’s members are composed entirely of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s higher-ups and promising disciples, how could it be a diabolic creed?” Yun Zhi declared matter-of-factly.

Since the Heavenly Court Creed’s members are righteous cultivators, the Heavenly Court Creed is naturally a faction of the righteous path.

The five other people’s eyelids twitched. Due to their status and seniority, they couldn’t refute her.

“Then, this Dou Heavenly Sovereign...” Qiu Jin’an suddenly recalled the Nine-Netherworlds Creed Leader’s words.

“Dou Heavenly Sovereign casually plays with the stars like they are beans.”

Since the stars in the skies are Yun Zhi’s golden cores, she could naturally casually play with the stars!

And as for her peerless record of being unbeatable among her peers and defeating three opponents alone, Yun Zhi could totally achieve that with the national fortune’s power!

Lu Yang is also Yun Zhi’s Little Junior Brother, which means that Yun Zhi would secretly protect him whenever he goes out.

It aligns; everything matches up!

Those present were all clever individuals, quickly inferring that Yun Zhi was Dou Heavenly Sovereign.

Although Yun Zhi didn’t give a direct answer, everyone had a tacit understanding. We get it. It’s fine even if she doesn’t answer.

Yun Zhi continued, “The Heavenly Court Creed has already gained the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s trust. I advise against making a move on them for the time being to avoid alerting them prematurely.”

“Of course,” everyone readily agreed. Now that we know that the Heavenly Court Creed is on our side, things become much easier.

“The Heavenly Court Creed and the Nine-Netherworlds Creed have established a preliminary collaboration, where the Heavenly Court Creed provides technical expertise, while the Nine-Netherworlds Creed provides manpower. We have opened a barbeque franchise, with business just in its initial phase. The more creed followers involved in running the barbeque shops, the lower the likelihood of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed committing evil. Hence, I hope the imperial court can craft policies to invigorate the food and beverage industry, thereby discreetly supporting the development of the barbeque business.”

The Xia Emperor considered the idea. Boosting the food and beverage sector would benefit taxation, the nation, and the public. It’s a good initiative. “This can be arranged.”

“That’s great then. One more thing. Wu Youdao’s trio is in the Dao-Seeking Sect, and I managed to obtain some intelligence from them.”

Everyone exchanged knowing looks. But of course! With Yun Zhi right in Hanshui City, how could she have let them escape?

As Yun Zhi relayed Wu Youdao’s confession, the mood sombered.

“Just as I suspected,” the Xia Emperor sneered. “Daring to scheme against our national fortune means they must possess immortal-level combat power.” He was hardly surprised upon learning the cultivation realms of the two imperial preceptors.

Great Yu’s goal was to replace Great Xia. Despite knowing the national fortune is the creation of an immortal, they dared to entertain such ambitions, which could only prove that Great Yu had an immortal on their side.

“Great Yu’s next target is Ji Province, which is densely populated with many cities. It would be difficult to conduct a thorough search with the imperial court’s power alone. Thus, I’d like to request the immortal sects to lend a hand.”

Locating the whereabouts of Great Yu cultivators required cultivators to be minimally at the Fusion Stage. Even if the imperial court had many Fusion cultivators, they couldn’t dispatch all of them to Ji Province, for other areas also required Fusion cultivators to keep watch. Furthermore, Fusion cultivators from immortal sects were of better quality than those from the imperial court, enabling better response time and communication efficiency.

“This concerns Great Xia’s stability. The Five-Elements Sect won’t stand back.”

“Same goes for the Prison Suppression Sect.”

Except for the voiceless Hanging Monastery’s abbot, the representatives of the four immortal sects pledged their support. The Hanging Monastery’s abbot could only nod vigorously to express that he held the same stance.

He was frustrated. The Mouth-Shut Chan Meditation is truly not easy to cultivate. I had to suppress my urge to speak several times.

Facing the Taciturn Daoist Priest is still better. At least I can just use my fists instead of my mouth.

Chapter 454: The Xia Emperor’s Lifespan

The Xia Emperor was in a good mood now that the matter of Ji Province had gained the support of the Five Great Immortal Sects.

He then raised another matter. “As all of you have probably heard, the Corpse-Driving Sect Leader was supposed to have his body taken over. However, as his soul lamp was placed in the Dao-Seeking Sect, the Great Yu cultivators feared detection by the Dao-Seeking Sect and didn’t fully take over his body, leaving behind his soul.”

“That’s right! That grandson Lu Baqian narrowly avoided death. When I was dealing with the aftermath in Hanshui City, he kept flaunting his Transcendent Tribulation body all day. Utterly reprehensible!”

The Xia Emperor pretended he didn’t hear Qiu Jin’an’s outburst. “In that case, can we draw on this lesson and have other sects place their soul lamps with the Five Great Immortal Sects and the imperial court as a safeguard?

“As Fellow Daoist Yun has mentioned, Great Yu has at least four more Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. If a Fusion cultivator takes over the body of another Fusion cultivator, we could detect the ensuing battle. But it’s too simple for a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator to take over a Fusion cultivator’s body. That could be accomplished without anyone noticing.

“If we implement the soul lamp system, we could deter Great Yu cultivators from complete body takeover like what happened to Sect Leader Lu, preserving at least the victim’s soul.”

“This is feasible.” Yun Zhi nodded, becoming the first to endorse the Xia Emperor’s proposal. She had already conceived a similar solution on the way here and intended to propose it during the meeting, only for the Xia Emperor to be one step faster.

“I also see no issues with it.”

“The Prison Suppression Sect finds it workable.”

The Hanging Monastery’s abbot remained silent, which everyone took as tacit agreement.

Seeing that consensus had been reached, the Xia Emperor continued. “After this meeting, I’ll instruct people to compile a registry of sects to be distributed to you all and inform the sects on the list.”

Great Xia’s sect registration system was based on declaration. As long as one submitted to the authorities basic information like the number of members, size, location, and sect leader, the registration would be deemed successful, requiring neither review nor approval. However, any subsequent changes, such as the appointment of a new sect leader, would still need to be reported to the authorities.

Thanks to this system, Great Xia maintained clear records of the number of sects and their locations, allowing officials to quickly compile the registry requested by the Xia Emperor.

With the discussion of major matters concluded, the five sect leaders exited the hall with smiles and chatter—and the abbot of the Hanging Monastery with only smiles—painting a harmonious picture.

Eunuchs and palace maids stood respectfully outside the hall, ready to see off the five immortal sect leaders.

Cough, cough. The Xia Emperor was just discussing the Taciturn Daoist Priest with Qiu Jin’an when he suddenly burst out coughing. Clamping his mouth, his palm became speckled with blood, and a stark white strand of hair appeared within his dense, black hair, glaringly conspicuous.

“Your Majesty!” The chief eunuch nearly lost his soul from fright, rushing forward in great strides to support the emperor.

“Summon the imperial physicians! Quickly!” The other eunuchs and palace maids scrambled about in obvious panic.

“What’s wrong with you?” Qiu Jin’an frowned, his expression shifting as he grasped the Xia Emperor’s wrist.

“Why are you so weak?!” This shouldn’t be the case though. Even provincial governors enjoy protection from the national fortune, immune to poisons and ailments. As Great Xia’s emperor with supreme command over the national fortune, it’s all the more unthinkable that there’s something wrong with his body.

The Xia Emperor waved his hand with a bitter smile, reluctant to elaborate. The Hanging Monastery’s abbot silently recited “Amitabha” in his heart, though he couldn’t say anything.

Possessing the highest cultivation among them, Yun Zhi saw through the Xia Emperor’s condition at a glance. “His lifespan is exhausted.”

“Lifespan exhausted?” Luo Hongxia was stunned, never imagining the Xia Emperor would face such a crisis and so abruptly.

The Xia Emperor looked up at Yun Zhi with similar astonishment. I’m always shielded by the national fortune, so nobody should be able to detect my condition, yet Yun Zhi had discerned it instantly.

Realizing that he could no longer conceal the matter, he relented. “After all, I’m only at the Divine Transfiguration Stage.”

Among the six present, Yun Zhi’s cultivation was the highest, while the Xia Emperor’s was the lowest.

Whether one could become an emperor bore no direct relation to one’s cultivation level. After all, no matter how high the emperor’s cultivation was, could the emperor suppress the whole world alone?

“That still doesn’t add up. You’re only a thousand years old. Divine Transfiguration cultivators can typically live 1500 to 2000 years old.” The Prison Suppression Sect Leader frowned in bafflement. With Great Xia facing internal turmoil and external threats, the Xia Emperor’s lifespan exhaustion crisis would inevitably trigger unrest, and all manner of demons and monsters would emerge. This doesn’t bode well.

“When I was crown prince, I suffered a life-threatening illness and was on the brink of death. To treat my illness, I consumed numerous rare medicinal ingredients, including two Herb Kings’ roots and leaves. Unfortunately, my body was too frail to absorb the nourishment properly. Though my life was preserved, my lifespan was reduced.”

The other five had heard of this incident, and so did the older eunuchs and palace maids.

“Our sect has several Little Herb Kings, Eternal-Life Cedar, and whatnot to extend one’s lifespan,” Qiu Jin’an offered. We can’t afford to have anything happen to the Xia Emperor now.

The Eternal-Life Cedar, whose spring and autumn each spanned eight thousand years, was a peerless rarity among life-extending medicinal ingredients. The Boundless Longevity Stone grew every year, though imperceptibly, requiring ten millennia to expand visibly. The scrapings from its surface were top-tier supreme treasures that tempted even Fusion cultivators.

The Xia Emperor’s eyes brightened briefly at Qiu Jin’an’s words before dimming again as he shook his head lightly. “It’s no use. After consuming too many natural treasures, the imperial physicians say my body has developed resistance. No Little Herb Kings or other medicinal treasures can help now.” The lifespan problem is fatal. Even the national fortune’s power can’t compensate. Only by becoming an immortal and attaining an endless lifespan can this issue be resolved.

“How much longer do you have?”

“Probably about ten years.” I know my own body best.

Everyone fell silent. Ten years passed in the blink of an eye for cultivators, far too brief. Is the Xia Emperor going to close his eyes forever just as the Grand Era begins unfolding before him?

Since ascending the throne, the Xia Emperor diligently served the nation and people. Under his rule, Great Xia’s power had grown steadily, its national fortune solidifying by the day. He was a rare wise monarch who could rank among the top three in the history of Great Xia.

Does Heaven envy his talents, making him die at this critical juncture and denying him even a glimpse of the true Great Era?

This isn’t fair.

But even if it isn’t fair, what could be done about it?

The Prison Suppression Sect Leader couldn’t help but offer words of comfort. “There’s still plenty of time. I’ll go back and consult the other elders. With how vast the world is, there must be other solutions.” I refuse to believe we can’t extend the Xia Emperor’s lifespan by several decades or even a century.

The five immortal sect leaders departed the imperial capital, soaring through the skies with silent sighs in their hearts, each returning to their respective sects to seek solutions.

“Come to think of it, a crown prince hasn’t been designated, right? That’d be another bloody storm.”

“Great Yu, Great Qian, the Demon Region, and the East Sea. With internal turmoil and external threats, and now with his lifespan drying up...truly turbulent times.”

After everyone left, the Xia Emperor declined to be attended to and proceeded to the imperial palace’s ancestral grounds, hoping his old ancestor might provide a solution.

Chapter 455: Fourth-In-Command of the Everlasting Lineage

At the Dao-Seeking Sect’s Hundred Refinements Peak, Li Haoran was still recalling his past life memories about Mu Baiyi.

As a vice creed leader from the new generation, the youthful and spirited Mu Baiyi was held in high regard by Qin Haoran.

“Mu Baiyi was a pitiful child. He grew up in poverty and became a cultivator, hoping to earn money after joining a sect. Instead, the sect shut down before he could make much.

“Later, he saw that the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s monthly stipend was decent and decided to join them. He mentioned that he originally wanted to join the Everlasting Creed because their followers earned a monthly stipend triple that of a local official’s.”

“Then why didn’t he join them?” Qin Yanyan interjected.

“The Everlasting Creed was too well-hidden—he couldn’t even find their entrance. On the other hand, it was easy to find the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. Just find a random ghost in the wild, and there’d be a one-tenth probability that it belonged to the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. Just like that, he could track down the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

“Of course, that was in the past. Eventually, Qin Haoran realized it was too risky and could easily expose them to the righteous path, so he learned from the Everlasting Creed, making the Nine-Netherworlds Creed equally hard to find now.

“Qin Haoran had a pretty good relationship with Mu Baiyi, who helped him quite a bit in the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. Once, when Qin Haoran heard that banks were profitable, he wanted to start one. But he was worried no one could deposit money, and he would become a laughing stock. Thus, he had Mu Baiyi transform into various people—male, female, old, and young—to make deposits on opening day.

“Basically, he was hiring shills—a common business tactic.” Thanks to Qin Haoran’s memories, Li Haoran was now well-versed in all sorts of shady commercial practices.

“Did the bank succeed?”

“No. Qin Haoran forgot to obtain approval from the authorities when he opened the bank, so the two were arrested for illegal absorption of public deposits. The two explained that no one had actually deposited any money and that it was all staged.”

“Did the authorities release you?”

“No. The authorities said it constituted illegal absorption of public deposits and fraud, warranting combined penalties for both crimes.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Qin Yanyan, “...”

“During their imprisonment, the two studied various laws industriously. In the end, they were released after serving their full terms, returning as experts.” Li Haoran hadn’t fully inherited Qin Haoran’s memories. Otherwise, I’d at least be a legal expert now.

“Fortunately, Qin Haoran had prepared for rainy days and anticipated this disaster. Before entering prison, he had arranged everything and prevented the sect’s financial deficits from being exposed.”

This is a testament to Qin Haoran’s incredible foresight.

Li Haoran wanted to continue recounting the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s glorious days when a cold, graceful figure appeared behind him.

“Big Senior Sister.”

“Greetings, Big Senior Sister.” As a Heavenly Court Creed member, Qin Yanyan had debated whether to address Yun Zhi as “Creed Leader” or “Big Senior Sister.” After a series of internal struggles, she chose to follow the majority.

“Big Senior Sister, I was just confirming with Junior Brother Li. The white paper-hatted man at Hanshui City is indeed the Nine-Netherworlds Creed Leader, Mu Baiyi.”

“Nine-Netherworlds Creed Leader Mu Baiyi? Got it. All of you have done well. Little Junior Brother, come with me.”

~~~

Lu Yang obediently followed Yun Zhi back to Heaven’s Gate Peak.

“Big Senior Sister, did you need me for something?”

“Not you. I need Senior Immortal Fairy.”

“Looking for me?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy sprang up from her bed like a carp leaping from water, cheerfully darting out from the mental space. “Speak! What do you need from me?” It was rare for Yun Zhi to seek her help, and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was rejuvenated, feeling like she was ten years younger.

I’m now only six years old.

“Something is wrong with the Xia Emperor’s lifespan—he only has about ten years left. Little Herb Kings are ineffective on him. Do you have any ideas, Immortal Fairy?”

Lu Yang was flabbergasted. Everyone in the outside world says the Xia Emperor is in his prime, pursuing grand ambitions, with Great Xia’s future looking bright. How could he suddenly only have a few years to live?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy excitedly asked, “When do we start the uprising?” She believed the Dao-Seeking Sect had the resources and the scale to vie for supremacy in the world. When the time is ripe, the masses would rally behind us, and success would be guaranteed!

Isn’t this what Lu Yang mentioned in the strategies he proposed to the Nine-Netherworlds Creed?

With top-tier powerhouses like me and Yun Zhi, can’t we make anyone emperor?

“...Not an uprising. Immortal Fairy, do you have lifespan-extending methods?”

The special trait of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s Dao Fruit is “Everlasting.” Even if she dies, she can be revived so long as someone calls out her honorific title and name. Let alone cultivators—even Little Herb Kings envy such an ability. In Yun Zhi’s view, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was the most likely candidate to resolve the Xia Emperor’s malady.

“Give him an Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit and let that Xia Emperor or whoever become the fourth-in-command of the Everlasting Lineage?” First come, first served. The newcomer naturally has to be ranked last.

The Everlasting Lineage is a force to be reckoned with—the first-in-command is the head of the Five Ancient Immortals, the second-in-command is a Golden Core old ancestor, the third-in-command is a half-immortal, and the fourth-in-command is the current emperor. Lu Yang suddenly felt that his position as second-in-command of the Everlasting Lineage carried significant weight.

Yun Zhi shook her head. “The imperial palace’s ancestral grounds would certainly not agree.” If the Xia Emperor becomes the fourth-in-command of the Everlasting Lineage without rhyme or reason... Yun Zhi could imagine the outrage from the person in the imperial palace’s ancestral grounds and how he would likely challenge the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to a duel.

And this would expose the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s existence.

Yun Zhi needed a solution that could be shown to the world.

“If Little Herb Kings don’t work, then immortal fruits... Mine can preserve corpses and ensure they are everlasting. It can only be used after one dies.

“The Qilin Immortal’s and the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s immortal fruits also don’t have effects that grant eternal life or lifespan extension.

“Wait, does he have sons? See if you can fetch water from the Mother-Child River. It could let him leave behind a descendant.”

“He has nine sons and seven daughters.”

“So fertile? Is he giving birth to piglets?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy muttered. Even drinking the water from the Mother-Child River and Twins River won’t achieve the Xia Emperor’s fertility.

The Qilin Immortal and the Dragon and Phoenix prodigies had tried for years without giving birth to a single little Qilin.

The higher one’s cultivation, the harder it was for them to leave behind an offspring.

“Ah!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy screamed, suddenly remembering a clue. “There’s a natural spiritual peach tree. It is born and nurtured by heaven and earth and not within the scope of natural treasures. Its immortality peaches[1] have lifespan-extending effects! We five have eaten the peaches from that tree. They were very delicious and juicy.”

“Where is this natural spiritual tree?” Yun Zhi had never heard of this, and neither were there records of it in ancient texts.

“No idea. The peach tree had legs. It ran away after we plucked its peaches.”

Yun Zhi nodded. This is a lead, just that it’s elusive. She instructed Lu Yang to keep up with his cultivation practice while she consulted other elders.

After Yun Zhi left, Lu Yang pensively headed to the scripture library.

“What are you going there for?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy asked.

“I vaguely recall seeing a book regarding longevity in the scripture library. It was buried right at the bottom, so few people have probably studied it. Who knows if it might help?”

1. A reference to the immortality peaches kept by Xi Wangmu. ☜

Chapter 456: Longevity Art

The scripture library was where Lu Yang spent most of his time apart from Heaven’s Gate Peak.

While most people’s cultivation techniques were inherited from predecessors, Lu Yang had authored his own. To write his cultivation technique, he had practically lived in the scripture library, reading extensively and internalizing numerous schools of thought, finally creating his groundbreaking cultivation technique—Clear Heart True Nature Mantra.

During his intensive study, he vaguely recalled coming across a book with spells related to longevity. At the time, he had only skimmed it without much thought. After all, he was a Golden Core cultivator in the prime of his youth, so lifespan concerns seemed distant.

“Immortal Fairy, do you know any longevity spells?” As an immortal, surely she’d know some longevity spells or cultivation techniques even if she doesn’t practice them herself, right?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy hummed and contemplated seriously. “No longevity ones, but I know several spells that boost combat power mid-battle by burning one’s lifespan. I used them myself a few times before becoming an immortal.”

Lu Yang could imagine the urgency and desperation back then that warranted the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to activate lifespan-burning spells. Seeing how unconcerned she looked right now, Lu Yang refrained from asking her the details.

“And after you became an immortal?”

“There was no more need then. Think about it. Half-immortals definitely can’t defeat immortals, and an immortal’s opponent can only be immortals. Since an immortal’s lifespan is infinite, when two immortals fight and burn their lifespans, how does that make any difference?”

Lu Yang thought about it. That does make sense. Duels between immortals would probably revolve around their respective Dao Fruits.

“Although burning lifespan was useless, self-detonation was still powerful.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy giggled. The force from an immortal’s self-detonation could wipe out an entire star system or even beyond that.

And my Dao Fruit is perfect for self-detonation.

While the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others would be doomed from one self-detonation, I was different. I could instantly revive after self-detonating and repeat endlessly unless someone stopped me.

Lu Yang eyed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy with an odd expression. It’s my first time hearing of consecutive self-detonations. The Everlasting Dao Fruit is terrifying indeed. With such combat tactics, who wouldn’t be scared?

~~~

Arriving at the scripture library, they found Zhou Lulu on duty.

Zhou Lulu sat with her head bowed over a book, strands of hair cascading down to frame her delicate features. From afar, she resembled an exquisite painting, exuding a graceful serenity.

If the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could learn even a fraction of her demeanor, her standing in Lu Yang’s heart would have risen dramatically.

“Senior Sister Zhou, it’s been a while,” Lu Yang greeted with a smile, recalling how she had offered him much assistance during his early days in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

When I just joined the sect, I was first poisoned by a senior brother’s pill fragrance, then received boiling water baths from Big Senior Sister, and had to lift vats and knead tofu all day for training.

In contrast, Senior Sister Zhou recommended books that could quickly build my fundamentals and books that were essential for travels. She even told me that the weapons in the dining hall are cheaper than in the Great Mission Hall. These make her kindness seem much more precious in comparison.

Zhou Lulu was engrossed in her reading when Lu Yang’s greeting startled her. She instinctively raised the book to shield half her face, her eyes evasive. “Ah, it’s Junior Brother Lu.”

Lu Yang looked at her helplessly, worried about speaking too loudly and frightening her.

Zhou Lulu was Fifth Elder Zhou Xin’s daughter and a Nascent Soul cultivator of absurd strength. During the exchange with the Five-Elements Sect, she had been the main force of the Nascent Soul combatants, giving the Five-Elements Sect’s cultivators a tragic thrashing.

If Senior Sister Zhou and I fight, I’ll get beaten up one-sidedly. It’s just that Senior Sister Zhou is too timid and afraid of talking. From a personality standpoint, victory might not be impossible with the Unbeatable Golden Core.

Lu Yang noticed that Zhou Lulu was currently reading 108 Hammer Techniques. The title doesn’t seem to match Senior Sister Zhou’s image, but it perfectly suits her identity.

“Are you here to study?” Zhou Lulu mustered her courage to ask, checking if she could offer any assistance.

“I’m here to find a book on spells related to lifespan extension,” Lu Yang replied vaguely. The problem with the Xia Emperor’s lifespan would trigger various chain reactions. The fewer the people who know, the better.

“Lifespan-extending spells. Let me think. Is it the Eternal Verdancy Art, which allows one to transform into a tree and plant its roots into the ground to witness the passing ages?

“Or is it the Turtle Longevity Art, which extends one’s lifespan by emulating tortoise behavior?”

“Neither seems like it.” Lu Yang couldn’t match any with his recollection.

“Then I’m afraid I can’t help.” Zhou Lulu shook her head lightly. I haven’t read all the books in the scripture library..

With the scripture library’s extensive collection, only the retired library keeper Elder Tao might have finished reading all of it.

After thanking her, Lu Yang entered the scripture library.

Zhou Lulu kept staring at Lu Yang’s back and only resumed reading after she was sure that Lu Yang had no intention of turning back. Soon, she was immersed in her own literary world.

Many disciples chose to study in the scripture library, researching spells and cultivation techniques and modifying them to make them a better fit. However, some disciples stubbornly pursued ill-suited methods through sheer brute force.

Lu Yang had heard of a senior male disciple obsessed with money. A few years ago, he had borrowed Touching Stone To Gold Art. Every day, he poked stones, meditated to attain comprehension, cultivated his body and mind, learned principles of spells, and consulted people everywhere, never slacking off a single day.

Finally, after a full year, the heavens rewarded his perseverance, and he learned the One-Finger Chan Meditation. With a finger, he could cleave mountains and shatter the ground. Every time he poked one’s body with a finger, it would leave bloody holes. It could be said to be utterly terrifying, worthy of serving as a trump card.

This male disciple couldn’t be blamed. The principles of Touching Stone To Gold Art involved the disassembly and reassembly of internal structures of matter. Its difficulty exceeded what the average person could grasp.

On the other hand, those who couldn’t master it had alternative solutions. A female disciple once achieved the feat of pinching a stone into a diamond by relying entirely on grip strength, becoming the talk of the sect for a while.

Weaving through the other disciples occupied with studying, Lu Yang followed his memory and crouched in a corner of the scripture library.

A layer of dust coated the books, a clear sign that the place hadn’t been cleaned in a long time. Given the vast collection in the scripture library, it was normal for some books to fade into oblivion. For instance, Lu Yang had discovered the forbidden book Dragon-Phoenix Transformation the first time he visited the scripture library.

“I remember it should be here?

“Found it!”

Lu Yang’s eyes lit up as he located a book wedged in the shelves. Its title was simple yet elegant.

Longevity Art.

“I knew I remembered correctly!” Lu Yang was excited. The scripture library is truly a place of treasures. They even have legendary spells like this.

“Such a spell actually exists?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy clicked her tongue in amazement. This is good stuff.

Although I don’t need it, Lu Yang can use it in the future.

Chapter 457: How Many Sect-Leader One-Day Experience Vouchers Can This Immortal’s Contribution Points Redeem?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s approval means that this spell is authentic and a genuine rarity.

After Lu Yang borrowed Longevity Art, he returned to Heaven’s Gate Peak. Arriving at his usual cultivation spot, he pored over every character with intense focus.

“‘Long’: unbroken continuity; ‘-Gevity’: ceaseless growth...”[1] The preface explained the titular concepts while warning that malicious cultivators could invite calamity upon themselves by misusing it.

Lu Yang contemplated. Since I’m upright and aboveboard, I can’t be considered a malicious cultivator. Hence, he began studying without reservations.

Lu Yang took two deep breaths, exhaling impurities as his mind settled into a focused and meditative state, wholly absorbed in learning this new spell. Perhaps it was because Lu Yang was truly talented in spells or the spell was simple to pick up, he quickly grasped its fundamentals.

“It’s this easy to cultivate?” Lu Yang was surprised. Looks like I’m indeed fated with longevity. “But how do I prove that I’ve mastered this thing?” Lu Yang was frustrated. I can’t possibly wait until my theoretical lifespan ends and check whether I’ll die then.

That’s an awfully high price to pay just to prove a point.

“Never mind. Let me test it out first. Maybe I’ll figure something out.” Lu Yang acted on his idea right away. As he activated the Longevity Art, he felt his scalp tingle.

Away from Lu Yang’s eyes, his hair grew at an alarming speed. He instinctively touched his head and gasped. “Why is my hair so long?!”

Why would the Longevity Art affect my hair?

“In Buddhist sects, hair is often called ‘the three thousand strands of worldly troubles.’ Could the creator of this spell be hinting that longevity is lonely and ultimately a worldly trouble? Loneliness will accompany those who live long lives; longevity is a curse. Thus, one should not seek longevity?” Lu Yang was perspicacious and tried to view it from a different perspective to infer the spell creator’s intentions, obtaining a sudden epiphany.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy couldn’t help but advise him. “Why don’t you check the back of the last page?”

“What do you mean? There’s writing on the back?”

Following the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s suggestion, Lu Yang flipped to the back of the last page.

This spell promotes long hair growth and specializes in treating baldness and hair loss. Do not use it on those from Buddhist sects, for it may easily cause trouble.

Lu Yang, “...”

If you meant ‘long hair growth,’ write it as that! Why did you write it as ‘longevity (long growth)?!’ [2]

Who even abbreviates it like that?!

Who the hell wrote this spell?!

Lu Yang snapped the book shut furiously and saw the author’s name on the cover: Tang Shengyi.

Tang Shengyi was the shifu of the Dao-Seeking Nine, Lu Yang’s grand-shifu, and had already retired.

Lu Yang calmed down, half of his anger dissipating. “Grand-Shifu, who names things like this... Wait, Immortal Fairy, you knew about this spell?”

“Of course. When you were reading in the scripture library, I was too, though with my immortal consciousness. I’ve read this book.”

“Then why did you say this spell is suited for me and that I could use it in the future?”

“Doesn’t the Longevity Art pair well with your Arhat Fist?”

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, your brain only works at times like this, huh?

Well, Xia Emperor, you’re on your own. I’ve tried my best.

Just as Lu Yang was about to argue further, he saw Yun Zhi returning to Heaven’s Gate Peak after the meeting with the elders.

Yun Zhi glanced at Lu Yang, slightly puzzled. Lu Yang’s hair wasn’t this long when I left?

Upon noticing the Longevity Art manual in his hand, she understood what had happened.

“Big Senior Sister, did you find a way to extend the Xia Emperor’s lifespan?”

She shook her head. “Only the Immortal Fairy’s clue about the spiritual tree sounds feasible. The elders’ solutions were somewhat...”

Although Yun Zhi didn’t elaborate, based on Lu Yang’s impression of the elders, he could roughly guess the elders’ ideas. They might even have proposed something like “refine the Xia Emperor into a walking corpse and pretend he’s still alive.”

“Lass Yun, you remember that I’ve just captured three Transcendent Tribulation souls, don't you?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy drifted out of Lu Yang’s body.

“Naturally. The souls you caught are extremely useful, Senior Fairy.”

“Then shouldn’t I get contribution points in exchange?”

“You should.”

“Then how many Sect Leader One-Day Experience vouchers can I redeem?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy made no effort to hide her intentions.

Lu Yang stared at her in horror. Is it too late to change my golden finger cheat now?

Yun Zhi did a brief calculation. “Roughly two months’ worth.”

“That much?!” The Everlasting Fairy grinned from ear to ear. Last time, I was only the sect leader for three days—hardly satisfying. This time, I get two whole months. Now, that’s satisfying!

“In that case, I want to be the sect leader for two months!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy announced, afraid Yun Zhi would renege.

Lu Yang hastily intervened. “Big Senior Sister, that can’t do! The Immortal Fairy uses my body in public. Last time, when I was acting sect leader for three days, we could use the excuse of saying I found our shifu who’d been missing for ten years—a meritorious deed. But what about this time? We can’t possibly say that I found our shifu who’d been missing for ten years for the twentieth time, right?

Yun Zhi replied breezily, “No matter. We’ll just say that Shifu was impressed by your successful performance as acting sect leader the last time and wishes to groom you further, thus letting you become acting sect leader for two more months.”

As sect leader, the Taciturn Daoist Priest could appoint anyone as acting sect leader.

And as his disciple, Yun Zhi could make him say whatever she wanted him to say.

“Any more questions? If not, it’s settled then! I’ll be the sect leader!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy beamed like she was celebrating the New Year.

“Coincidentally, in two months, the sect will hold a grand celebration to commemorate its 120,000th anniversary. Senior Fairy, you can use these two months to prepare and showcase to the world the grandeur of an ancient immortal.” The corners of Yun Zhi’s mouth curved into a faint smile that vanished quickly.

“Sect celebration?” Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy exchanged bewildered looks.

After a quick explanation from Yun Zhi, the two learned that while the Dao-Seeking Sect was said to have 120,000 years of history, it was technically two months shy.

The Dao-Seeking Sect’s founding date was the sixth day of the eleventh month—the day their founding ancestor, the Innate Daoist Priest, got lost.

The sect celebration would be a lively event with major factions visiting.

The moment the Everlasting Immortal Fairy heard that she had to organize the sect celebration, her expression showed clear signs of regret. “I feel that such matters are best left to members of the Dao-Seeking Sect. I’ll abstain.”

Yun Zhi was slightly surprised as she looked at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “Senior Fairy, you are our sect’s guest elder. How are you not a member of the sect? If you are not our sect’s guest elder, you can’t get contribution points.”

“Hmm...” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pouted, trapped between a rock and a hard place.

“Senior Fairy, or do you find the matters of the sect celebration too overwhelming and too much of a hassle, so you’re planning to bow out?”

“How can that be?! Isn’t it just organizing a celebration? I’ll become the acting sect leader for these two months!” A heroic valor burst forth from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, her eyes blazing with fighting spirit.

“I’ll have to trouble you then, Senior.”

“No trouble at all!”

1. The term “longevity” in Chinese is made up of the characters for “long” and “life.” ☜

2. The term is made up of four characters and means something along the lines of hair growth. However, if you combine the first character and second character, it becomes the term for “longevity.” ☜

Chapter 458: The Everlasting Immortal Fairy Inspects the Dao-Seeking Sect

Mortals cherished every birthday, but cultivators were different. Their lifespans spanned centuries or even millennia, and some frequently entered seclusion. Celebrating their birthday every year would be unbearably annoying.

Among cultivators, the custom was to hold a small celebration every decade and a big one every century.

The Dao-Seeking Sect’s 120,000th anniversary was an occasion worthy of grand celebration. Few factions in the Central Continent had existed longer than the Dao-Seeking Sect. Among the Five Great Immortal Sects, the Dao-Seeking Sect was the oldest.

When the time came, major factions would attend the celebration to offer their congratulations. Not much needed to be said for the imperial court, four other Great Immortal Sects, and S-class sects, but it was uncertain whether first-class sects could attend. It could be said that receiving an invitation to the Dao-Seeking Sect’s celebration was a mark of prestige.

One could imagine the magnificent scene in the Dao-Seeking Sect in two months.

Though the mere thought of what would happen in two months made Lu Yang’s scalp prickle. I’m only at the Golden Core Stage. Why do I have to be responsible for such matters? Isn’t it too soon?

“What do you mean you’re responsible? I am the acting sect leader!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy corrected him.

Just like how a new official assuming office would set three fires to assert their authority, she set her first fire on Lu Yang.

“Come, hand over your body.”

An order from the sect leader is absolute. With no choice, Lu Yang obediently relinquished control of his body.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy occupied Lu Yang’s body and stretched lazily, her face wreathed in smiles. “Hehe, having a body and not having a body are really poles apart.”

She turned her gaze to Yun Zhi, setting her second fire. “And you, Lass Yun, announce my appointment as acting sect leader to the entire Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“Understood.” Yun Zhi’s attitude toward the acting sect leader was much better than to the actual sect leader; she followed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s instructions without hesitation.

~~~

As a result of Yun Zhi’s dissemination, news of Lu Yang’s reappointment as acting sect leader spread like wildfire across the sect.

“What? Lu Yang’s the acting sect leader again?! What did he do this time?”

“Did the sect leader appoint him?”

“Hasn’t Big Senior Sister been the acting sect leader all this while? Why the change?”

When a conspiracy theorist caught wind of the news, they fell silent for a long time before mysteriously telling the others, “According to my analysis, this change in acting sect leader likely involves a power struggle among the higher-ups!”

The others were floored. They were no fools and understood the underlying implication. “You’re saying the sect leader thinks Big Senior Sister has held power for too long and wants to replace her with Lu Yang, sparking a fierce power struggle between the two?”

“No. I’m saying that Big Senior Sister wants a break and asked the sect leader to return, but he refused and designated Lu Yang to take over.”

“...”

“That seems to make sense.”

~~~

Strolling through the sect with Lu Yang’s body, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s radiant smile made Lu Yang appear years younger.

“Greetings, Sect Leader.”

“Greetings, Sect Leader.”

Lu Yang’s senior brothers and sisters—or rather, in this moment, his disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect—greeted him with respectful bows.

“All good, all good.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded, lifting her hand to indicate there was no need for such enthusiasm. I’ve only been in office for an hour. I still have two months ahead.

She meandered toward the arena frequently used by disciples. On the stage, two Divine Transfiguration cultivators clashed intensely. It was a dazzling display of assorted spells and techniques, with one wielding crackling lightning and the other bending space.

The disciples around him eyed Lu Yang warily, fearing that Lu Yang would pull another “Law Follows Words” stunt and randomly challenge beyond his level.

Lu Yang also eyed himself warily.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stood beside the arena stage with hands clasped behind her back, watching the duel quietly with no intention of getting onto the stage.

Now that Lu Yang has formed the Unbeatable Golden Core with my assistance, there’s no longer a need to get onto stage and battle beyond his level to cultivate his Unbeatable Momentum.

What’s the point of battling on stage? They’ll just pretend they still don’t know I’m the acting sect leader and thrash me mercilessly.

This is the warning from the Unbeatable Golden Core—extremely useful.

Heeding the Unbeatable Golden Core’s advice, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suppressed the itch in her heart and silently stayed put below the stage.

“The fight was so-so,” she commented insipidly without a fluctuation in her voice, exuding the aloofness of an expert.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had no real purpose for descending the mountain except for flaunting her new status.

Next, she ambled to One More Time Barbeque Shop on the commercial street, where the Everlasting Immortal and the Everlasting Creed’s higher-ups happened to be gathered.

Now, all members of the Everlasting Lineage and the Everlasting Creed’s higher-ups were present—an impressive and formidable lineup.

The Everlasting Creed’s higher-ups were ecstatic. Following Lu Yang really does pay off! Just days ago, he was still a junior disciple. And now, he’s already the acting sect leader!

Chefs Liu and Gao wore odd expressions, recalling a distant memory. The last time Lu Yang was the acting sect leader, he had sabotaged and tricked us into becoming barbeque chefs here.

In a flash, four months have already passed.

“Business is not bad, right?”

“Thanks to the first-in-command, business has been thriving.” While others couldn’t sense the difference with Lu Yang, how could the Everlasting Immortal—third-in-command of the Everlasting Lineage and the bearer of the Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit—not recognize that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was currently controlling Lu Yang’s body?

“Work hard. This barbeque shop is our Everlasting Lineage’s front and pride. Don’t tarnish its reputation!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy exhorted.

“Yes!” Having obtained their leader’s approval, everyone swelled with morale.

“Mmm, good attitude. The Nine-Netherworlds Creed is expanding the market and opening shops everywhere. Lass Yun has followed my instructions to seek out the Xia Emperor, and he has promised to support our franchise.”

Naturally, the outgoing acting sect leader would brief her successor on the contents of the meeting.

“There’s such a good thing?!” The Everlasting Creed’s higher-ups were moved. They had assumed that the role of acting sect leader was only in name. They didn’t expect her to hold real power—able to command the Big Senior Sister of the sect with just a word, and even make the Xia Emperor personally step in to help.

With the support of the imperial court, One More Time Barbeque Shop will definitely spring up across the continent and flourish, becoming the leader of the barbeque market.

“Which of you can paint? You can capture this sect leader’s historic inspection and display it at the entrance.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy heard that the emperor’s calligraphy was especially valuable among the common folk; any shop that could display the emperor’s inscription would have booming business.

As an almighty immortal and the acting sect leader, surely the combination of my two identities surpasses the emperor’s?

“Let me.” The Everlasting Immortal volunteered himself to be at the first-in-command’s beck and call. This is a fortuitous opportunity bestowed by the Immortal Fairy. As the third-in-command, I know best how powerful the Big Boss is.

Soon, the Everlasting Immortal completed the painting.

It depicted Lu Yang standing in the center, surrounded by the Everlasting Immortal and the Everlasting Creed’s higher-ups, all posed in reverence as they looked to him.

This painting was naturally displayed at the entrance, drawing every passer-by’s gaze.

Lu Yang rubbed his chin. I can’t help but feel like this painting looks strange, yet I can’t put a finger on it.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy still wanted to tour around and visit every elder’s peak from First Elder to Eighth Elder to spread her name far and wide within the Dao-Seeking Sect. But just as her plan had gotten underway, Yun Zhi suddenly appeared beside her.

“Sect Leader, it’s time for you to handle official sect affairs.”

Chapter 459: The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s Golden Finger Cheat Makes Her Life Smooth-Sailing

When the Everlasting Immortal Fairy heard Yun Zhi’s reminder, her expression turned vivid, looking like an overworked official who had slogged away for a grueling year and just stepped out of their doorstep for a vacation, only to be summoned back by their superior to attend to official duties.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy suddenly remembered that she had been revived with the aid of a golden finger cheat, and it was precisely its existence that made life since her resurrection smooth-sailing.

“Lu Yang, help me handle this.” The third fire was set on Lu Yang’s head as Lu Yang was forced to regain control of his body.

Lu Yang, “...”

Just you wait, one day I’ll capture three Transcendent Tribulation souls and become acting sect leader myself, then make you do my work!

Yun Zhi hauled Lu Yang back to Heaven’s Gate Peak.

“All of these.” Yun Zhi dumped a stack of documents before him, some accumulated while she was processing their shifu’s prison release procedures, and others piled up while she was away at the meeting in the imperial palace.

Bit by bit, it added up to this much.

“The top priority is assigning personnel to Ji Province,” Yun Zhi reminded Lu Yang to sort the matters according to their urgency.

Wu Youdao had revealed Ji Province as the next target. The imperial court and the Five Great Immortal Sects had to comb through Ji Province meticulously to search for traces of Great Yu cultivators.

“As for the nine elders...”

Lu Yang was conflicted. With over three hundred cities in Ji Province, sending too few people there to help wouldn’t work. But what is an appropriate number?

It’s inconvenient for Sixth Elder to travel out, while Eighth Elder may easily be arrested if he steps out of the sect—neither can be dispatched.

Just as Lu Yang deliberated, Yun Zhi advised, “While the Dao-Seeking Sect indeed has nine elders, it doesn’t mean there are only nine Fusion cultivators. The vice hall leader of the Great Mission Hall, overseer of the Hundred Refinement Peak’s dining hall, the manager of the commercial street, the proprietor of Hundred Fragrance Restaurant... They are all Fusion cultivators from the same generation as the elders.” She listed a bunch of people Lu Yang had never met before.

“There are many people from the elders’ generation. It’s just that they are either on external missions, in semi-retirement mode within the sect, or guarding secret domains. Although they can’t compare to the elders in cultivation, they are still much stronger than Fusion cultivators in the outer world.”

Lu Yang had previously found it odd. With so many disciples in his generation, the elders’ generation couldn’t possibly comprise only nine people. Where had the rest gone?

Only now did he understand. The eight elders and Shifu are actually the diligent ones. The rest are hidden in places I can’t see.

For instance, the dining hall produces powerful weapons, and I’ve bought weapons there several times, but I never heard that it had an overseer. And Hundred Fragrance is another example. I’ve been there a few times, yet I’ve never seen its proprietor.

“What about Elder Tao from the scripture library?” Lu Yang recalled the amiable old man he had encountered in the scripture library while he was writing his cultivation technique.

“Elder Tao is from the same generation as Grand-Shifu. He has already retired and doesn’t involve himself in external affairs.”

“Alright then. I’ll dispatch Second, Third, and Fourth Elder, as well as the vice hall leader of the Great Mission Hall, overseer of the Hundred Refinements Peak’s dining hall, the manager of the commercial street, and the proprietor of Hundred Fragrance Restaurant—altogether seven people to Ji Province.”

First Elder kept watch over the Great Mission Hall, while Fifth Elder and Seventh Elder were the sect’s financial pillars, so none of them could leave.

“There are two vice hall leaders.”

“Both shall go. That makes eight.” Lu Yang waved imperiously, deploying these outstanding Fusion cultivators to support Ji Province.

“I’ll notify them now.” Yun Zhi nodded and took the initiative.

After she left, Lu Yang jolted back to his senses. There must be more peers of the same generation as the elders. Could Big Senior Sister have wanted to dispatch these people, which was why she told me about them?

“It can’t be, it can’t be.” Lu Yang shook his head, feeling that he was overthinking it.

Lu Yang picked up the top document and opened it to see that it was an invitation to Yun Province Grand Ceremony. It stated that it hoped the Dao-Seeking Sect could send its young disciples to participate in the grand ceremony. After the standard pleasantries, a special note was appended for emphasis. If possible, please refrain from sending disciples Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

Lu Yang, “...”

What’s wrong with me and Meng Jingzhou? We shone so brightly during the Qing Province Grand Ceremony that the whole world knows about the event!

Among all provincial grand ceremonies, the Qing Province Grand Ceremony is the most renowned—a testament to our painstaking efforts.

Lu Yang penned his official decision. Let Wei Nanfei and Jin Qinqin attend.

These two were his batchmates. In their childhood, one was rescued by Dai Bufan, while the other accidentally consumed a Qingmu Immortal Fruit. Both viewed Lu Yang as their role models. Their cultivation speed was inferior to Lu Yang and the other four, but their foundations were solid, making footprints with every step. By the time they reached Lu Yang’s cultivation realm, they might rival Li Haoran and become the Dao-Seeking Sect’s future backbone.

Attending such large-scale events would be of tremendous aid to them in the future. For instance, if a few Great Yu cultivators pop up during the grand ceremony, the two could broaden their horizons.

The next document was an official missive from the Golden Buddhist Kingdom. It said that Lu Yang’s Second Senior Brother, whom he had never met, had mastered the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body. He relocated the temple’s Buddha statue all day and activated his Sixteen-Foot Golden Body before sitting on it. His Sixteen-Foot Golden Body was cultivated so well that it appeared more sacred than the actual Buddha statues, fooling even monks.

Only after a week did the old abbot realize they had been providing offerings not to a Buddha statue but Lu Yang’s Second Senior Brother. Throughout this week, his Second Senior Brother had maintained his Sixteen-Foot Golden Body state.

Judging by the tone of the official missive, it wasn’t the first time Second Senior Brother had done something like this. Those people from the Buddhist Kingdom wished that the Dao-Seeking Sect could quickly take him back.

“As expected of Second Senior Brother. He sure is Shifu’s legacy successor,” Lu Yang remarked sincerely.

Next was an invitation from Sword Tower, accompanied by a letter. It mentioned that the elders of Sword Tower had unanimously recognized the Taciturn Daoist Priest as the “foremost figure in Sword Dao” of the current era. They hoped that the Taciturn Daoist Priest could head to the Sword Tower to receive the plaque “Foremost Figure in Sword Dao.” Many experts from the Sword Dao community would attend and respectfully welcome the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s arrival.

Based in Shu Province, the Sword Tower stood preeminent even among first-class sects, representing the orthodox Sword Dao. The Sword Tower was once an S-class sect, though it was downgraded to a first-class sect after its Sword Dao Supreme Lord passed away.

Although the Sword Dao Supreme Lord had passed, his legacy and foundation remained. The Sword Tower had a dozen Fusion cultivators skilled in Sword Dao. It could be said that the Sword Tower’s power was stronger than half-baked S-class sects like the Corpse-Driving Sect. The Sword Tower represented the orthodox Sword Dao, while the Taciturn Daoist Priest represented the pinnacle of Sword Dao.

When the Taciturn Daoist Priest once challenged the Sword Tower to a duel, he defeated a dozen cultivators in succession before besting the tower leader of Sword Tower.

However, the Sword Tower had always looked down on the Taciturn Daoist Priest. Is giving him a plaque a sign of concession?

Yun Zhi had finished her task of informing the entire sect. Upon returning, she saw Lu Yang staring at Sword Tower’s invitation in deep thought.

“You want Shifu to go to Sword Tower to collect the plaque?”

“Yes. Wouldn’t this alleviate the relationship between Shifu and Sword Tower?”

“Give up. Shifu won’t go.”

“Why not?” Lu Yang was baffled. “Doesn’t Shifu want to reconcile his relationship with the Sword Tower?”

“Sword Tower acknowledged Shifu long ago, admitting his status in Sword Dao. This isn’t the first time they’re offering Shifu a plaque, but Shifu has never gone there to claim it.”

“Shifu is indifferent to fame and worldly rewards?” Lu Yang mused.

“Because every attendee has grudges with Shifu. Going there would be akin to walking into a trap,” Yun Zhi replied.

“...Shifu’s enemies truly appear where we least expect them to. By the way, can we assign Shifu to Ji Province?”

After some consideration, Yun Zhi stated seriously, “You are the acting sect leader, while Shifu is the sect leader. You can’t order Shifu.”

“So it won’t work?”

“So I can write a letter and suggest that Shifu go to Ji Province.”

Chapter 460: Working in Shifts

Lu Yang politely declined the Sword Tower’s invitation to the Hongmen Feast—an obvious death trap. As promised, Yun Zhi penned a letter at the side desk, suggesting that the Taciturn Daoist Priest visit Ji Province.

“Big Senior Sister, you can locate Shifu?” Lu Yang suddenly recalled their shifu had enemies everywhere and operated like a sly hare with three burrows, making his whereabouts elusive.

“I can.” While she spoke, she finished the letter to the Taciturn Daoist Priest and gracefully folded it into a paper crane. Lifting it, she blew gently. The paper crane’s eyes gleamed with life as its wings fluttered, flying out of the cave abode.

“This is...” Lu Yang had never seen such a spell before.

“A minor spell I created to pass the time. I call it Folding Paper (Origami) Art,” Yun Zhi replied offhandedly.

Lu Yang inhaled sharply. Creating spells to pass the time? How does one achieve that?

Is the gap between people this vast? Why is my way of passing the time listening to ancient scandals and dark history from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy?

Although Lu Yang had feared that listening to such ancient secrets in the past would result in ancient immortals joining hands to eliminate him, he feared nothing now.

There’s no need to be scared. If these matters get leaked, I’ll definitely get eliminated. Since death awaits either way, why fear listening to a few more stories?

“It’s just creating spells; child’s play.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was dismayed by Lu Yang’s lack of knowledge and experience. What’s difficult about creating spells? “I could already create spells at the Golden Core Stage. That was when I created the Play-Dead Technique. Study well under me and you’ll be able to create spells too!”

Faced with the lofty promises painted by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Lu Yang kept a respectful distance, utterly unmoved.

What use is the Play-Dead Technique? What about the Water-Repelling Mantra?

Lu Yang continued reviewing the documents.

The elders bewailed their poverty, requesting more spirit stones. First Elder needed spirit stones as rewards for the missions in the Great Mission Hall, Second Elder didn’t have enough spirit stones to sustain the arrays in the herb garden, Third Elder lamented having less wealth than his disciple Meng Jingzhou...
