All the reasons seemed valid, making Lu Yang uncertain whether he should refuse or allocate funds.

“Leave this to me.” Yun Zhi took the documents from the elders. It’s still too early for Lu Yang to deal with such matters.

Lu Yang inwardly noted, It seems like navigating the dynamics among the elders requires a certain finesse. I'm still too young and haven’t yet figured out their relationships or how they interact. I’ll need to learn more from Big Senior Sister.

Then Lu Yang watched Yun Zhi write two words at the end of each document: Request Denied.

Yun Zhi was worried that Lu Yang’s skin was too thin to turn them down directly.

Loop by loop by loop, Lu Yang finally processed every document.[1]

“Whew—finally, it’s all done.”

As he went through the paperwork, he felt none of the exhilaration of wielding authority—instead, he found that an immortal’s trials were truly grueling.

At least I’ve passed this daunting trial safely.

“My turn, my turn!” Seeing the work was completed, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy took over Lu Yang’s body, eager to strut around and flaunt.

“Perfect timing. With the documents settled, it’s time to sort out the sect celebration’s guest invitation list,” Yun Zhi stated flatly, her gaze drilling into the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy, “...”

“I’ve worked so long without rest!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pouted, though doing it with Lu Yang’s face was a peculiar sight.

Yun Zhi was unmoved, seeing through her ploy at a glance. “It was Lu Yang who handled the documents just now. It’s your turn now.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy flashed a saccharine smile, trying to get into Lu Yang’s good books. “Lu Yang, why don’t I return your body to you?”

Lu Yang remained impassive, seeing through her fake smile at a glance.

Left with no choice, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could only hang her head dispiritedly and begin filtering the guest list.

“These are all the S-class and first-class sects registered with the imperial court.” Yun Zhi had prepared the compiled registry beforehand.

The imperial court and four Great Immortal Sects would certainly be invited.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy counted the sects on the list. “Eight S-class sects, 116 first-class sects.” This implied that eight more sects apart from the Five Great Immortal Sects had Transcendent Tribulation experts.

“Wait, it’s nine now. The Corpse-Driving Sect is also considered an S-class sect.” The Corpse-Driving Sect Leader barely scraped through and carried the sect into the S-class sect category.

The number of S-class sects rarely changed for centuries. The list provided by Yun Zhi was based on the previous month’s calculations, so it should technically be the newest version. However, the Corpse-Driving Sect Leader happened to break through right afterward.

Lu Yang tallied the currently known Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. At least five from the Five Great Immortal Sects and eight from the S-class sects.

The imperial court undoubtedly has more. There are four garrison generals at the borders, one of whom I have met after the Hanshui City incident, and another who was deployed by the imperial court during the annihilation of the Everlasting Creed. Since the Luoshui Guard specializes in handling archaic cultivators, they surely consist of Transcendent Tribulation cultivators.

And these are only those on the surface. There has to be more in the dark. Most Transcendent Tribulation cultivators—excluding the Corpse-Driving Sect Leader—are highly senior and rarely intervene.

“All nine S-class sects must be invited. These 116 first-class sects require screening...” Yun Zhi patiently taught the Everlasting Immortal Fairy how to carry out the selection.

Due to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s peak intelligence, she quickly figured out a screening method. “Should we exclude all those who bear grudges against the Taciturn Daoist Priest?” This is a good idea. If we invite a bunch of the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s enemies, it’d be hard for the celebration to go on.

“Then there will be no sects we can invite.”

“Fine then.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s plan had failed before it even began.

With Yun Zhi’s step-by-step guidance, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy soon produced a guest invitation list according to Yun Zhi’s wishes.

“Ask Big Senior Sister how to handle Second Senior Brother’s matter.” Lu Yang recalled he had received a complaint from the Golden Buddhist Kingdom during Yun Zhi’s absence.

In a flustered manner, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy retrieved the document buried at the bottom.

Yun Zhi opened it and scanned it. “Ah, it’s about Second Junior Brother again.”

“What should we do?”

“No matter. This isn’t Second Junior Brother’s first time doing something like this. The Buddhist Kingdom has complained before. You don’t have to care.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy uttered an “oh” and scribbled in reply: You don’t have to care about him.

Regaining control of his body, Lu Yang read the description of the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body in all its grandeur and grew envious. “By the way, Big Senior Sister, can I learn the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body?”

Imagine roaring in battle as the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body rises, as imposing as a deity and as dignified as Buddha, sweeping through armies.

Just the thought of it is so cool!

“You can give it a try.”

1. It was really hard to translate this tongue twister. The meaning is like “Lu Yang continuously continuously continuously...” and the character “Lu” is repeated. The original Chinese sounds like this: Lu Yang luluxuxu luluxuxu luluxuxu ☜

Chapter 461: Learning the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body

The Sixteen-Foot Golden Body was one of the Buddhist sects’ supreme arts. Once mastered, the practitioner would be enveloped in a golden body, resisting attacks while delivering attacks, flawless in both offense and defense. Those who attained the highest level of the golden body could shed their mortal flesh and bone and become a Buddha on the spot.

Legends spoke of an enlightened senior monk in the Buddhist Kingdom who comprehended the Dao under a Bodhi Tree and achieved major success with the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body. No attack in the world could break his golden body, and he could be said to be unbeatable in the world.

Though picking up a supreme art was arduous, Yun Zhi deemed it less challenging than Cosmos in Palm, so she believed Lu Yang could learn it.

Lu Yang had a senior brother at the Apex Golden Core Stage who had also mastered the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body.

“Who said the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body is a Buddhist spell? It already existed in the ancient era!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy declared. I am most qualified to speak in this aspect.

“It already existed in the ancient era?” Neither Lu Yang nor Yun Zhi had known this.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy snorted. “Of course! Though everyone in ancient times called their golden bodies ‘Sixteen-Foot Golden Body,’ the sizes varied wildly. It wasn’t until the five of us became immortals that the proportions of the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body were fixed.”

Lu Yang was baffled. “What does all of you becoming immortals have to do with the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body?”

“Naturally, it’s because we standardized the measurement system! Back then, every race and tribe had its own measuring standard. After we became immortals, we dictated a fixed length for a zhang.”

Lu Yang was stunned. I can believe it if it were the other four immortals, but you, Immortal Fairy, had a hand in standardizing measurements?

“It was the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s idea. One day, he solemnly informed us that some people claimed he was eight zhang (25 meters) tall, while others said he was only one chi (33 centimeters). He suspected the discrepancies stemmed from differing measurement standards of various tribes. After we standardized the measurement system, the problem was gone.”

“Standardizing measurements worked that well?”

“Mmm, I was busy enforcing the new standardized measurements across the various tribes then, so I didn’t have time to inform the world about the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s actual height.”

“So you were the one spreading rumors!”

“You can’t call that spreading rumors. At the start, a follower asked me how tall the Heaven Mandate Immortal was, but I was half-asleep then and blurted out ‘eight zhang.’ Before I could do anything, it spread like wildfire. Realizing the severity of the situation, I hastily told the follower that the Heaven Mandate Immortal was one chi tall.

“Think about it. If one rumor says eight zhang and another says one chi, wouldn’t the average be his actual height?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s logic was so impeccable that Lu Yang couldn’t immediately refute it.

She continued, “Besides, I can execute a golden body too. It’s just that I know too many things to bother with the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body. Techniques like Heaven-Earth Manifestation or Size At Will serve similar purposes—battling with a huge form.”

Yun Zhi nodded in agreement. As they say, the Great Dao returns to simplicity, and different routes lead to the same destination. Many spells and techniques bear similarities; mastering one is sufficient. There’s no need to excel in everything.

“Come with me.” Yun Zhi led Lu Yang to the same clearing in the back mountain, where she had taught him Shrinking Earth To Inches.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy darted out from Lu Yang’s body, eager to instruct him as well.

Lu Yang’s confidence soared, and he brimmed with fighting spirit. With Big Senior Sister—a powerhouse of the current era—and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy—a powerhouse of the ancient era—guiding me, there’ll definitely be no problem!

“To cultivate the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body, one must first maintain a tranquil mental state.”

“To cultivate the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body, one must first mobilize their qi and blood.”

Yun Zhi and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy spoke simultaneously, leaving Lu Yang dumbfounded.

Who should I listen to?

Yun Zhi looked at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy coolly. “A tranquil mental state allows one to unlock their full potential. Why do you want to mobilize the qi and blood?”

Unfazed by Yun Zhi, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy stared at Lu Yang, not planning to back down. “Qi and blood connect the meridians, and the meridians carry spirit energy. Since the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body is a fusion of qi and blood and spirit energy, one should naturally mobilize their qi and blood first.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, shouldn’t you be locking eyes with Big Senior Sister? Why are you looking at me?

Also, should I say something to express my stance in a situation like this?

But I don’t dare to offend either.

Caught between these titans of the past and present, Lu Yang had no choice but to tuck his tail between his legs and keep his head down.

“I am the acting sect leader. Listen to me!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy played her trump card, forcing Yun Zhi to relent.

“...Fine.”

Thus concluded the battle between these titans of the past and present—a silent duel that had gone unnoticed by the world.

“I’ll teach you. Close your eyes. Feel the qi and blood inside you and try to mobilize them.”

Lu Yang shut his eyes and turned his senses inward. The roar of torrential rivers and lakes filled his ears. It was the sound of his qi and blood. They surpassed that of Golden Core cultivators, outclassing even some Nascent Soul cultivators.

“Harness that power. Synchronize its pulse with your meridians. The stronger the resonance, the stronger the power of your qi, blood, and spirit energy!”

Thump, thump, thump. The surroundings were completely silent, save for the sound of Lu Yang’s pounding heart.

“Expand your qi, blood, and spirit outward. Visualize them as solid matter bursting forth from within and taking form outside your body, ideally in the same form as you!”

Yun Zhi gave a slight nod by the side. The Immortal Fairy’s approach is roughly similar to mine. Be it a calm mental state or qi and blood, they ultimately lead to the cultivation of the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body.

Now, the rest will be up to Lu Yang.

Unaware of Yun Zhi’s expectations for him, Lu Yang’s eyes remained shut. His qi and blood surged through him, but his mental state was serene. A wisp of sensation flickered at the edge of his awareness—elusive yet tangible, surreal yet real.

He seized it and pulled with all his might!

Qi and blood churned, spirit energy erupted, and the two forces intertwined, spiraling through his body at high speeds before gushing outward. The moment they left his body, the formless energy turned into a golden brilliance, as if forged from gold itself.

Boom! The Sixteen-Foot Golden Body materialized.

Ten meters away from Lu Yang!

A question mark popped out of Lu Yang’s head.

Shouldn’t the golden body be enveloping me? Why did you run so far away?

“Never mind. It may be a bit far and lacks defensive utility, but at least it can attack.”

The Sixteen-Foot Golden Body was extraordinarily sturdy. A single swing of the arm could overwhelm any Golden Core cultivator. Lu Yang attempted to control the golden body, only to find it utterly responsive like a statue.

Lu Yang, “...”

Why do other people’s golden bodies come with offensive and defensive features, while mine comes with neither?

“Why don’t you try going into your golden body?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suggested. It was her first time encountering something like this. Other people cast the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body around themselves and stay inside it. Perhaps it works the same in Lu Yang’s case.

Nearby, Yun Zhi wore an equally perplexed expression. I see nothing wrong with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s method. But why did it produce such a result?

With no other options, Lu Yang complied and jogged to the golden body’s feet. As expected of a golden body I’ve cast. Its exterior is incredibly sturdy. Even I can’t find an entry point.

“Try from beneath its feet?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suggested again.

Lu Yang could only crouch and lift the golden body’s foot to enter the golden body.

Within the golden body, Lu Yang’s excitement bubbled. This is my golden body! Let the world witness its might!

He willed it to move.

It did not move!

He willed it to move again.

It still did not move!

As sturdy as a golden mountain!

“...The hell did I cultivate—a golden body or a freaking tortoise shell?!”

Chapter 462: The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s Storytelling

“You don’t say; this golden body’s defense is pretty impressive.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was ever adept at spotting strengths. “If you were to attack your own golden body, nothing except for Village in Palm could damage it. Everything else would at most scratch the surface.”

“That tough?” Lu Yang blinked. He had assumed sword techniques could breach the golden body’s defenses, never expecting the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to hold it in such high regard.

“Well, of course, this immortal taught you after all!”

“It wouldn’t hurt to keep it as a defensive move.” Lu Yang nodded. After a full day of learning the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body, I have at least made some gains.

Now, with Village in Palm for offense and the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body for defense, who could possibly defeat me?

~~~

At a teahouse.

The Daoist priest’s storyteller gavel struck the table with a sharp clack, and a tale began to unfold. The man was shabbily dressed, and his horsetail whisk rested on the table, though his eyes gleamed with spirit, making his overall appearance oddly mismatched.

“Within the Dao-Seeking Sect is a prodigy by the name of Lu Yang. This young man’s talent is truly extraordinary. Upon entering the sect for the first time, he displayed heaven-defying talent—an extremely rare Single Spirit Root!

“And what does a Single Spirit Root signify, you ask? Everyone here is probably aware that before the Great Era’s arrival, such a spirit root appeared only once in a hundred years! Despite all that, Prodigy Lu’s Single Spirit Root is the finest of its kind.

“There was another disciple with a Single Spirit Root who entered the sect alongside him—the eldest young master of the Meng Family. And who is this scion? The Meng Family stands as the foremost among all ancestral clans in the world, making their eldest son the foremost figure among all young masters. Yet even with such a status, Eldest Young Master Meng still couldn’t help but burn with envy at Lu Yang’s Single Spirit Root!

“Once word of Prodigy Lu’s Single Spirit Root spread, numerous ancestral clans and sects sought marriage alliances with him, only to be turned away by the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“In contrast, despite Eldest Young Master Meng’s lofty position and immense talent, not a single marriage proposal came his way. Such was the gulf between them!

“After joining the sect, Prodigy Lu was taken in as the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s final disciple.”

The crowd gasped softly. Who could have imagined that Prodigy Lu’s Single Spirit Root would be so impressive?

The ragged Daoist priest was a wandering storyteller, having only arrived at the teahouse a few days prior. At first, the patrons had turned up out of habit, expecting little from his storytelling. But the moment this ragged Daoist priest opened his mouth, he stunned his entire audience—he narrated the Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect, including stories no one had ever heard of!

This was the newest version of the Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect!

Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect was the most beloved story among the common folk, its iconic episodes often the subject of fervent discussion—plots like the “the Innate Daoist Priest met an immortal guiding the way and found the Dao-Seeking Sect,” “the Dao-Seeking Nine descend the mountain to vanquish evil and uphold righteousness,” and “the Taciturn Daoist Priest opens the heavenly gates with his sword, with all heroes pledging allegiance.”

Anyone who hadn’t heard of the Dao-Seeking Sect would be considered hopelessly behind the times.

Since the ragged Daoist priest was narrating the newest version, it naturally became the talk of the town. The teahouse owner had been grinning so widely these past few days that new wrinkles had formed on his face.

“At that time, a great devil lurked within the Dao-Seeking Sect. The Taciturn Daoist Priest was suppressed by this devil, who then took over his position as sect leader, yet this incident escaped the detection of everyone in the sect.

“Prodigy Lu was the first to sense something amiss. He saw through the great devil’s disguise, tracked down the Taciturn Daoist Priest, and surmounted countless trials and perils before finally removing the seal to free the Taciturn Daoist Priest and return him to the world!

“After this ordeal, the Taciturn Daoist Priest saw past the affairs of the mundane realm and chose to roam the world, leaving sect affairs in the hands of his proudest and most accomplished eldest disciple.

“For his contribution in rescuing the Taciturn Daoist Priest, Prodigy Lu earned the sect’s recognition and was hailed as a great meritorious hero.

“Even the sect leader of the Five-Elements Sect personally visited the Dao-Seeking Sect, requesting an audience with this young prodigy. Upon meeting Prodigy Lu, the Five-Elements Sect Leader treated him with utmost respect, regarding him as an equal and extending the courtesies befitting a fellow sect leader.”

The audience murmured in awe. If the Five-Elements Sect Leader showed so much deference to Prodigy Lu after the rescue, the Taciturn Daoist Priest must indeed hold an exalted position.

“Prodigy Lu possessed exceptional judgement and an impressive record of battle achievements. What is the Dao-Seeking Sect? It is ranked first among the Five Great Immortal Sects. Every disciple in there is a prodigy and unparalleled among their peers.

“However, Prodigy Lu dared to challenge beyond his level. At the Foundation Establishment Stage, he challenged three higher major realms—battling Golden Core, Nascent Soul, and Divine Transfiguration cultivators in succession, emerging victorious every time! Everyone in the Dao-Seeking Sect was astounded by these feats.

“Although Prodigy Lu is remarkably talented, he remains humble. He maintains excellent relationships with his senior brothers and sisters, and they also often seek him out for sparring sessions—everyone learning and growing together with harmonious camaraderie.”

Even if the audience had never met Lu Yang, they had gained a rough impression of him. Formidable cultivation and exemplary character—what a perfect cultivator.

Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect told how the Taciturn Daoist Priest was renowned throughout the land. Wherever he went, someone was bound to recognize him and enthusiastically invite him to banquets, even arranging sword dance performances in his honor. However, the Taciturn Daoist Priest would decline and say, “The friendship between gentlemen should be as insipid as water; there is no need for such fanfare and extravagance.” Those who were turned down would always appear disappointed and regretful.

What does this prove? It proves that the Taciturn Daoist Priest has friends everywhere. Prodigy Lu’s humility and penchant for making friends must have come from his shifu, the Taciturn Daoist Priest. No wonder he is the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s final disciple. The disciple truly takes after his master.

The ragged Daoist Priest spoke with torrential eloquence, recounting Lu Yang’s adventures for a full morning before finally bringing his storyteller gavel down with a clack.

“Tomorrow, I shall tell of another legendary disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect—Prodigy Meng! With the Immortal Dao in his heart, he remains unflustered in the face of temptation, his willpower rivaling that of enlightened senior monks.

“See you tomorrow, everyone!” The ragged Daoist Priest downed his tea in one gulp and rose to take his leave.

“This is the money for your storytelling today.” The teahouse owner personally passed a pouch of silver to the ragged Daoist priest.

To the teahouse owner, the ragged Daoist Priest was a money-shaking tree. As long as he’s around, our teahouse business will keep flourishing by the day!

The ragged Daoist priest accepted the silver with a smile, tucking the pouch into his sleeve.

A paper crane fluttered its wings, landing on his shoulder.

The ragged Daoist priest froze, recognizing the paper crane. It’s a letter from Little Yun.

“Little Yun needs me for something?” That shouldn’t be the case though. She just completed my prison release procedures. It hasn’t even been a few days; why is she looking for me already?

The letter from Yun Zhi was worded with caution and politeness. It explained the plans Wu Youdao had revealed about Ji Province and clarified that Lu Yang was currently in charge of managing the sect’s affairs—she was merely helping to write the letter.

At the end of the letter, Yun Zhi wrote:

Little Junior Brother isn’t skilled with words. He asked me to relay this to you, Shifu. The matter of Ji Province is of utmost importance. Please do not refuse and head there posthaste.

“Ji Province, huh... I’m in Ji Province right now.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest put away the paper crane and sighed softly. “Just what cultivation realm is Little Yun at? A mere paper crane could pierce through the ‘Rules’ set by a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator and deliver this letter to me completely intact.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest looked up at the impenetrable sky canopy enclosing the city.

It now bore a small hole in the shape of a paper crane.

Chapter 463: Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate

A few days ago, the Taciturn Daoist Priest was released from prison. After parting ways with Yun Zhi, he continued his travels across the continent, promoting the Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect—and incidentally, his glorious and magnificent image.

When he arrived at Dingxin City in Ji Province, he realized the entire city was enveloped by “Rules.” One could enter but not leave. To the outside world, Dingxin City appeared to function as usual, with a steady stream of people coming and going.

In truth, this was due to the power of “Rules.” Entry was permitted, but exit was impossible. The people who seemed to leave the city in the eyes of the outsiders were merely fake humans formed by the Rules. These fake people were indistinguishable from real people—identical in memory, habits, and behavior. Only when the Rules dissipated would these fake people vanish from the outside world.

At first, the Taciturn Daoist Priest considered piercing through the Rules with a single sword strike. But just as he was about to act, his battle-honed sixth sense warned him to pull back.

He soon realized the “Rules” were not at the Fusion Stage, but at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. If he acted recklessly, he would draw the attention of the one who had established the Rules, complicating matters.

“What rotten luck.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest spat on the ground, focusing intently on formulating a plan.

First, he disguised himself as a ragged Daoist priest, telling stories in a teahouse while observing the Rules. They had been in place for some time, yet the city operated as usual, implying their creator’s objective didn’t lie in destruction.

After several days of observation—and with the teahouse business booming—the Taciturn Daoist Priest finally figured out the Rules in this place.

Different identities and statuses required adherence to different rules. Sentries followed sentry rules, officials followed official rules, and teahouses and restaurants had their own sets of rules.

Though numerous, the core Rules were just two:

<Rule 1: The Great Xia Dynasty does not exist; only the Great Yu Dynasty reigns here.>

<Rule 2: Everyone in Dingxin City is a subject of the Great Yu Dynasty.>

This confirms the Rules have been established by a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator from Great Yu.

But what is their goal? What purpose does carving out a piece of Great Xia’s territory to “establish” Great Yu serve?

The Taciturn Daoist Priest had pondered this question for days without any clue. It wasn’t until his dear disciple’s paper crane arrived that realization dawned upon him.

Great Yu wants to seize a portion of the national fortune’s power in Hanshui City and attempt to deploy it in Dingxin City—the schemes in both Hanshui City and Dingxin City are interconnected. The aim is to study and harness the power of national fortune.

As for why Great Yu hasn’t abandoned Dingxin City despite their failure in Hanshui City and the capture of Wu Youdao’s trio, it’s because Great Yu cultivators are still unaware that they’ve been caught.

Back then, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had let Wu Youdao’s trio escape on the surface, only to secretly recapture them later. To the world, it seemed the trio had fled successfully. Great Yu’s cultivators only knew what the public knew; they weren’t omniscient.

“So that’s how it is. Great Yu’s ambitions are not to be looked down upon.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s lips curled into a cold smile as he gazed up at the hole punctured by the paper crane in the sky canopy.

The sky canopy is a manifestation of the Rules. Its failure to heal suggests a loophole in the Rules has emerged. It also means that the Great Yu Transcendent Tribulation cultivator has detected the paper crane’s presence.

“Daoist, what’s wrong? Who sent the letter?” The teahouse owner asked gingerly, unnerved by the ragged Daoist priest’s eerie smirk.

“My eldest and youngest disciples.”

“They’re also storytellers?”

“Something like that. Ah, boss, I have to go back on my word. I can’t continue storytelling here tomorrow. Please apologize to the patrons on my behalf.”

“Ah, why?” The teahouse owner was dumbfounded. Everything has been fine; why quit so abruptly? And where can he even go? It’s not like he can leave Dingxin City, right?

Suddenly, an overwhelming pressure descended upon the city, plunging it into chaos. Panic spread as people stood frozen, unsure where to run or what they were up against.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest sighed softly. “Because it’s time for me to act.”

With a flick of his horsetail whisk, it transformed into ten thousand swords, blotting out the sky. Countless golden rays were unleashed, momentarily matching the oppressive pressure.

The people in the city were no longer affected by the oppressive pressure.

“A momentary lapse, and a pest slipped in!” The figure releasing the oppressive pressure glared fixedly at the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

When the paper crane flew toward the Taciturn Daoist Priest, he had also noticed the latter’s existence. He could tell that the Taciturn Daoist Priest, while formidable, was still at the Fusion Stage and hardly a threat.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was undaunted as he soared upward to confront the figure. Raising his hand, the ten thousand swords merged into a single peerless sword, bathed in lightning as it materialized in his hand.

“Ten Thousand Swords Return to One?!” The voice carried surprise. To witness this highly revered sword technique among Sword Dao cultivators here is unexpected.

“I am the sect leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect, the Taciturn Daoist Priest. Who are you?”

“You may address me as the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest narrowed his eyes. Historical records mention that the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord was an Intermediate Transcendent Tribulation cultivator from the early days of Great Yu.

Not totally unbeatable.

Clutching the treasured sword, countless metal artifacts and magical treasures throughout the city resonated, as if answering his call or bowing to his supremacy; the tremors of the magical treasures reverberated through the heavens.

His sharp blade gleamed, resplendent as a rainbow and cold as ice, pointing skyward with scathing murderous intent. Slowly, he uttered the name of this move. “Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate.”

The sword cleaved down like a flowing river, shaking the sky canopy. Carrying boundless killing intent, it surged toward the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord.

Watching the sword descend from the sky like a waterfall, the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord’s hairs stood on end as he barely dodged the attack.

Boom! The sword qi shattered the heavenly canopy, making the firmament tremble. Clouds dispersed, revealing a clear sky and a blazing sun hanging high as millions of civilians in Dingxin City watched in awe.

The Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord’s heart quailed at this scene. This is no move a Fusion cultivator should be able to unleash!

“Still hardly a threat. How many times can you execute such a move?” A trump card like this would drain a Fusion cultivator’s spirit energy after one or two uses. Not a threat at all!

“As many times as I please!” The Taciturn Daoist Priest burst into peals of laughter, unleashing Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate again.

Caught off guard, the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord reacted a beat slower, and his arm was severed cleanly. Sword qi perforated the severed limb from inside out, pulverizing it into dust.

“You’re courting death!” the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord bellowed in rage. To think I lost an arm to a Fusion cultivator? If word gets out, what face do I have to continue mingling in the cultivation world?!

“Asura Body!” A three-headed, six-armed Asura phantom emerged behind him, wielding drums, pagodas, and rulers...

The Taciturn Daoist Priest and the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord clashed in a frenzied battle, shrouding the world in darkness, turning day and night upside down, and shattering space and knitting it again.

The longer they fought, the more alarmed the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord grew. It’s my first time facing a Fusion cultivator who can match me!

Unfortunately, the Taciturn Daoist Priest couldn’t maintain this state for long. After a brief exchange, the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord seized an opening, and his Asura Body pierced the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s defenses, causing his aura to plummet.

“To have forced me this far, you should be proud. Now die!” The Asura Body’s six arms descended like divine retribution, their might unstoppable.

“How dare you hurt a cultivator of Great Xia?!” A thunderous roar echoed nearby, its sheer force alone pausing the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord’s movements.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest coughed blood but laughed upon seeing who had joined. “Took you long enough! Any later, and I’d have prepared to break through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage!”

“Who are you?!” The Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord fixed his eyes on the visitor. This person’s shout could halt my attack—his cultivation surpasses mine!

“Chen Tao, Head of the Luoshui Guard’s Nine Palaces.”

Chapter 464: Lost a Fortuitous Opportunity

The Taciturn Daoist Priest had pieced everything together after he received his disciple’s letter. A battle was inevitable. While he could hold his own against a Great Yu Transcendent Tribulation cultivator temporarily, he would undoubtedly lose out in prolonged combat.

The letter had stated that experts from the imperial court and the Five Great Immortal Sects were already en route. His task was simple—ignite a grand battle to draw the opponent’s attention and buy time until reinforcements arrived.

“Senior Chen Tao.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest glanced upward at the figure now confronting the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord, his heart settling down.

The Luoshui Guard was the imperial court’s specialized force for dealing with plundering cultivators and archaic cultivators. Among them, the strongest nine were known as the “Nine Palaces.” As their head, Chen Tao’s cultivation realm and power were unfathomable.

In terms of seniority, Chen Tao was even older than the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s shifu; he was a bona fide old monster of the cultivation world. The fact that the imperial court had dispatched Chen Tao spoke volumes about how seriously they viewed the Great Yu cultivators’ threat.

“Pah!” The Taciturn Daoist Priest spat out a mouthful of bloody saliva, his face grimacing in pain; he felt as if his whole body had fallen apart.

During the fight earlier, he had used sword qi to reinforce his body, temporarily bolstering his physical resilience. But now that the sword qi had dissipated and his injuries acted up, every acupoint was bleeding, soaking his robes in blood in mere breaths.

“Truly brutal.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest fished out several pills from his sleeves, each a supreme-grade pill etched with pill marks and exuding pill fragrance, and swallowed them whole.

His wounds began to close, the pain easing.

“Cleanse Body. Cleanse Garment.” As the Taciturn Daoist Priest cast the Body-Cleansing Technique and Garment-Cleansing Technique, the bloodstains vanished, and his robes became pristine as new, his body now feeling light.

“Seventh Senior Brother’s pills never disappoint.” The pills he had just consumed were priceless treasures that Seventh Elder had refined from the roots of Little Herb Kings. It could even be the headline item of an auction for Fusion cultivators. Since the Taciturn Daoist Priest often traveled around and was bound to run into danger, he always kept such life-saving pills on hand.

“Chen Tao of the Luoshui Guard?” The Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord’s gaze locked onto the elderly newcomer without a shred of carelessness. He could sense a lethal threat radiating from Chen Tao.

“Run!” This is no place to linger. I must escape right away!

“Let’s see where you can run to!” Another voice rang out behind the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord.

Whirling around, the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord blanched. Another Transcendent Tribulation cultivator has arrived!

From below, the Taciturn Daoist Priest recognized the new visitor—another of the Luoshui Guard Nine Palaces. “The Luoshui Guard has three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators in total, yet the imperial court has sent two at once. They’re truly going all out.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest grinned. The more people join, the lower the chances of the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord escaping.

Without hesitation, the newcomer unleashed a river of talisman runes that flowed out from the void and coalesced into chains of law, aiming to capture the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord alive.

The Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord’s heart sank. The talisman runes flow naturally and ceaselessly like a river, proof that this person has achieved major success in talismans. Once these chains weaved from the talismans bound me, I’m afraid I wouldn’t be able to break free in a short amount of time.

He charged skyward, desperate to breach the encirclement by the two Transcendent Tribulation cultivators.

“Trying to escape? Have you asked the Dao-Seeking Sect?!” Grandpa Ba’s voice boomed from above as he stomped downward on the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord.

Grandpa Ba stood at the array’s core, forming a blockade above Dingxin City, while Third Elders and others took positions according to the Seven Stars.

Seven Stars Converged—North Star Array!

The Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord avoided them, activating his Asura Body, which rampaged and shattered space. Just as he was about to lunge into the rift, a voice echoed from within.

“Did you forget the Prison Suppression Sect?”

From the space rift surged ancient ferocious beasts—Dijiang Bird[1], Golden-Winged Great Peng Bird, Hundun Beast, and more—their mountain-sized forms exuding primeval savagery, and their features twisted as they bared their fangs.

Eight strong figures stepped out of the space rift, their bodies adorned with tattoos of these very ancient ferocious beasts.

It was the Prison Suppression Sect’s battle tattoo cultivation method!

“The Five-Elements Sect...”

“The Moon Laurel Immortal Palace...”

“The Hanging Monastery...” Though the Hanging Monastery had sent only one person, it was their Custodian Monk, whose combat prowess was no less than Qiu Jin’an’s.

Officials and generals from the imperial court also joined the fray, brimming with battle spirit as they cracked their knuckles.

Due to their high cultivation, the two Nine Palaces from the Luoshui Guard had arrived first, soon followed by Fusion cultivators from the Five Great Immortal Sects, who besieged Dingxin City until not even a drop of water could leak out.

In total, over forty Fusion cultivators had gathered. And these weren’t just any Fusion cultivators—they hailed from the Five Great Immortal Sects. Any one of them was capable of outmatching the average Fusion cultivator.

With the two Nine Palaces and the immortal sects’ Fusion cultivators, even Wu Youdao’s trio would have been reduced to punching bags. Even if the trio had obtained Wilderness Province’s national fortune and Wu Youdao’s Dragon-Tiger Qi had undergone evolution, they would still stand no chance.

To prevent another Hanshui City incident, the imperial court and immortal sects had specially mobilized overwhelming manpower to purge Ji Province of all potential threats. It could be said that if any Great Yu cultivator dared to show themselves now would face the combined wrath of the righteous path!

By the same logic, the Taciturn Daoist Priest dared not show himself either.

The people in Dingxin City had never witnessed such a sight. They couldn’t distinguish Transcendent Tribulation cultivators from Fusion cultivators, nor were they aware that any one of these figures outclassed their own city lord—a mere Void Refinement cultivator.

However, this didn’t stop them from cheering in excitement. They had been tormented under the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord’s rules for far too long, where even minor infractions would lead to death, forcing everyone to live in constant vigilance.

“Boss, I’ll take my leave first. Until we meet again.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest bid farewell to the gobsmacked teahouse owner.

In truth, the teahouse owner was a cultivator, but his cultivation was mediocre at best, so he opened a teahouse in Dingxin City to pass the time. Even he could sense that the cultivators who had just arrived eclipsed the city lord in cultivation; they were peak experts in the cultivation world. It had been nearly a hundred years since so many experts acted together. Even now, he still couldn’t believe his eyes.

“Ah, you’re leaving?” The teahouse owner wanted to urge the Taciturn Daoist Priest to stay. Just now, he spoke like he was prepared to lay down his life and go all out against the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord. So why is he leaving now that help has arrived?

“If I don’t leave now, I won’t be able to leave anymore.” Without further explanation, the Taciturn Daoist Priest slipped away while the crowd’s attention was on the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord.

“Capture him alive!” Chen Tao barked, then led the charge. Biting his fingertip, he sent droplets of golden blood flying out, each transforming into divine weapons that rained toward the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord.

“It’s been ages since we’ve seen Senior Chen Tao’s Hundred Refined Divine Weapons!” Someone from an immortal sect marveled, joining the assault with a kaleidoscope of attacks that rendered the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord helpless.

Despair took root in the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord’s heart as the chains formed from talisman runes shackled him, sealing his cultivation.

“Finally caught one!” Chen Tao smirked. Until now, Great Yu cultivators have only been captured by the Dao-Seeking Sect. This time, it’s finally the imperial court’s turn.

“By the way, where is that cultivator who tied with the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord?”

Chen Tao had directed all his attention on the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord, not registering the person who had fought with the latter.

“Ask the city lord. He must have seen him,” Grandpa Ba suggested.

Under the scrutiny of so many experts whose cultivation far surpassed his own, the trembling city lord sketched a face they all knew too well.

“Damn it! That little Taciturn brat got away!”

Everyone slapped their thighs in frustration, as if they had lost a tremendous fortuitous opportunity.

If the Taciturn Daoist Priest had stayed, what a perfect chance for payback it would have been!

“Interrogate and torture the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord. If not for him, that little Taciturn brat wouldn’t have escaped!”

The Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord, “...”

Didn’t I hear that Great Xia cultivators get along peacefully? It sure doesn’t look that way...

1. Dijiang ☜

Chapter 465: Great Yu’s Imperial Preceptor: The Dao-Seeking Sect Must Die

Inside a masterless cave domain, an old man whose face was wreathed in wrinkles abruptly rose from his seat upon hearing his subordinate’s report, his terrifying aura flooded every inch of space.

“What? Dawnbreaker was captured?!”

Seeing the Imperial Preceptor’s fury, the subordinate braced himself to reply, “Yes. The Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord was captured by Great Xia. Several of our brothers hiding in Dingxin City have also lost contact and are likely caught.”

The Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord had been a crucial combat asset for Great Yu’s resurgence, a blade meant to carve into Great Xia. However, before he could even draw blood, he had been seized by Great Xia instead.

Damn it!

“I have seen the Rules over Dingxin City; they were indestructible. Outsiders shouldn’t have known what was happening inside the city, and Great Xia shouldn’t have reacted so quickly. Tell me everything you’ve learned. How was Dawnbreaker discovered?”

The news had come too abruptly, leaving the subordinate little time to gather details. “The Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord was discovered by the Dao-Seeking Sect Leader, the Taciturn Daoist Priest.”

“Taciturn Daoist Priest?” Since the Taciturn Daoist Priest was the sect leader of one of the Five Great Immortal Sects, the Imperial Preceptor had long kept tabs on him. This man’s whereabouts are erratic, and his intentions inscrutable—a truly troublesome cultivator.

“Your Excellency?” The subordinate hesitated upon noticing his master mumbling to himself.

“It’s nothing. Continue.”

“Somehow, the Taciturn Daoist Priest detected the anomaly in Dingxin City and entered alone. Since he was only at the Fusion Stage, the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord didn’t pay him much mind. For days, the Taciturn Daoist Priest simply told stories in a teahouse, making no other suspicious moves.

“But then, for some reason, a paper crane pierced through the heavenly canopy of rules established by the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord, creating a loophole. This gave the Taciturn Daoist Priest an opening.

“The Taciturn Daoist Priest unleashed Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate, cleaving the sky canopy and engaging the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord in battle. Though they were initially locked in a stalemate, the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord eventually gained the upper hand and defeated the Taciturn Daoist Priest. But just as he was about to deliver the killing blow, the Luoshui Guard’s Nine Palaces arrived and stopped him.

“Originally, the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord could have escaped, but reinforcements kept coming, including another Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, over thirty Fusion cultivators from the Five Great Immortal Sects, and a dozen more from the imperial court.”

The Imperial Preceptor sighed, raising a hand to signal that his subordinate didn’t have to continue elaborating. I can guess what happened afterward. Against so many cultivators, Dawnbreaker couldn’t have escaped, and even suicide would have been difficult.

The subordinate was indignant. “If not for those reinforcements, the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord could have escaped!”

The Imperial Preceptor shook his head. Things are far more complex. He analyzed the incident calmly. “There are three suspicious points here.

“First, why did the Taciturn Daoist Priest enter Dingxin City? Was it truly a coincidence?

“Second, how did that paper crane penetrate the sky canopy and create a loophole? Who folded the paper crane, and what is their cultivation level?

“Third, why did people from the imperial court and the immortal sects arrive in Ji Province so timely? Was it a coincidence or premeditated?

“Upon further contemplation, these three points of suspicion can be connected.”

Though the subordinate appeared meek before the Imperial Preceptor and didn’t raise his head, he was in fact an old monster at the Fusion Stage, once a prominent, sharp-witted figure in the early days of the Great Yu Dynasty. The shocking news had momentarily stunned him, but now, with the Imperial Preceptor’s reminder, realization also dawned upon him.

Following the Imperial Preceptor’s theory, he deduced, “Before entering Dingxin City, the Taciturn Daoist Priest must have already noticed the anomaly within the city. He contacted the imperial court in advance, arranging for them to lie in wait while he scouted the city alone. Both parties likely agreed that if they didn’t hear from him in the next few days, they would breach the sky canopy with the paper crane.

“A few days later, the paper crane pierced through, triggering the great battle!”

The Imperial Preceptor nodded approvingly. My subordinate is clever enough to follow my reasoning. Still, he added, “That paper crane doesn’t seem like something a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator could produce. It was probably the work of a half-immortal.”

Tapping his chair, the Imperial Preceptor showed a trace of relief. “There must have been a half-immortal figure overseeing Dingxin City then. With this lineup of one half-immortal, two Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, over forty Fusion cultivators, do you think their goal was to capture Dawnbreaker? No—they meant to capture me!

“I’ve looked into the Taciturn Daoist Priest. His actions are erratic, bizarre, and abstruse. As the sect leader, why did he abandon his duties, instead wandering everywhere and telling stories? Is this what a Fusion cultivator and a sect leader would do?”

The subordinate nodded. As a Fusion cultivator and sect leader myself, I would never do something like this.

“Only after this incident do I understand his intention! His wandering and storytelling were a ruse—he was actually tracking us down!”

The subordinate felt enlightened. The Imperial Preceptor’s intelligence is truly not what mine can compare to. “So that’s how it is!”

“This Taciturn Daoist Priest—no, not just him. The entire Dao-Seeking Sect is an obstacle to Great Yu’s resurgence!

“The Calamity Venerable Lord was captured by the Dao-Seeking Sect at the Qing Province Grand Ceremony.

“Huang Ming, the mole we planted in the Corpse-Driving Sect, was exposed by the Dao-Seeking Sect’s disciples. His Majesty was forced to act prematurely, ruining the plan. And all three of them remain missing!

“Now, the Taciturn Daoist Priest is even scouring the land for our whereabouts.

“Every step of our plan has been thwarted by the Dao-Seeking Sect. Once or twice could be a coincidence, but three times? It proves that the Dao-Seeking Sect’s fortune impedes the fortune of Great Yu’s resurgence!

“The Dao-Seeking Sect has 120,000 years of history, founded during the Great Yu Dynasty. Yet they’re opposing us at every turn now. They really don’t know what’s good for them! Do they think aligning with the imperial court and establishing the so-called Five Great Immortal Sects would save their lives?!” Murderous intent seeped out from the Imperial Preceptor’s gaze, sending a chill down his subordinate’s spine.

The last time the Imperial Preceptor revealed such an expression was 180,000 years ago, when he was in seclusion and most Transcendent Tribulation cultivators fell into slumber, awaiting the Great Era.

Six ambitious Transcendent Tribulation cultivators conspired to overthrow the dynasty. Joining forces, the six had shaken heaven and earth. City after city fell before their unstoppable advance, and even the imperial capital was breached.

Right then, the Imperial Preceptor burst forth from his seclusion. Facing the six alone, he still gained the upper hand, slaughtering them one by one before burying a million rebel soldiers alive. For three days, blood clouds loomed over the Central Continent’s skies.

Is the Imperial Preceptor going to make a move on the Dao-Seeking Sect this time? The subordinate clenched his fists in excitement. It’s time for the Dao-Seeking Sect to witness the wrath of Great Yu!

Even six Transcendent Tribulation cultivators weren’t a match for His Excellency. What is a mere Dao-Seeking Sect? Do they think they could withstand the Imperial Preceptor’s fury?

The Imperial Preceptor rose slowly, like a primordial beast awakening, its roar tearing through the void to proclaim its terror and might to all the world. In a steely voice, he ordered his subordinate, “Gather everyone and prepare to move!”

The subordinate was emotional as he stared at the Imperial Preceptor. “Are we making a move on the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

The Imperial Preceptor looked at him like he was an idiot. “With Dawnbreaker captured, Great Xia will learn about this cave domain soon. We must relocate, of course.”

The subordinate, “...”

Chapter 466: Kill Lu Yang First

In a new masterless cave domain, Great Yu cultivators steadily unpacked furnishings from their storage rings, decorating their new grotto. Even a palace was retrieved from the storage ring, its opulent halls towering in the barren cave domain.

Beside the palace was an unassuming thatched hut—the Imperial Preceptor’s dwelling.

As the Imperial Preceptor considered himself a mountain recluse, his abode was deliberately austere. Crouching on a low stool, his eyes were as deep as wells, displaying the image of an ascetic expert.

“Now we’re safe. The Dao-Seeking Sect forced us to relocate—what utter humiliation!”

Who am I? The second imperial preceptor of Great Yu, the successor and promoter of Great Yu’s golden age, and mentor to several virtuous Yu emperors revered by the people.

The first imperial preceptor had two outstanding disciples. The elder disciple conquered lands to establish the Great Yu Dynasty, and he was later known as the Founding Yu Emperor, while I was the second disciple.

Not only am I the second imperial preceptor, but also the junior brother of the Founding Yu Emperor. Who in the world would dare slight me?

And I myself am an expert with terrifying cultivation, single-handedly crushing six Transcendent Tribulation experts.

It’s all because of that damned Taciturn Daoist Priest’s scheme that Dawnbreaker was captured and our cave domain’s location was exposed!

The subordinate’s eyes burned with fury. How dare a mere sect challenge a dynasty? “Damn Dao-Seeking Sect!”

The Imperial Preceptor’s gaze darkened as he strategized. “Up to now, the Dao-Seeking Sect has obstructed Great Yu three times.

“At the Qing Province Grand Ceremony, one of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s cultivators intervened, but it’s unfortunate that the national fortune obscured their identity.

“The second time was when Lu Yang, that little disciple at the Golden Core Stage, saw through Huang Ming’s identity in the Corpse-Driving Sect.

“Finally, the Dao-Seeking Sect Leader, the Taciturn Daoist Priest, used himself as bait to capture Dawnbreaker.

“These three must die. We’ll start with the person with the lowest status—Lu Yang. If Great Yu hesitates further, Great Xia and that hidden Great Qian will mock us!”

Since both Great Yu and Great Qian intended to overthrow Great Xia, they were rivals. The Imperial Preceptor had searched for Great Qian’s hideout multiple times, hoping to pit Great Qian and Great Xia against each other and weaken each other, allowing Great Yu to reap the benefits from the sidelines.

It’s a pity we ended up empty-handed.

The Imperial Preceptor ordered, “Investigate this little disciple called Lu Yang and find out where he is now. Kill him if possible.”

“Understood!”

After the subordinate left, the Imperial Preceptor contemplated. According to the reports, a third faction had appeared during the Hanshui City battle, claiming to be the Supreme Grand Heavenly Sovereign, an immortal from the Heavenly Court Creed; she defeated Wu Youdao’s trio.

“What exactly is this Heavenly Court Creed? And who is Dou Heavenly Sovereign?” Despite the Imperial Preceptor’s extensive knowledge and investigation of power dynamics of the current era, he had never heard of the Heavenly Court Creed, much less Dou Heavenly Sovereign.

“This Heavenly Court Creed seems to have appeared out of nowhere. Strange. Why did the Heavenly Court Creed obstruct Wu Youdao? Do they also covet the national fortune’s power?”

Five days later, the subordinate returned.

“Found Lu Yang?”

“Yes.”

“Killed him yet?”

“About that...”

“You can’t even kill a mere Golden Core cultivator?!” The Imperial Preceptor seethed, clearly dissatisfied with his subordinate’s performance. If everyone is like this, how could Great Yu hope to restore its glory?

His subordinate wanted to cry, but no tears came. “Your Excellency, Lu Yang is now the acting sect leader.”

“Huh?” The Imperial Preceptor thought he had misheard. Although I despise the Dao-Seeking Sect, surely they couldn’t have fallen to a plight where their acting sect leader is a Golden Core cultivator.

I was reluctant to target the Taciturn Daoist Priest precisely because he is a sect leader. Making a move on him would be too conspicuous, and things could easily go wrong. Now that Lu Yang has become the acting sect leader, there’ll certainly be many people protecting him. Acting recklessly wouldn’t be wise.

“According to my investigations, this involves internal power struggles within the Dao-Seeking Sect. A cultivator named Yun Zhi has effectively controlled the sect for years, acting as de facto sect leader. She is the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s eldest disciple, and her cultivation is unclear. The Taciturn Daoist Priest was unwilling to let Yun Zhi hold power for too long and render him a figurehead, so he appointed his youngest disciple Lu Yang as acting sect leader.”

The Imperial Preceptor sneered. “Your analysis is too superficial. Lu Yang is merely a Golden Core cultivator. How could he possibly vie for power with his senior sister? This is clearly the Dao-Seeking Sect anticipating my move against him and elevating his status to acting sect leader preemptively as protection!

“Let me ask you, did Lu Yang’s appointment as acting sect leader happen after his return from Hanshui City?”

His subordinate gazed at the Imperial Preceptor with awe and admiration. “Your Excellency is astute! It was precisely after returning from Hanshui City that Lu Yang was made acting sect leader!” Isn’t this why we follow the Imperial Preceptor? It’s because of his brilliance in governing heaven and earth and his flawless foresight!

A knowing expression crossed the Imperial Preceptor’s visage. “Hmph. There aren’t that many coincidences in the world. Behind every coincidence lies a scheme.”

“Then this Lu Yang...”

“Kill him! We must kill him! So what if the Dao-Seeking Sect has seen Great Yu’s payback coming? Do they believe they can protect a mere Golden Core cultivator? I will let the Dao-Seeking Sect and all under heaven know that all schemes are reduced to nothing in the face of absolute power!”

The subordinate was overjoyed. He could already envision the Dao-Seeking Sect’s gobsmacked faces and helpless rage after they slaughtered Lu Yang. “I also learned that the Dao-Seeking Sect will be holding their sect celebration in two months for their 120,000th anniversary. Many factions will be invited then, and we could seize this chance to infiltrate!” Normally, the Dao-Seeking Sect’s defenses are impenetrable with strict entry protocols; only during such large-scale events will vigilance relax slightly.

“I didn’t know about that.” The Imperial Preceptor’s eyes glinted as his lips curled into a smile. “Looks like Heaven truly favors Great Yu.

“The Dao-Seeking Sect has been around for 120,000 years. Time for it to be extinct.” He casually sentenced the Dao-Seeking Sect to death. If we can’t even deal with this insignificant sect, what hope do we have of restoring Great Yu?

~~~

Meanwhile, Lu Yang remained unaware that he had been marked by the Imperial Preceptor and added to the must-kill list.

This was a misunderstanding born of asymmetric information.

At the Qing Province Grand Ceremony, the Calamity Venerable Lord could have escaped, but Lu Yang summoned Yun Zhi, who defeated him.

In Hanshui City, Wu Youdao’s trio was about to obtain the national fortune’s power, but the Everlasting Immortal Fairy residing within Lu Yang intervened and captured the three.

In Dingxin City, the paper crane that reached the Taciturn Daoist Priest had been written at Lu Yang’s directive.

Had the Imperial Preceptor known Lu Yang was involved in all three incidents, the latter would have been added to the must-kill list long ago. But even if Lu Yang knew he was already on the must-kill list, he wouldn’t pay much mind to it. After all, far more pressing matters demanded his attention now.

“Big Senior Sister, did you just say I have to attend a meeting in the imperial palace as acting sect leader?”

Chapter 467: Ancient Immortal Gatherings

Lu Yang was currently impersonating the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s golden finger, exercising the authority of acting sect leader to plan the sect celebration. After all, we can’t just invite everyone over to eat and drink while the Immortal Fairy gives her opening and closing remarks. That would be too lackluster for a 120,000-year anniversary.

Let alone passing Yun Zhi’s standards, even Lu Yang himself couldn’t bear to look at it.

Well, maybe it could pass the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s standards.

“Celebrations should be about having fun together. Why make it so complicated?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy spoke from experience, advising Lu Yang to abandon modern extravagant customs. “Even our ancient immortal gatherings weren’t this elaborate. When I offered to cook, the Qilin Immortal and the others told me not to cook so as not to overexert myself.”

These so-called ancient immortal gatherings were essentially the Everlasting Immortal Fairy using her charisma to gather four other unfortunate souls, occasionally including the Qilin Immortal’s two wives.

“Then what did you do at these gatherings?”

“Exchange cultivation insights, of course. With only five of us immortals then, it was hard to find peers to discuss with, so everyone treasured each gathering. We would freely speak and study the remarkable applications of Dao Fruits. Such intellectual exchanges often sparked new ideas or left trials for later generations.”

Lu Yang nodded. This finally sounds like the immortals in my impression—discussing the Immortal Dao and setting trials for future generations.

“Specifically?”

“Specifically, I researched how to maximize the damage from self-detonation.

“The Heaven Mandate Immortal asked if we could brainstorm other tricky tribulation punishments.

“The Epoch Immortal said he developed new applications of the Epoch Dao Fruit, creating a mysterious space where time flowed differently; one day inside equaled a year outside.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Please stop terrorizing the world.

“Other times, we would write stories, like the Heavenly Court and Buddhist sects. Don’t underestimate these tales! We crafted them with care, and every one of them contained profound principles to inspire future generations.

“The Heaven Mandate Immortal claimed it would also obscure ancient history for later generations, thereby covering up any embarrassing incidents.”

Lu Yang felt that the Heaven Mandate Immortal was another ruthless individual. Even with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s “help” in dragging him down, he went to great lengths to maintain his image. I wonder whether he is aware that he has become a philanderer who seduced married women and impregnated countless women.

Since I empathize with the Heaven Mandate Immortal, I hope he empathizes with me too by showing mercy when coming for my life.

“Sometimes, we’d play catch with the planets. Mortals called it ‘meteor showers’ and viewed them as divine miracles, making wishes upon seeing us tossing the planets around.”

Lu Yang proved an excellent listener, quietly absorbing these ancient tales from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy for a full hour, occasionally reacting to the stories and prompting thoughtful questions.

It’s said that history constantly repeats itself and that one should draw on the lessons from history. After carefully considering the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s experiences from the ancient immortal gatherings, he found no lessons he could draw on and finally reached a conclusion.

I have wasted an entire hour.

Just then, Yun Zhi walked into the cave abode. Although her countenance remained impassive as usual, her little junior brother Lu Yang had a fifty percent accuracy in reading her micro-expressions.

I’m certain she has business to discuss.

Despite the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s lower accuracy rate, she also made the same judgment. After all, I’m performing magnificently as acting sect leader. Lass Yun wouldn’t visit for no reason.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was bubbling with joy on the inside. I’m the acting sect leader, while Lu Yang and Lass Yun are my loyal adjutants.

“Big Senior Sister, what brings you here?” Lu Yang asked, still in control of his body.

“I just received news that the Xia Emperor has an idea that he needs to implement, and he hopes the sect leaders of the Five Great Immortal Sects can convene for a meeting in the imperial palace.”

Lu Yang and Yun Zhi stared at each other for a few seconds before Lu Yang pointed at himself incredulously. “Me?”

“Not you. It’s Senior Immortal Fairy,” Yun Zhi corrected seriously.

“That’s good then...wait, how is there any difference?!”

“Of course, there’s a difference!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy huffed. “I will be attending the meeting, not you!” She eyed Lu Yang, suspicious that the latter harbored treasonous ambitions.

Lu Yang tuned out the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s outcry.

Despite my impressive credentials—being the youngest disciple of the Taciturn Daoist Priest, Big Senior Sister’s little junior brother, the second-in-command of the Everlasting Lineage, creed founder of the Everlasting Creed, young creed leader of the Heavenly Court Creed, host to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, the strongest Golden Core cultivator, and record-holder for challenging beyond one’s level—the thought of sitting alongside the Xia Emperor and other sect leaders to discuss major affairs of the righteous path still makes me uneasy.

“I’ll go with you.” Yun Zhi finally shared a piece of good news.

Lu Yang exhaled slightly. I’m just an insignificant Golden Core cultivator. How am I qualified to sit with the other four immortal sect leaders? But with Big Senior Sister present to provide support, the pressure will reduce drastically.

“Let’s go.”

No preparation was needed for the meeting; they simply had to be present in person. Yun Zhi exited the cave abode and pinched a cloud from the sky with two fingers, and an auspicious cloud appeared beneath her feet.

“Acting Sect Leader, after you.”

Lu Yang’s body was taken over, and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy unceremoniously used his body to step onto the cloud. She stood with her arms crossed, gazing ahead with lofty aloofness.

“Lass Yun, set off.”

Whoosh. The cloud accelerated violently. Caught off guard, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy lost her footing and tumbled from one end of the cloud to the other, barely clinging onto it with half her body dangling precariously over the edge.

After much effort, she finally climbed back onto the cloud, albeit in a sorry state. “Lass Yun, you did that on purpose!” She pouted at Yun Zhi.

Yun Zhi deadpanned, “No, it was an accident.”

“On purpose!”

“An accident.”

“On purpose!”

“Accident.”

Lu Yang interjected, interrupting a great battle between cultivators of the past and present that was about to boil over. “By the way, Big Senior Sister, did the Xia Emperor mention the meeting’s agenda?”

“He said he wants to organize a competition for young cultivators to identify those who have dispersed their cultivation to start anew.”

“What?”

~~~

The Imperial Preceptor lifted his head, eyes narrowing as he watched the auspicious cloud pass overhead.

“Your Excellency, what’s the matter?” his subordinate asked, hoping to assist his master.

“That was Lu Yang on the cloud just now.”

His subordinate was floored. “What?! Should we strike now?”

They had come to the Dao-Seeking Sect’s vicinity to survey the sect’s surrounding defenses and layout to plan for their infiltration. Never did they expect to see their target the moment they arrived.

The Imperial Preceptor had his own plans and shook his head. “No need. Killing him now would be letting him off too easily. We must wait until the celebration begins and kill him in front of everyone!

My goal isn’t just to kill Lu Yang—I will annihilate the Dao-Seeking Sect!

Chapter 468: First Visit to the Imperial Capital

In the imperial palace, the Xia Emperor and the four immortal sect leaders fidgeted uncomfortably—neither sitting nor standing felt appropriate. Despite all their meetings, they had never encountered such a situation.

Lu Yang occupied the seat designated for the Dao-Seeking Sect Leader, while Yun Zhi stood behind him like a subordinate.

With Yun Zhi standing, who dared sit?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy dared.

After all, the invitation is for me, the acting sect leader. As the leader of the Five Ancient Immortals, what’s wrong with me sitting here? Even sitting on the imperial throne would be perfectly normal.

Staying in his mental space, Lu Yang wasn’t as nonchalant as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

The imperial capital was the largest, most prosperous city and nexus of power on the Central Continent, constantly drawing countless cultivators to flock to its gates.

Lu Yang was no exception. He yearned to visit, eager to experience its unique cultivation sights and scenery. However, he hadn’t expected it to happen so soon.

I’d imagined myself arriving discreetly, accidentally stumbling into some conspiracy. After solving it, I’d find myself caught in a whirlpool of political machinations, navigating power struggles and the fight for the throne. I would survive through wit and by maneuvering between various factions, my actions eventually drawing the attention of the Xia Emperor.

While I stand before the emperor during the court assembly, foes would spew endless accusations of treason, only for the Xia Emperor to dismissively wave his hand at them with a meaningful look and declare, “He’s the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s disciple. It’s impossible that he’d rebel.”

My enemies would be shocked.

The officials would be shocked.

Cultivators in the imperial capital would be shocked.

And just like that, my name will spread across the world.

This is standard procedure.

But I didn’t expect myself to skip through all that process and end up straight at the finale, meeting the Xia Emperor in the palace now.

“Fellow Daoist Yun, why don’t you take a seat?” the Xia Emperor suggested with an ingratiating smile.

Yun Zhi shook her head. “I am but an ordinary disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect now. How am I qualified to sit? This Sect Leader Lu is our acting sect leader.”

The Xia Emperor, “...”

What an ordinary disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect indeed.

“Is this Sect Leader Lu the same Lu Yang mentioned in our meeting half a month ago?” Xia Emperor asked despite knowing the answer. They had just brought up how the Heavenly Court Creed was established by Lu Yang—an outstanding young talent.

I didn’t expect that in just half a month, this young talent would rise to sit as my equal.

From his mental space, Lu Yang secretly observed the Xia Emperor. This monarch of the mortal realm and foremost figure of the righteous path isn’t as austere and decisive as in the legends, and neither does he carry the genteel of a scholar. His temples are streaked with white, and his cheeks hollow—signs of deficiency in qi and blood and waning vitality.

If not for knowing his identity, no one would have guessed that this man was hailed as a legendary emperor of the ages. Perhaps the Xia Emperor once possessed an imposing yet scholarly aura. But now, drained of his lifespan, his former glory had dimmed.

“You know the Xia Emperor and Sect Leader Qiu,” Yun Zhi briefed Lu Yang—and by extension, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy—before the meeting. “This is Fellow Daoist Luo Hongxia, the palace leader of the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace and Lan Ting’s shifu. She even brought Lan Ting to our sect to propose marriage.”

Luo Hongxia’s eyes twitched. I really wasn’t there to propose marriage. She swept her gaze over Lu Yang’s clean and unadorned features. So this is the boy Lan Ting couldn’t stop thinking about? He isn't as good-looking as Lan Ting described.

The moment she recalled starry-eyed Lan Ting gushing about Lu Yang’s brilliance after returning from the Qing Province Grand Ceremony, she felt her blood boil. With a cold snort, she pointedly showed Lu Yang a sour face.

“She doesn’t look well. Did she eat something wrong?”

“This is Yang Ding, sect leader of the Prison Suppression Sect.”

“Greetings.” Yang Ding held no hostility toward Lu Yang. Although Lu Yang was the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s disciple, he was also Yun Zhi’s little junior brother. The positives and negatives canceled out, leaving no reason for animosity.

Yun Zhi introduced the only Transcendent Tribulation cultivator present. “This is Master Jiesha of the Hanging Monastery. He’s currently cultivating the Mouth-Shut Chan Meditation.”

Due to Master Jiesha’s shriveled frame, the kasaya passed down through generations of the Hanging Monastery hung loosely on him. His eyelids drooped as he fingered his prayer beads, offering only a silent nod.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was slightly stunned. This was her first time meeting an enlightened Buddhist monk. She didn’t expect the Buddhist sects she and her fellow immortals had fabricated to be cultivated in earnest by later generations and even expanded upon.

The wisdom of later generations is truly not to be underestimated, no less inferior than mine.

Her brow scrunched up slightly.

“What’s wrong?” Lu Yang asked.

“Someone’s spying on this place—likely the master of the national fortune.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s senses were sharp when it came to countersurveillance; after all, she was someone who could track the ancient immortals.

Lu Yang understood what was going on. An immortal affiliated with the imperial court is likely keeping tabs on this place. That’s perfectly normal.

The Xia Emperor opened his mouth, but Yun Zhi beat him to it. “After returning to the sect, I consulted many elders. One erudite senior proposed a method that can break through lifespan limits and extend one’s life.”

“What method is it?” The others couldn’t find a solution for the Xia Emperor’s predicament despite scouring their own sects.

“In the ancient era, there was a natural spiritual peach tree. Consuming its fruits could extend one’s lifespan, but the tree can run. Its current whereabouts are unknown.”

“Such a thing exists?!” Everyone was visibly moved. None had heard of the natural spiritual tree. The Dao-Seeking Sect’s foundation is truly terrifying.

The Xia Emperor was the first to regain composure. “I’ll dispatch people to search for it.” There's no use rushing; whether I can find it depends on fate.

He pivoted to another important matter. “Great Yu’s plans in Ji Province have been exposed; your esteemed sect’s Taciturn Daoist Priest uncovered the conspiracy first. To save the civilians, he used himself as bait and threw himself into the fray, using Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate to shatter the Great Yu Transcendent Tribulation cultivator’s Rules. He engaged in a battle of strength and wits and sent out a signal, holding out until Palace Leader Chen Tao and reinforcements from the immortal sects arrived. Finally, they captured this Great Yu cultivator together.

“His deeds drew widespread acclaim. Palace Leader Chen Tao and the elders from the immortal sects showered praises on the Taciturn Daoist Priest and were extremely impressed with him, wishing to honor him formally. However, the Taciturn Daoist Priest forsook fame and recognition, choosing to withdraw after his meritorious contributions. Everyone tried to search for him multiple times, but to no avail.”

Everyone present wore odd expressions. They had already heard the reports on Dingxin City from the elders of their respective sects. This version seems to diverge quite significantly...

“Who wrote this report?” Qiu Jin’an was perplexed. Did a spy from the Dao-Seeking Sect infiltrate the imperial court? This is practically praising the Taciturn Daoist Priest to the high heavens.

The Xia Emperor’s face darkened. “The folk pingshu story Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Qiu Jin’an, “...”

All eyes locked onto Lu Yang and Yun Zhi, the message clear: The Taciturn Daoist Priest is from your sect, and he’s always starting rumors and creating trouble—what are you going to do about it?

With her shrewd mind, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy borrowed Yun Zhi’s words. “I was appointed acting sect leader by the sect leader—I have no authority over him.”

“So?”

“So, I can write a letter, suggesting the sect leader abdicate in my favor. Once I become sect leader, I’ll have authority over him.”

Chapter 469: The Increasingly Lively Anniversary Celebration

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s words sent ripples of shock across everyone. As expected of the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s most junior disciple. He’s only at the Golden Core Stage, yet he is already planning to usurp the sect leadership.

Even Yun Zhi turned her head slightly in surprise.

Lu Yang buried his face in his hands. I knew nothing good would come from attending this meeting.

Immortal Fairy, stop trying to emulate Big Senior Sister all the time. Even if you can mimic her words, you can’t mimic her ability.

Shifu might agree to you staying as sect leader forever, but Big Senior Sister won’t!

Right, Big Senior Sister?

Lu Yang turned to Yun Zhi, only to find her wearing a contemplative expression, as if she was genuinely considering the feasibility of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s proposal.

The Xia Emperor coughed lightly, steering the conversation away. “Ahem, let’s not dwell on the Taciturn Daoist Priest. We’ve already learned the location of the Imperial Preceptor from Great Yu’s Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. Mr. Chen Tao rushed there immediately, but unfortunately, he was still a step too late. The Imperial Preceptor and his subordinates had already fled, leaving the cave domain empty—even the ground had been scraped and stored away in storage rings.”

His tone sounded helpless. The imperial court had acted swiftly enough, even skipping the interrogation and torture for the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord and directly searching his soul to pinpoint the Imperial Preceptor’s location as fast as possible.

However, the Great Yu faction was no pushover either. They abandoned their cave domain without hesitation, fleeing with a speed that rivaled the crafty Everlasting Creed’s.

With the Nine-Netherworlds Creed bamboozled by the Heavenly Court Creed, the two Great Yu imperial preceptors were undoubtedly the greatest hidden threats. Catching them sooner would ease the imperial court’s burden.

“I’ve gathered everyone here today to discuss the issue of archaic cultivators dispersing their cultivation to cultivate anew. In the past, we only set our sights on those at the Fusion and Transcendent Tribulation stages.

“As it happens, Sect Leader Lu—the person involved—is here. After the incident with Huang Ming of the Corpse-Driving Sect, we realized our previous understanding had some serious blind spots. These archaic cultivators are ruthless in their pursuit of fortuitous opportunities in the Great Era, even resorting to something as uncertain as dispersing their cultivation to cultivate anew.

“Right now, they’re still weak and pose no immediate threat. But give them time to grow, and they’ll become a big problem. They may stab us in the back at a critical moment or leak core intelligence.”

Luo Hongxia frowned, finding the matter intractable. “We recognize the problem, but is there any solution?”

The Xia Emperor had convoked them precisely because he had an idea.

“I’ve thought of a solution. I’ll issue an edict to call upon all young cultivators in the land to participate in a grand competition—starting at the city level, then the provincial level, and finally the national level. Every young cultivator must participate, with no exceptions or excuses permitted.

“Let’s take Qing Province as an example. Qing Province will internally select thirty individuals from each cultivation stage, representing the pinnacle of Qing Province’s young cultivators. Then, we’ll gather the young cultivators from all seventeen provinces for a grand tournament. From there, we can identify those who might be archaic cultivators who have dispersed their cultivation to cultivate anew.

“What are the characteristics of such reforged cultivators? They possess vast experience, avoiding the typical mistakes in cultivation. Their combat styles also differ from modern cultivators. These two factors would likely make them stand out.”

This was a feasible method, but Luo Hongxia remained slightly doubtful. “But wouldn’t the archaic cultivators deliberately concede defeat halfway through or deliberately lose at the provincial level? They’d never reach the national level and show themselves to us.”
