The Xia Emperor shook his head. “Concede defeat? How could archaic Fusion cultivators yield or lose on purpose to their peers after dispersing their cultivation to start anew? Their pride wouldn’t allow it. If they do concede defeat, even if they achieve success in their cultivation in the future, their mental state will be flawed and prevent them from going far.”

Lu Yang could attest to this. During his fight with Huang Ming, the latter had even resorted to Mental Arrows to secure victory; he would rather risk exposing his identity than lose.

“Why only young cultivators? Why not older ones?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was puzzled but didn’t voice her question out loud, secretly asking Lu Yang instead.

“Think about it, Immortal Fairy. What do these reforged cultivators seek? It’s perfection at every cultivation stage before advancing to the next. Why would they choose to stay at one cultivation stage until they’re old? There’s no benefit in that.”

“That makes sense. I thought the same,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy replied.

Yang Ding raised another loophole in the plan. “But what if your imperial edict doesn’t work and the reforged cultivators refuse to participate? Those who are part of sects won’t have a choice; their elders will drag them there even if they don’t want to attend. However, others may hide in cave domains and stay there until they reach the Fusion Stage. What do we do with those?”

The Xia Emperor analyzed, “Then there’s nothing we can do. If they remain hidden in cave domains, no one will discover them, and any imperial edict will be useless. But such cases should be rare. Great Xia is a new world to them. Could they truly resist the temptation to explore it—ignoring modern cultivation theories and faction dynamics and focusing solely on cultivating in seclusion?

“Besides, even if they emerge from seclusion after reaching the Fusion Stage, they’ll just be another rogue Fusion cultivator who has no access to core intelligence, rendering them hardly any threat.”

After the Xia Emperor’s explanation, everyone agreed the plan was sound. While it wouldn’t ferret out all archaic reforged cultivators, tracking down some was better than none.

“Should the immortal sects send participants?”

“Yes. Archaic reforged cultivators would have reached the peak of every cultivation stage. Ordinary cultivators may not defeat them. We can’t let these archaic cultivators win the championship, can we?”

“The immortal sect disciples will serve as the safety net.”

“Alright.”

“Coincidentally, the Dao-Seeking Sect’s sect celebration is around the corner. We can host the final national-level tournament there. What do you think, Sect Leader Lu?” The Xia Emperor turned to Lu Yang.

“Of course, no problem!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy agreed readily; she had already received Yun Zhi’s approval.

The more attendees, the livelier the celebration, and the more it would showcase my prowess as acting sect leader!

Seeing the gleeful Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Luo Hongxia suggested, “By the way, Sect Leader Lu, since you defeated the reforged cultivator Huang Ming at the same cultivation stage and even Sect Leader Qiu is full of praises for you, would you be willing to demonstrate your remarkable skills?” Though she framed it as a friendly exchange, her real intention was to teach Lu Yang a lesson. It wouldn’t be too harsh, so Yun Zhi wouldn’t intervene.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy showed a troubled expression. “Wouldn’t it be unfair for the strong to bully the weak?” As an almighty immortal, fighting a Fusion cultivator would mean fighting beyond two major realms.

Luo Hongxia misunderstood, assuming she meant that a Fusion cultivator fighting a Golden Core cultivator would be unfair. She retrieved a small circular box from her storage ring. “This is a supreme treasure of the immortal palace. It can adjust our cultivation to the same realm. It’ll absolutely be fair!”

As the almighty Moon Laurel Immortal Palace Leader and a top-tier Fusion cultivator, even if I lower my cultivation to Lu Yang’s level, I can still beat him up easily!

So what if Lu Yang had defeated a reforged cultivator? They’re merely cultivators with shaky foundations. I’m far stronger than them!

Chapter 470: The Everlasting Immortal Fairy Uproots the Laurel Tree

“Then bring it on.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was eager to give it a try, not afraid of Luo Hongxia’s challenge. I've dominated the ancient era for sixteen glorious years, stringing together victory after victory. Challenging beyond my level is practically a part and parcel of daily life. I’m also the inventor of the Unbeatable Golden Core. When it comes to battle, I fear no one!

Even Yun Zhi is not an exception!

No one intervened. Instead, they found the situation rather interesting, clearing space for Luo Hongxia and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to get at it and showcase their potential. Everyone, including Qiu Jin’an, wanted to see Lu Yang’s true aptitude. During Lu Yang’s fight with Huang Ming, Qiu Jin’an had sensed that Lu Yang hadn’t shown his full hand and believed he had other trump cards up his sleeve.

Luo Hongxia opened the small circular box. It was a treasure named the Light-Retaining Treasure Box, refined from the horn of a xiezhi unicorn.[1] Chanting an ancestral incantation, she activated the box. Two beams of light shot out, enveloping her and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy respectively.

Just as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was about to dispel the light beam, Luo Hongxia said, “Don’t resist. The treasure box will adjust our cultivation to the same level.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy decided to give Luo Hongxia some face and ceased resisting.

With a whoosh, the two of them were sucked into the treasure box.

The interior was boundless space, and its environment could be freely altered based on the wielder’s will. Mountains, rivers, lakes, and oceans could be conjured for terrain-based combat.

The moment they entered the treasure box, Luo Hongxia’s cultivation began plummeting all the way from the Fusion Stage to the Intermediate Golden Core Stage. Her physical strength and mental power also adjusted accordingly.

“Intermediate Golden Core Stage, huh... Truly nostalgic.” Luo Hongxia smiled. In my youth, I was a peerless prodigy whose mere presence made peers of the same level lose the courage to fight. Now that I have returned to the Intermediate Golden Core Stage with the experience of a Fusion cultivator, who could possibly defeat me?!

“Begin!”

Luo Hongxia tossed a seed, casting the Tree-Planting Mantra. It sprouted into a graceful laurel tree, its leaves swaying and shimmering with vibrant vitality. The laurel tree could provide her with endless energy.

“Bright Moon Aloft!” As she raised her hand, an argent moon appeared in the sky. It sprinkled its moonlight over the world and morphed into a light cone as it barrelled toward the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Every light cone carried impressive power; a single strike could incapacitate an ordinary Golden Core cultivator.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy dodged with feline nimbleness, her subtle movements evading every attack. This was the “Qilin Step” she had derived after observing the Qilin Immortal’s scurrying about with his agile footwork during their battles. It allowed him to narrowly dodge a few of her attacks—a rare feat, unlike the Heaven Mandate Immortal, who relied solely on brute defense due to his inferior footwork.

Seeing that none of her attacks were landing, Luo Hongxia performed hand seals, transforming the light cones into a ceaseless downpour.

Faced with this unavoidable attack, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy stamped her foot, causing the loess beneath to ripple like ocean waves. Layer upon layer surged forth, forming a roaring tsunami of yellow earth that threatened to swallow Luo Hongxia before the light cones could hit their target.

With a single finger pressed against the yellow soil, the entire mass instantly became incredibly hard and stopped moving, blocking the light cones that rained down.

“Pointing Ground To Steel?!” Luo Hongxia gasped, never expecting Lu Yang to be capable of this move.

She then snorted coldly. So what if he knows an ancient spell?

“Moon Mortal Descent!” The moon came crashing down toward the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, colliding with the steeled earth in an explosion that stirred plumes of dust.

As the dust settled, Luo Hongxia scanned the battlefield for Lu Yang’s figure but found no trace.

“Wait, he’s underground!” Luo Hongxia’s rich combat experience kicked in. Qiu Jin’an had often ambushed her with this move in their youth. Practice made perfect, allowing her to react in the shortest time possible.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had employed a bona fide Earth Escape Technique, its effects nearly identical to Lu Yang’s “Shrinking Earth.”

Luo Hongxia leaped into the sky. This way, I’ll be able to dodge no matter which direction Lu Yang attacks from.

“Bright Moon Aloft.” Another luminous hung overhead, ready to bombard Lu Yang the moment he surfaced.

Bang! The Everlasting Immortal Fairy burrowed out of the earth, not to attack Luo Hongxia but the laurel tree she had planted at the start of the battle.

Luo Hongxia’s continuous assaults demanded more power than an Intermediate Golden Core cultivator could sustain; even Lu Yang would struggle. The conclusion was obvious—the laurel tree provided Luo Hongxia with a steady stream of power.

This was a common battle technique used by the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace. Only Nascent Soul disciples could master it; even Lan Ting couldn’t cast it. Luo Hongxia had relied on her experience to execute it at the Golden Core Stage.

A flicker of panic crossed Luo Hongxia’s visage before her composure returned. She hadn’t anticipated that her opponent would be so shrewd as to identify her weak points this swiftly.

The laurel tree possessed no offensive capabilities. It only had two traits: provision of spirit energy and impregnable defense. Even if Lu Yang has several formidable offensive spells at his disposal, breaching the laurel tree’s defenses within a short time is impossible!

“Quite tough.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy delivered a casual punch that merely made the laurel tree sway, with not even a single leaf falling. “Looks like I’ll need to use some special methods... Paraquat Fist!”

To cultivate the Immortal Fairy Fist Technique, she had studied tens of thousands of herb-related fist techniques. From them, she derived a specialized fist technique designed to counter herb-based lifeforms. With a single punch, all nearby herbs would wither, leaving no plant alive in its path. Hence, it came to be known as the Paraquat Fist—Withered Hundred Herbs.

Once the fist connected with the laurel tree, the leaves wilted yellow, and its branches drooped. In the blink of an eye, the tree had withered!

Luo Hongxia suddenly coughed out a mouthful of blood, her complexion turning ghostly pale from the backlash of the laurel tree. She didn’t expect her opponent to kill the laurel tree with one punch. What kind of fist technique is this?!

But so what? Even without the laurel tree, how could I lose to a junior?

As Luo Hongxia dove down, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy uprooted the laurel tree and swung it at her, smashing her into a daze.

~~~

In the imperial palace, prominent figures of the righteous path clustered around the treasure box, buzzing with speculation.

“Who do you think will win?”

Since those outside couldn’t view the situation inside the box, they could only guess.

“Probably Hongxia. Her combat experience surpasses even those reforged Fusion cultivators. Lu Yang is just a junior. How is he supposed to fight her?” Yang Ding rubbed his cheek.

“I think so too,” the Xia Emperor concurred.

“Don’t dismiss Lu Yang entirely,” Qiu Jin’an cautioned, not daring to speak too definitively. After all, Yun Zhi personally trained this little junior brother; he’s bound to have a few other tricks.

“Look! The treasure box is glowing! The outcome is about to be decided!”

Boom! Luo Hongxia was blasted backward out of the treasure box, seeing stars with her mouth full of leaves.

1. Xiezhi is a mythical Chinese “unicorn.” You may have seen statues or sculptures of it. ☜

Chapter 471: The Everlasting Immortal Fairy Against the Four Sect Leaders of the Great Immortal Sects

“Fellow Daoist Luo, are you alright?” Yang Ding was startled. He had just declared that Luo Hongxia would undoubtedly crush Lu Yang. How did she get flung out so abruptly?

Her posture was also far from dignified—mouth stuffed with yellowed leaves and hair dishevelled with twigs and foliage, as if she had collided headlong into a tree.

“Pah!” Luo Hongxia spat out the leaves. “Nothing serious. Just accidentally got smacked by a tree.” Her wounds were already healing. Once outside the treasure box, her cultivation reverted to the Fusion Stage.

“Got smacked by a tree?” Qiu Jin’an was nonplussed. Ordinary trees couldn’t have harmed Luo Hongxia. Did Lu Yang use the Tree-Planting Mantra as an offensive method? Although Qiu Jin’an knew the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace’s tradition of fighting with laurel trees and the trees’ astonishing defense, the idea that someone could uproot a laurel tree mid-battle never crossed his mind.

“This junior Lu Yang is a little uncanny. I accidentally fell into his trap.” Luo Hongxia gritted her teeth. Had the laurel tree not withered suddenly, I wouldn’t have lost so quickly.

“That powerful? Or did you underestimate him and let a junior seize an opening?” Yang Ding eyed her skeptically. Luo Hongxia had a history of underestimating her opponents in her youth, her complacency leading to her undoing multiple times.

“If you’re so skilled, why don’t you try?!” Luo Hongxia flared up.

“Fine, I’ll try it then!” Yang Ding refused to believe what had happened. Luo Hongxia has a habit of underestimating foes, but I don’t. Besides, the more I use battle tattoos, the more proficient I become. Now, even if I can only use battle tattoos at the Golden Core Stage, their versatility, adaptability, and sheer power surpass even sword cultivators’!

A beam shot out from the treasure box, enveloping Yang Ding. Familiar with its mechanisms, he didn’t resist and successfully entered the box, his cultivation lowered to the Golden Core Stage.

“Fellow Daoist Yang should be able to win.” The Xia Emperor nodded.

Unlike the semi-secluded Moon Laurel Immortal Palace, the Prison Suppression Sect’s disciples often left the sect to uphold justice and punish wrongdoings. Having experienced numerous battles, Yang Ding’s combat experience was superior to Luo Hongxia’s. Combined with his unique battle tattoo cultivation method, Yang Ding’s combat power increased the more his cultivation realm was suppressed.

“That should be the case.” Qiu Jin’an was extremely confident in Yang Ding. No matter how strong Lu Yang is, he shouldn’t be able to defeat Yang Ding.

Only Master Jiesha and Yun Zhi remained silent.

Whoosh. The treasure box shook, and Yang Ding tumbled out, failing to balance himself before his head crashed against the ground.

“Damn it! What kind of fighting style was that?!” Yang Ding cursed, seething with indignance. I’ve never fought such a stifling battle. It felt like he had calculated my every move, dragging me into his rhythm. Under such circumstances, my defeat was naturally inevitable.

“And your hair?” Qiu Jin’an wore an odd expression. Yang Ding had entered with a head of black hair, but he exited with a head of no hair. Qiu Jin’an already knew the answer, for he was present when Lu Yang unleashed his Arhat Fist on Huang Ming.

“I’ve never seen such a reprehensible fist technique! I can let it slide if it only hits people, but it even made my hair fall out!” Yang Ding was incensed as he touched his shiny scalp. Paired with his tattoos, Yang Ding now resembled an escaped crime lord; people would pin all kinds of crime on him, and no one would believe he was innocent.

“That was the Arhat Fist with Fist and Spell As One,” Yun Zhi explained, making Master Jiesha’s eyes gleam.

Arhat Fist? One with fist and spell merged and capable of causing hair loss?

Why didn’t such a promising budding talent join our Hanging Monastery, but instead was snatched up by that bastard Taciturn Daoist Priest?

“Fist and Spell As One... No wonder,” Yang Ding groaned. Now that I think about it, it did seem like Fist and Spell As One. It’s just that the spell’s effect was so absurd that I couldn’t react in time.

“By the way, Old Qiu, Lu Yang’s clamoring for you to go in to get pummeled next.” Yang Ding grinned deviously at Qiu Jin’an. “This brat said the only thing you have going for you is your slightly higher cultivation. At equal levels, he would thrash you like a grandson.”

“He’s tired of living!” Qiu Jin’an bellowed in rage. With Luo Hongxia and Yang Ding as precedents, even he wasn’t certain he could defeat Lu Yang, so he was reluctant to step in.

But after such taunts from Lu Yang, how can I continue staying out of this?

I, Qiu Jin’an, am someone with pride!

The treasure box’s beam swallowed Qiu Jin’an into the box.

~~~

“Why did Sect Leader Yang appear all of a sudden?” Lu Yang was baffled. After the Everlasting Immortal Fairy used his body to defeat Luo Hongxia, she was restoring her stamina when Yang Ding descended from the sky and demanded a duel.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy immediately used the Unbeatable Golden Core, following its advice to steadily force Yang Ding into retreat. In the end, still following its suggestion, she returned control to Lu Yang, allowing him to personally unleash the Arhat Fist, delivering simultaneous blows to both mind and body.

“Speaking of which, how do we get out?” Having defeated two opponents in succession, it was time they left; Lu Yang searched for an exit.

“Lu Yang, you brat! You’ve got guts to challenge me!” Qiu Jin’an boomed, also descending from the above and leaving Lu Yang utterly bewildered.

“Come come come, leave this to me!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy exercised her authority as sect leader again to take over Lu Yang’s body.

~~~

Whoosh. The treasure box quivered as a bruised Qiu Jin’an staggered out.

“Old Qiu, are you fine?!” Yang Ding yelled, rushing to support him.

Qiu Jin’an shot Yang Ding a venomous glare and shoved him aside. Only mid-battle had he realized that Lu Yang never trash-talked. This old bastard made it up!

His cultivation and wounds healed simultaneously. “Nothing serious. This brat Lu Yang does have some skill. It’s just that the last thing he said rubbed me the wrong way.”

“What did he say?” Yang Ding’s eyes lit up.

“He said that even the Five-Elements Sect and Hanging Monastery combined still wouldn’t be his match!” Qiu Jin’an slapped his thigh as he gnashed his teeth.

Master Jiesha stopped rolling his prayer beads. His eyes blazed.

All had suffered a thrashing; they must reclaim their dignity no matter what! The Fusion cultivators were young and inexperienced, but a veteran Transcendent Tribulation expert like Master Jiesha would definitely defeat Lu Yang at the Golden Core Stage!

Without a word, Master Jiesha strode forward, his momentum soaring and his gaze firm as he stepped into the treasure box.

Soon, he stumbled out of the treasure box in a sorry plight, now sporting a head of thick, black hair.

His state was better than the three before him. Marginally.

Master Jiesha showed Qiu Jin’an a menacing expression. He had learned during the battle that Lu Yang hadn’t trash-talked.

“Ahem.” Qiu Jin’an coughed. “Now that all of us understand Lu Yang’s combat power... Fellow Daoist Luo, please let him out.”

Luo Hongxia rolled her eyes. I’d wanted to let Lu Yang out ages ago, but you fools just kept charging in one after another, practically surrendering yourselves. No one could’ve stopped you!

Reciting an incantation silently, the treasure box opened, releasing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Huh, it’s over already? Isn’t there still an emperor who hasn’t suffered a beating yet?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy scratched her head, itching to fight more.

The Xia Emperor, “...”

Chapter 472: Internal Battle Among Immortal Sects

The Xia Emperor sifted through his memories. Aside from consistently guessing that Lu Yang would lose, I don’t remember doing anything that might have provoked him.

Given that those inside the treasure box aren’t aware of what happens outside, the conclusion is obvious—Lu Yang simply wants to beat me up.

The Xia Emperor firmly refused to duel Lu Yang one-on-one.

You must be joking! Even Master Jiesha lost. It’s not like I excel at martial arts either. Stepping in there will definitely leave me in a more tragic plight than Luo Hongxia. Judging by Lu Yang’s ruthless tactics—forcing Luo Hongxia to gnaw on leaves, driving Yang Ding to become a monk, and making Master Jiesha return to secular life—he probably has no regard for reverence toward the old, nor would he show any respect to a pitiful old man like me, a flickering candle in the wind.

He applauded softly with a smile as pleasant as a spring breeze, pretending he didn’t hear the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s challenge invitation.

“Wonderful, wonderful! As expected of a youth prodigy to wield such combat prowess at such a young age. Your future knows no bounds!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded, calmly accepting the Xia Emperor’s praise. But of course. My Unbeatable Momentum has been built through winning countless battles until I ascended to an immortal.

“So, you want to fight me?”

The Xia Emperor developed temporary hearing loss and showered Lu Yang with accolades. “Sect Leader Lu, you have made a name for yourself and demonstrated brilliant talents of a promising youth with such vigor and spirit. There’ll surely be a place for you in the upcoming Great Era!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy kept nodding. As the head of the Five Ancient Immortals, I was unbeatable throughout the land. After her accidental death and subsequent rebirth, she discovered the world had forgotten both her name and her legends. Now, with the imminent arrival of the Great Era, she had the opportunity to restore her former glory in ancient times. I must reclaim everything that rightfully belongs to me!

“I like what you’ve said. So, shall we exchange a few moves?”

The Xia Emperor pressed on. “Although your shifu is the Taciturn Daoist Priest and you can’t serve the court as an official, you’re still a son of Great Xia. When you retire from your position as sect leader, I shall grant you the privilege of attending court without hastening your pace,[1] being announced with only your title,[2] and wearing your sword[3] and shoes[4] into the palace hall.”

This was no trivial reward. Such honors require monumental achievements to obtain, the kind that could be recorded in the annals of history.

Setting aside Lu Yang’s extraordinary combat prowess demonstrated by defeating four immortal sect leaders, his pivotal role in annihilating the Everlasting Creed and establishing the Heavenly Court Creed to countervail the Nine-Netherworlds Creed alone would merit such imperial favor.

Of course, the real reason was that the Xia Emperor was trying to stall for time.

He frantically signaled to Qiu Jin’an and the others with his eyes, urging them to help change the subject of their conversation. I can’t count on Yun Zhi. I shot her a meaningful glance, but she returned me an expressionless stare.

Qiu Jin’an cleared his throat and praised Lu Yang as if he wasn’t the one who had just been beaten up. “Sect Leader Lu’s combat awareness is truly outstanding. Although I held back, forcing me to this extent is no small feat. When I was at the Golden Core Stage a long time back, I was undefeated throughout the land.”

Yang Ding nodded, rubbing his shiny bald head as he commented on the earlier battle. “That’s right. In all my years, I’ve never seen combat instincts like Sect Leader Lu’s. He’s a born fighter who has mastered the essence of Fist and Spell As One at a young age—truly the little junior brother Yun Zhi has groomed. It’s a pity that when we fought earlier, I was bullying the young with my seniority, so I was embarrassed to use my full strength, and that led to my accidental defeat. Were I truly at the Golden Core Stage, I would gladly have a good spar with Sect Leader Lu. When it comes to combat between Golden Core cultivators, I’ve never feared anyone.”

Luo Hongxia looked at the shameless pair with undisguised contempt, feeling it was a grace to share the title of immortal sect leader with them. “The spells Sect Leader Lu employed are equally remarkable and unlike anything I’ve ever heard of, as if he’s created a style of his own. With just these skills, defeating those wild cultivators who dispersed their cultivation to cultivate anew would be no problem at all. If I were still at the Golden Core Stage, I would only have a ninety percent win rate against such opponents—hardly worth mentioning.”

What did it mean to be an immortal sect leader? Not only did it demand one’s cultivation to be sublime, but it also required one to represent the sect in the outside world. These three are truly worthy of their title. Their shameless thick skins can rival even Shifu’s.

As expected, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s attention was successfully diverted. She no longer dwelled on sparring with the Xia Emperor and instead asked curiously, “Since all three of you were so formidable at the Golden Core Stage, who was actually the strongest?”

“Haha, what a good question. I was the strongest at the Golden Core Stage,” all three immortal sect leaders declared simultaneously.

As soon as the words left their mouth, the air seemed to freeze, and the atmosphere grew palpably tense. Even Lu Yang could feel the oppressive murderous tension while observing from his mental space.

The three sect leaders exchanged glances, subtly shifting their feet and spreading out with vigilance.

Qiu Jin’an narrowed his eyes. “Oh?” he remarked casually. “Wasn’t I the strongest? At the Golden Core Stage, I challenged opponents beyond my level and destroyed an entire branch of the Everlasting Creed, capturing the branch leader and vice branch leader alive, both of whom were at the Nascent Soul Stage.”

Yang Ding sneered. “Ridiculous! I was simply confined because that old Taciturn scoundrel sabotaged me. Otherwise, I would have made a name for myself across the world. As if you’re the only one who could defeat Nascent Soul cultivators!”

Luo Hongxia was also brimming with confidence and not willing to be outdone. “At the Golden Core Stage, we were united against the Dao-Seeking Nine and never had the chance to face off against each other properly. Looks like the timing can’t be any better.”

“Bring it on then!”

“Who’s afraid of whom?”

“Fight!”

Luo Hongxia activated the treasure box, which shot out three beams of light that sucked all three inside, suppressing their cultivation to the Golden Core Stage.

Right after they disappeared into the box, the murderous atmosphere dissipated, leaving the air quiet once more.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy blinked in confusion, unable to understand why the three had suddenly started fighting. “Aren’t the Five Great Immortal Sects supposed to stand united against common adversaries? This doesn’t feel united at all,” she mumbled. Even we Five Ancient Immortals were more united than this.

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, do you want to take a guess at why they’re fighting?

After waiting a while and sensing no movement from the treasure box, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy figured the outcome of the battle wouldn’t be decided quickly. “There’s nothing else, right? If there’s nothing else, should we head back?”

With fewer people at the meeting, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s enthusiasm waned. At any rate, we’ve finished discussing the matters, and I’ve finished beating up people. It’s time to return.

As acting sect leader, I have to manage the vast Dao-Seeking Sect and handle countless affairs every day.

“There’s nothing else. You may return.” The Xia Emperor’s gaze toward Lu Yang noticeably changed. I can’t wait for this troublesome living Buddha to leave. Not even the Taciturn Daoist Priest had been this much trouble in his Golden Core days.

“Let’s go.” Yun Zhi was satisfied with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s performance. No major complications arose.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy swung her arms as she swaggered out of the palace, with Yun Zhi following half a step behind in perfect decorum. The two departed on their cloud, leaving only the Xia Emperor and Master Jiesha behind.

“Master, you...”

Master Jiesha made no further comments, tearing through space as he left. In truth, he had also wanted to enter the treasure box and show the juniors like Qiu Jin’an what true unbeatability at the Golden Core Stage looked like. But as their elder, he couldn’t bring himself to stoop to such behavior.

Of course, there was another reason. He suspected that if he had entered the box, he might have faced combined attacks from all three opponents, which he reckoned he couldn’t have withstood.

The Mouth-Shut Chan Meditation is truly hard to practice. I could only nod or shake my head during the meeting. It’s unbearably suffocating not being able to speak.

1. If you have watched some dramas, most people are supposed to walk quickly in the presence of the emperor. ☜

2. Having an audience with the emperor could involve a complicated procedure. After all the administrative steps, one’s title followed by their name would be announced. It is an honor to be addressed by only the title and without the name. ☜

3. Starting from the Qin Dynasty (the first dynasty after unification of China), officials were not allowed to carry their swords with them during court assembly due to safety considerations. ☜

4. Before the Yuan Dynasty (the short dynasty under the reign of the Mongols), officials were not allowed to wear their shoes during court assembly as a sign of respect for the emperor. ☜

Chapter 473: Preparations Across the Board

News of the imperial court’s tournament spread swiftly across the continent. Since the finals were to be held at the Dao-Seeking Sect, coinciding with their 120,000-year anniversary, the event was officially named the Dao-Seeking Grand Tournament.

Countless sects were restless, eager to dispatch their most prized disciples into battle. The imminent arrival of the Great Era brought forth a surge of geniuses. Many factions had taken in disciples whose talents eclipsed previous generations, waiting for the perfect moment to stun the world.

Now was finally the opportunity they had been waiting for!

“The Five Great Immortal Sects’ leaders as judges, untransmitted spells, natural treasures, half-immortal-tier cultivation insights, access to secret domains, ancient texts... Even I would be tempted by such rewards! Were I still young, I’d surely vie for them myself!” The Sword Tower Leader sighed.

Why hadn’t such an amazing opportunity existed in my youth? To battle the continent’s finest talents, not to mention the lavish rewards... Forget prizes for the disciples, even if they were given to an entire sect, these rewards would still be a sumptuous gift.

“Ming Tai, you are our Sword Tower’s most gifted disciple in a thousand years and the sole inheritor of our Supreme Lord’s true lineage. This Dao-Seeking Grand Tournament will be your stage, and your name shall resound through the land!”

“I will not let the sect down!”

~~~

“Although our Waterfall Sect is a second-class sect and didn’t qualify for the finals in the past, it’s different this time with you here, Kong Hao. Your talent rivals even the core disciples of first-class and S-class sects!

“I know you’ve always kept a low profile. Even when you became a true lineage and core disciple, you never tried to win over people and build your own factions like the others, instead devoting yourself solely to cultivation and staying away from worldly affairs.”

“Shifu, I...” Kong Hao hesitated. He had chosen the Waterfall Sect precisely to shun the spotlight to avoid trouble. Yet, even if I don’t cause trouble, trouble comes knocking on my door. I can’t even turn this down.

His shifu continued, “If it were any other competition, not participating would be fine. But this is organized by the imperial court. Your shifu doesn’t expect you to win the championship. Just entering the finals would secure a spot for our sect to attend the Dao-Seeking Sect’s celebration. That would bring immense benefits to our sect!

“Besides, with the leaders of the Five Great Immortal Sects as judges, their pointers alone would be of tremendous help to your cultivation!”

“Alright.” He forced himself to acquiesce.

~~~

“Half-immortal cultivation insights? Great Xia actually dares to offer such invaluable stuff? Despite slaving away for the Great Yu Dynasty and slumbering until now, they didn’t even reward me with Transcendent Tribulation insights. Since they didn’t give it to me, I’ll take it from Great Xia instead!

“With those cultivation insights and other prizes, along with my Single Spirit Root, I have much better chances of reaching the Transcendent Tribulation Stage! There shall also be a place for this true lord in the future!”

~~~

“Heh. The finals at the Dao-Seeking Sect? What a coincidence. I was contemplating how to infiltrate the Dao-Seeking Sect, and now, the opportunity has delivered itself.

“Dao-Seeking Sect, huh? When chaos erupts at your celebration, don’t blame me—blame your imperial court’s decisions instead!”

“It’s just that the Dao-Seeking Sect and the imperial court will surely invite experts to watch over the place. This will be tricky. I wonder what cultivation they’ll be at. Never mind, to be safe, I’ll bring everyone.”

~~~

Moon Laurel Immortal Palace.

Luo Hongxia informed her disciple, “Lan Ting, the sect requires a disciple at the Intermediate Golden Core Stage to attend the finals. I have chosen you. Are you willing?”

“Understood!” After receiving the orders, Lan Ting stole a glance at her shifu. Why is Shifu wearing a veil? I can’t see her expression. After a moment of hesitation, she mustered her courage to ask, “Shifu, will I get to see Lu Yang at the Dao-Seeking Sect this time?”

Luo Hongxia’s eye twitched as she gritted her teeth. “Yes, of course, you’ll get to see him. You’ll see him no matter what!”

~~~

Five-Elements Sect.

“Bai Ming, our Five-Elements Sect needs someone at the Intermediate Golden Core Stage to represent us in the competition. You must bring glory to our sect at the tournament.”

“I promise to fulfil this duty. But I have a question.”

“Speak.”

“What’s with the injury on your face?”

“Some questions are better left unasked.”

~~~

Prison Suppression Sect.

Yang Ding addressed his disciple. “Tianzhi, I have but one request. If you encounter anyone from the Five-Elements Sect, beat them mercilessly. You don’t have to give them face!”

“Yes.”

As Yan Tianzhi turned to leave, Yang Ding stopped him. “Wait, aren’t you curious about my injuries?”

“Anyway. I didn’t. Hit you.”

~~~

Slaughterhouse.

“...”

“Shifu, say something! Even if we Buddhist sects emphasize comprehension through intuition and not words, you can’t just give me a look and expect me to understand it by myself!

“Shifu, why did you have to cultivate the Mouth-Shut Chan Meditation for no reason? Now you can’t speak, communicate through your spiritual consciousness, or even write.”

Master Jiesha still didn’t speak.

Shi Chan was at a loss for words. He set down his butcher’s knife and ruminated on the meaning behind his shifu’s gaze.

Everything about the Hanging Monastery is great—senior and junior brothers get along harmoniously, resources are abundant, and we have Transcendent Tribulation experts to guide us.

The only problem is that people talk in riddles.

I used to grumble that Shifu’s words are as good as saying nothing. Well, great—now he doesn’t even speak.

“Forget it, I should get back to slaughtering pigs.”

~~~

Arriving at Heaven’s Gate Peak, Meng Jingzhou entered Lu Yang’s cave abode to find him reclining in his chair with his hands over his belly in indolence.

Big Senior Sister isn’t around.

“Why did you call me here?” Meng Jingzhou scowled, finding Lu Yang unpleasant to the eye. Why are you brat the acting sect leader again?

As promised, Qiu Jin’an had taught Meng Jingzhou an untransmitted spell of the Five-Elements Sect. Meng Jingzhou had just returned from the Five-Elements Sect when he received the acting sect leader’s summons.

“Little Meng! Come, sit, make yourself at home,” Lu Yang said with a wide grin.

Meng Jingzhou scanned the cave abode. There was only one chair—currently occupied by Lu Yang.

Am I supposed to ride on your head, you brat?

Lu Yang automatically ignored Meng Jingzhou’s glare and said leisurely, “You probably have heard of the imperial court organizing a tournament alongside our sect’s celebration. The tournament is carefully divided into categories for every minor cultivation stage. The sect places great importance on this event. After multiple discussions with the elders, we’ve confirmed the participating disciples for each category, but the spot for the Intermediate Golden Core Stage remains undecided, and it’s been quite a dilemma.

“Only the finest disciples can represent our sect. After much consideration, I stood my ground against all objections to choose you.”

Meng Jingzhou’s eyes lit up, the corners of his mouth involuntarily curving into a smile as a comfortable warmth filled him. That sounds more like it. “So you’re admitting I’m stronger than you?”

Lu Yang’s smile was even wider. “I’m a judge.”

All my silent hardships and working like a draft animal under the Everlasting Immortal Fairy without complaint have been for this very moment.

“F*ck!”

Chapter 474: The Everlasting Immortal Fairy: I’ll Help Cultivate in Your Stead

A month and a half passed in the blink of an eye. During this time, the Central Continent buzzed with excitement. City-level and provincial-level competitions unfolded in full swing, gathering all of Great Xia’s talents onto the tournament stages. Match after match brought surprises, as previously obscure cultivators rose to fame overnight, leaving those who knew them utterly dumbfounded. Even meticulously groomed disciples, in whom first-class sects had placed great hopes, were occasionally defeated by unknown minor cultivators.

Soon, the day of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s celebration arrived.

~~~

During the past month and a half, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy ran amok within the Dao-Seeking Sect with Lu Yang abetting her misdeeds—the pair colluding as perfect partners in crime.

At Heaven Gate’s Peak, two Lu Yangs sat inside the cave abode, one reviewing official documents, the other fast asleep—equally occupied in their own ways.

“Just hold on a little longer. Once the celebration passes, it’ll all be over!” Lu Yang pumped himself up while going through the documents. As the celebration approached, he pored over lists of outstanding young talents who had risen through provincial-level competitions and the representatives from various attending factions.

He was currently using the Tree-Planting Mantra’s wooden clone, while the one sleeping was the Everlasting Immortal Fairy who had successfully taken over his body.

“Immortal Fairy, are you sure this counts as ‘helping me to cultivate?’”

Perhaps stirred by a pang of conscience, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt that constantly taking over Lu Yang’s body was improper, as it kept cutting into his cultivation time, so she offered to help him in his cultivation.

After all, we share the same body. It’s the same no matter who’s cultivating.

Then, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued sleeping.

“Haaah.” Roused by Lu Yang, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy let out a huge yawn and scowled at him. “Of course, I’m cultivating! This is the Sleeping Cultivation Method, which operates on the same principle as my sleeping to restore my cultivation. It is a supreme cultivation method only immortals master. As a mortal, the profundities within naturally elude your comprehension.”

Lu Yang inwardly refuted, Aren’t immortals already at the pinnacle of cultivation? What possible use could a “Sleeping Cultivation Method” serve?

But due to the acting sect leader’s overwhelming authority, Lu Yang had no way to rein her in, so he could only return to his paperwork.

~~~

“So this is the Dao-Seeking Sect. How magnificent.” Ming Tai involuntarily remarked in awe as he stood before the Dao-Seeking Sect’s gate, gazing at the undulating mountain ranges beyond and feeling spirit energy permeate every pore of his being.

Representing the Sword Tower, he successfully advanced to the finals and now prepared to enter the Dao-Seeking Sect with his elder. The Dao-Seeking Sect is much more opulent and grand than the Sword Tower.

Ming Tai’s reaction went unnoticed among the crowd. Numerous finalists and the factions were visiting for the first time and were equally thunderstruck by the Dao-Seeking Sect’s lavish and imposing scale. If the spirit energy at the gates alone was this abundant, what wonders must await within?

“Ming Tai, let’s go.” The Sword Tower’s elder strode ahead, beckoning Ming Tai to follow.

The elder was no stranger to the Dao-Seeking Sect. He made his way through the bamboo forest with practiced ease and soon arrived at the center of the sect—the main venue of the celebration.

The main venue comprised Heaven’s Gate Peak, the eight elders’ mountain peaks, and the commercial street, the sect’s most bustling area.

“The Dao-Seeking Sect has certainly put in the work.” The Sword Tower elder stroked his beard. He could tell that the Dao-Seeking Sect took this celebration seriously. At the foot of Heaven’s Gate Peak, they had cleared an open space where a white jade altar now stood. Atop the altar were three towering statues draped in red cloth.

Upon the altar lay ceremonial items such as cauldrons (ding), food vessels (gui), stemmed plates (dou), wine vessels (zun), pots (hu), wine holders (jue), wine cups (xiaojue), candlesticks, incense burners, wine trays, and ceremonial instruments such as bianzhong (chime bells) and bianqing (stone chimes).[1] Other ritual items and tools appeared so ancient that even the elder couldn’t recognize them.

Everything was arranged according to the highest ritual standards. Several Dao-Seeking Sect disciples stood guard around the altar, ensuring no one approached before the ceremony commenced.

“It resembles the Barbarian Tribe’s ancestor worship ceremonies, though this is far more intricate,” the elder commented.

As the oldest branch of humanity, the Barbarian Tribe inherited legacies from ancient times. Their ancestor worship ceremonies were widely regarded as the most authentic recreations of rites in the ancient era. Many scholars seek out the Barbarian Tribe in hopes of piecing the fragments together to catch a glimpse of the ancient past.

What the Sword Tower elder failed to recognize were the elements Lu Yang had the Everlasting Immortal Fairy reconstruct from rites honoring ancestors and immortals in the ancient era.

Although the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was unreliable, her memory was still reliable. She easily reproduced the authentic and orthodox ceremonial procedures from ancient times. She could have conjured up even more ancient and orthodox immortal gatherings, but Lu Yang had vetoed that particular proposal.

“Elder Sikong, it’s been a long time.”

Hearing someone call him, the Sword Tower elder turned toward the familiar voice. It was Lu Baqian, the Corpse-Driving Sect Leader, who had been in the limelight as of late. Trailing behind him were the sect disciples slated to participate in the finals.

“Ah, Sect Leader Lu.” Elder Sikong greeted him with a wave, his unconstrained and clean movements characteristic of sword cultivators.

“Greetings, Sect Leader Lu,” Ming Tai echoed respectfully.

“Haha! How did you know I’ve advanced to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage?” Lu Baqian chortled, his eyes almost imperceptible.

Elder Sikong, “...”

“Brother Sikong, you still haven’t advanced to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage after so long. Looks like you have neglected your cultivation.” As the first among their generation to reach the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, Lu Baqian was flaunting his achievement everywhere he went. To make matters worse, his cultivation was so high that no one could bring him down.

Elder Sikong’s fingers silently gripped his sword hilt for a moment before deciding against drawing his sword.

“This is your Sword Tower’s disciple?” Having bragged enough, Lu Baqian finally noticed Ming Tai.

“Our sole outstanding disciple who has inherited the Supreme Lord’s legacy.” Speaking of Ming Tai softened Elder Sikong's expression with pride.

“The Supreme Lord’s legacy?” Lu Baqian gasped softly, his pupils contracting in astonishment.

A Fusion cultivator could be addressed as “True Lord,” a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator as a “Venerable Lord,” and a half-immortal as a “Supreme Lord.”

This person called Ming Tai has inherited the Sword Tower’s Supreme Lord’s legacy?!

The Sword Tower Supreme Lord was a Sword Dao half-immortal who perished before ascending to an immortal. The legacy he left behind had such exacting requirements that no one was qualified. Lu Baqian hadn’t thought he would meet its inheritor in his lifetime.

The Sword Tower sure played their cards close, quietly grooming such an impressive successor. If not for this tournament, they probably wouldn’t have been willing to bring Ming Tai out.

“Zhao Po, our Corpse-Driving Sect’s outstanding disciple.”

If not for the outlier Huang Ming, Zhao Po would be the Corpse-Driving Sect’s true number one of the younger generation. In addition, the battle at Hanshui City had tempered him and broadened his horizons. After Lu Baqian broke through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, he even personally guided Zhao Po, allowing the latter to improve by leaps and bounds on all fronts.

“Alright, that’s enough. While Sect Leader Lu and I chat, you youngsters can play around.” Elder Sikong shooed them away. Without the juniors present, he wouldn’t have to maintain his formal demeanor.

“Hello, Zhao Po, I’m Ming Tai. You’re a disciple of the Corpse-Driving Sect?” Ming Tai beamed, evidently a cheerful and eloquent person. “That is to say that you’ve experienced the Hanshui City incident?”

The Hanshui City incident was the largest battle seen in nearly a century, involving three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators and the Supreme Grand Heavenly Sovereign who crushed them. The event captured the world’s attention and was adapted into pingshu stories, widely circulated among the masses. Ming Tai frequented teahouses to listen to these tales.

To actually encounter someone who has experienced the Hanshui City battle firsthand—how could anyone stay calm?!

Zhao Po nodded. “Mmm. Back when the battle erupted in the skies above Hanshui City, Senior Brother Lu Yang and I were in the provincial governor’s estate and the nearest to the battle.”

“You even know Senior Brother Lu Yang?” Ming Tai's eyes sparkled, his voice rising an octave in heightened excitement.

What’s all the rage in teahouses? It’s Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect: Chronicles of Lu Yang!

Ahhh!

1. Some of the terms here are archaic and rare terms used nowadays. Anyway, full image gallery below! ☜

Chapter 475: Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect: Chronicles of Lu Yang

Zhao Po got a fright from Ming Tai’s reaction, not understanding why the latter was so excited.

“Haven’t you heard the pingshu story Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect: Chronicles of Lu Yang?”

Zhao Po shook his head. The sect leader has been pushing me to train day and night recently. How could I possibly have the time to listen to storytelling?

“I haven’t listened to the pingshu performances, but I do know Senior Brother Lu Yang. Why?”

“Tell me what Senior Brother Lu Yang did in Hanshui City! Was he really as overpowered as the legends say?”

“His combat prowess is indeed exceptional. I had a senior brother named Huang Ming, about my age, but his cultivation and combat talent were leagues ahead of mine. Later, I found out he was a Great Yu cultivator who had dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew. That’s why he was so strong.

“At the time, I didn’t know. By chance, Senior Brother Lu Yang and I were out exterminating ghosts when we bumped into Huang Ming. The two of them clashed because of me and ended up fighting.”

“Who won?” Ming Tai pressed eagerly.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, of course! He actually fought with Huang Ming, a reforged cultivator, and even managed to hold the upper hand effortlessly!”

“That incredible?!” Ming Tai was floored. Even if I am confident of defeating a reforged cultivator, achieving it with such ease would be impossible.

“You don’t say! Senior Brother Lu Yang and Senior Brother Meng Jingzhou told me their opponents were always at least at the Fusion Stage. Anyone below that wasn’t worthy of being their opponent.

“And the facts proved it. After defeating Huang Ming, a Great Yu Fusion cultivator appeared to kill them. Once that was dealt with, a Great Yu emperor suddenly came out of the woodwork, enveloping Hanshui City with the power of Rules.” Even now, Zhao Po shuddered at the memory. I’ve never encountered this many high-level cultivators in my entire life. But the moment I met Lu Yang, I ran into all sorts of monsters and demons.

Ming Tai mused, “No wonder. That explains everything. Eh, since you said Senior Brother Lu Yang is here in the Dao-Seeking Sect, do you think we’ll get to witness another Transcendent Tribulation-level battle this time?”

Zhao Po waved his hand, feeling that Ming Tai was overthinking it. “No way. Do you know where we are? This is the Dao-Seeking Sect. Even the Great Yu Emperor wouldn’t dare cause trouble here if he dares to come. Besides, there are so many elders and sect leaders present. Any Transcendent Tribulation cultivator who shows up will be in for a hard time.”

Witnessing one Transcendent Tribulation-level battle in a lifetime is already rare. How could we encounter it all the time?

Besides, even if we do encounter it, it would only be after the Great Era arrives, not just two months apart.

Zhao Po asked, “Do you want to grab something to eat? I heard the barbeque here is fabulous.”

Ming Tai wasn’t particularly interested in food. He believed cultivators ought to devote themselves wholeheartedly to cultivation—eating was unnecessary, merely a way to satisfy one’s cravings. However, Zhao Po was being hospitable, so he couldn’t refuse outright. “You go ahead. I’m not really fond of barbeque.”

“Aiya, don’t say that. The barbeque here is really good. You’ll understand once you try it. Wait here, I’ll buy some for both of us.” Ever the enthusiastic and sociable sort, Zhao Po dashed off before Ming Tai could protest. After all, in this world, the more friends you have, the more paths will open.

Ming Tai parted his lips to say something, but Zhao Po was already sprinting toward the commercial street, quickly disappearing into the crowd. He could only lower his hand and wait where he was.

Perhaps because the barbeque shop Zhao Po mentioned was too popular, Ming Tai waited and waited, but there was no sign of him returning.

“Since I’m just standing around, I might as well ask where Senior Brother Lu Yang is. When Zhao Po comes back, we can go see him together.”

Just then, a young man clad in robes of a Dao-Seeking Sect disciple passed by, and Ming Tai swiftly grabbed his sleeve.

The young man was caught off guard and nearly jumped out of his skin, thinking he had been ambushed by an enemy.

“Greetings, Senior Brother. May I ask if you know where Senior Brother Lu Yang is?”

“Lu Yang?” The young man’s expression turned odd as he scrutinized Ming Tai. Fair-skinned, scholarly, and completely unfamiliar—I don’t know him.

“Why are you looking for Lu Yang?” he asked warily.

“Well, I am Ming Tai from the Sword Tower. A few days ago, I was at a teahouse and heard the latest version of the Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect: Chronicles of Lu Yang. I admire Senior Brother Lu Yang greatly and wanted to seize this opportunity to meet him.”

“Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect: Chronicles of Lu Yang?” The young man was bewildered. What kind of ridiculous title is this?

“What did the storytelling say?”

“It said that Senior Brother Lu Yang is extraordinarily talented and the strongest even among those with a Single Spirit Root. He can even challenge beyond his level, defeating Divine Transfiguration cultivators while still at the Foundation Establishment Stage.

“And when he reached the Golden Core Stage, he became even more impressive! In the imperial palace, he fought toe-to-toe with the sect leaders of the four Great Immortal Sects—beating the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace Leader until her mouth was full of leaves, beating the Prison Suppression Sect Leader until he shaved his head and vowed to become a monk, and beating the Hanging Monastery Abbot until he was speechless and grew his hair back as he swore to renounce monastic life!”

At first, Ming Tai had thought the storytelling exaggerated Lu Yang’s feats. After all, folk storytelling is often embellished. But Zhao Po just confirmed that Senior Brother Lu Yang’s opponents are at least at the Fusion Stage.

Doesn’t this match the pingshu story perfectly?

“Senior Brother Lu Yang gave the four immortal sect leaders a harsh thrashing; even the palace eunuchs witnessed it! The Moon Laurel Immortal Palace Leader, the Prison Suppression Sect Leader, and the Five-Elements Sect Leader were all bruised and battered, their injuries still unhealed when they left the palace!

“His Majesty even lauded Senior Brother Lu Yang’s deeds and called him a prodigious youth, granting him the privileges of attending court without hastening, being announced with only his title, and wearing his sword and shoes into the palace hall!”

The young man’s expression grew even stranger. Not long ago, Shifu returned to the sect in the name of “caring for the righteous path,” asking me what happened during the meeting in the imperial palace. After I recounted the incident in detail, Shifu patted my shoulder approvingly, admitting he hadn’t done his job well as a shifu since he was frequently absent. He pledged to help me become famous and told me to wait and see.

Who could have imagined this was how he’d do it?!

He was aware that Qiu Jin’an and the other two had been beaten black and blue. After all, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was responsible for the mess, so he followed up on the subsequent developments.

Originally, the three had been competing for the title of “strongest Golden Core cultivator.” But the fight grew increasingly heated, and they all reverted to their true cultivation realms, leaving each other covered in wounds that wouldn’t recover for a while.

Ming Tai wanted to say something else when the distant toll of a bell reverberated from Heaven’s Gate Peak. It was ancient and resonant, as if it had been struck in the ancient past, its vibrations lingering in the air.

The bell rang twelve times in total, symbolizing the Dao-Seeking Sect’s 120,000 years of history. It also marked the beginning of the celebration. Everyone ceased their activities and gazed toward Heaven’s Gate Peak.

The young man strode to the altar. That was where he was initially headed before Ming Tai intercepted him along the way.

“Senior Brother, you still haven’t told me where Senior Brother Lu Yang is!” Ming Tai whispered urgently.

The young man’s robes dissolved into shimmering feathers, vanishing as immortal threads danced at his feet, weaving upward into dignified ceremonial garb—a coronet, black robes, a crimson skirt, white silk sash, yellow knee covering, and more.

He turned back, his eyes glinting with mirth. “I am Lu Yang.”

Chapter 476: Celebration Commences

As the bell tolled, guests gathered like clouds, crowding around the altar. Everyone’s gaze was fixed on Lu Yang, who was clad in ceremonial robes, his expression solemn and dignified.

Step by step, Lu Yang walked toward the altar, and the crowd instinctively parted before him. No one knew that a fierce battle of wills was currently raging in his mind.

“Come on, let me take over!”

“Immortal Fairy, are you even reliable? Why don’t I do it for you instead?”

“I have been worshipped by people since antiquity. I know the rite procedures better than you!”

After a heated back-and-forth, Lu Yang was forced to surrender control of his body.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy ascended the white jade altar, her strides steady and weighty, as though she had traversed the ages, bearing the gravitas of ancient history.

“Who is this? He looks so young,” murmured the elderly spectators. They were taken aback by Lu Yang’s appearance, which matched none of the figures they knew.

“I heard he’s Lu Yang, the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s most junior disciple. He has been making waves lately. Some claim he’s unbeatable among Golden Core cultivators and is the number one of the younger generation.”

“Unbeatable at the Golden Core Stage?” Such a title carried immense weight. The Golden Core Stage played an integral role in cultivation. To reign supreme at the Golden Core Stage and be called “unbeatable” signified limitless future prospects!

“That still doesn’t make sense. Even if he’s unbeatable among Golden Core cultivators, he shouldn’t be leading the ceremony and ascending the altar.”

“Rumors outside say the Taciturn Daoist Priest intends to groom this youngest disciple, appointing him as acting sect leader and entrusting even such a major ceremony to him.”

“You can’t trust those rumors going around. In my view, that old Taciturn scoundrel dares not show himself and has pushed his disciple to the forefront instead.”

“Sounds exactly like something he’d do.”

“To achieve so much at such a young age, his potential is boundless! I wonder if this Lu Yang has someone he likes. My family has a few girls of suitable age and decent talent.”

“But he’s the old Taciturn scoundrel’s disciple.”

“Forget it then.”

As the Everlasting Immortal Fairy ascended the platform, the bianzhong chime bells resonated, their grandeur transporting listeners back a hundred thousand years.

Fourth Elder and his disciples were performing the Dao-Seeking Sect’s ritual repertoire. As a Confucian cultivator, Fourth Elder was proficient in music, his flute capable of summoning a hundred birds to pay homage. In his youth, this talent of his had charmed countless maidens.

Upon the altar stood three towering statues draped in red cloth. With a spell from First Elder, the cloth fell away, revealing the statues: the founder of the Dao-Seeking Sect—the Innate Daoist Priest, the Primordial Heavenly Sovereign—the progenitor of immortal sects, the Resurgence Ancestor—the Vast Sea Daoist Lord.

These three held special significance in the Dao-Seeking Sect and were known as the Dao-Seeking Sect’s founding triumvirate. When Lu Yang formally became a disciple, their tablets had borne witness.

Holding a yugui jade tablet,[1] the Everlasting Immortal Fairy clasped her hands—left over right and palms inward—and bowed thrice to the tablets.

Below the altar, Yun Zhi observed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy performing the rites with precision and nodded in satisfaction.

According to protocols, even if Lu Yang was the acting sect leader, he shouldn’t have been qualified to preside over the ceremony as the Dao-Seeking Sect’s representative. However, the one standing on the altar wasn’t Lu Yang but the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

As one of the Five Ancient Immortals and wielder of the Everlasting Dao Fruit, the question wasn’t whether the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was qualified to pay respects to the three founding ancestors, but whether their fate profiles could withstand her paying respects.

Lighting the candles, incense spiraled into the air. In a clear and resonant voice, she recited the ritual text. “O Holy Divine Ones, begotten in remote antiquity... With sincere reverence, we offer fine silks, pure livestock, and abundant grains among manifold offerings...”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had ordered Lu Yang to write the ritual text, and in turn, he borrowed her authority to order Fourth Elder to write the ritual text. As the most cultured person in the entire Dao-Seeking Sect, Fourth Elder shouldered this imperative duty without hesitation.

At a glance, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could discern the sophistication of Fourth Elder’s writing. I don’t recognize half the characters, and the rest feel like tongue twisters when I read them.

After the recitation concluded, a satisfied smile graced her lips. That felt amazing.

In the past, others paid their respects to me. Today, for once, I paid my respect to others. As the acting sect leader and guest elder, honoring the Dao-Seeking Sect’s three founders is only fitting.

“Our sect has prepared a range of activities. Everyone, eat well, have fun, and relax for today. The finals will commence tomorrow.”

Lu Yang’s schedule for the celebration was simple: opening ceremony → guest festivities → tournament finals → closing ceremony.

The goal of the righteous path was to identify reforged archaic cultivators who had dispersed their cultivation and cultivated anew during the finals.

But Lu Yang doubted that combat performance alone could reveal whether one was an archaic cultivator. Hence, he proposed organizing activities to observe contestants’ behavior in addition to their battle performance before making a judgment.

The Xia Emperor and other immortal sect leaders approved the idea at once.

The Dao-Seeking was planted with many observers from the imperial court and the immortal sects. All were shrewd masters at reading subtle cues and expressions. As the Dao-Seeking Sect lacked such skilled individuals, they didn’t dispatch anyone of their own.

After the ritual concluded, a group of elders remained extremely curious about Lu Yang. Elder Sikong and Lu Baqian were among them; all were close Daoist friends.

“I heard this junior possesses extraordinary combat prowess and utterly humiliated the four Great Immortal Sects’ leaders and left them severely injured.”

“That must be a rumor. No Golden Core cultivator could achieve that, not even an immortal’s reincarnation.”

“You can’t exactly say that. As the Great Era approaches, it’s not strange for any kind of genius to emerge. Haven’t you heard the ancient legends of individuals born at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage with peerless cultivation and ultimately attaining the Dao to become an immortal?”

“What you said makes some sense, but I can’t help but feel that something about this seems off.”

“Look, Qiu Jin’an and the others are right over there. Why don’t we ask them directly?”

“Let’s go get answers.”

Cultivators acted with decisive boldness; when they thought of something, they would act on it immediately.

Qiu Jin’an and the other three wore stormy expressions as they scanned the crowd for the Taciturn Daoist Priest. News of the Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect: Chronicles of Lu Yang had reached them, and they instantly recognized the handiwork of that bastard Taciturn Daoist Priest.

After a month and a half of recuperation, their injuries had healed. Yang Ding’s and Master Jiesha’s hair had regrown and returned to normal.

“Fellow Daoist Qiu, I heard Lu Yang defeated all of you. Is it true?” the elders asked bluntly, their faces alight with barely concealed schadenfreude.

Four faces darkened simultaneously as they struggled to formulate a response.

“It’s true, but—” Qiu Jin’an admitted reluctantly and was about to launch into an explanation, only to be cut off by Lu Baqian.

“Now, Fellow Daoist Qiu, that’s hardly the proper attitude. One should accept defeat gracefully. Victories and losses are all part and parcel of cultivation. Why make excuses?” As a Transcendent Tribulation expert, Lu Baqian’s words commanded considerable weight.

“Exactly! Old Qiu, you’re always preaching about cultivators needing forthrightness and courage to acknowledge their shortcomings. Why doesn’t that apply to yourself?”

“This attitude will hinder your future cultivation.”

The elders piled on with increasing enthusiasm, unwilling to miss this golden opportunity to mock Qiu Jin’an and the others.

Finally reaching his limit, Qiu Jin’an shot Luo Hongxia a meaningful glance. Understanding his signal, she produced the Light-Retaining Treasure Box. Brilliant rays erupted as the bow swallowed the entire group.

Equalizing cultivation realms required mutual consent, but if it was simply trapping people inside, Luo Hongxia called the shots.

“Attack!”

Inside the treasure box, Master Jiesha struck first while Qiu Jin’an and the other two provided cover, wiping the floor with all the elders.

1. Yugui is a jade tablet held by ancient rulers or nobility during rituals and ceremonies. It tends to have a square base, but it wasn’t the case all the time. ☜

Chapter 477: Fishing

Lu Yang remained unaware that the guests invited by the Dao-Seeking Sect were currently being beaten up by another group of invited guests.

In the cultivation world, such occurrences were commonplace. As cultivators who wielded immense power, acting on whims and engaging in battles was the norm, and so was getting hunted down.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest could personally attest to this.

Having satisfied her ceremonial cravings, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy relinquished Lu Yang’s body back to him.

Along the roadside, disciples had set up stalls, hosting a variety of activities, so many that Lu Yang couldn’t even recognize them all.

When it was proposed that they could organize their own games, the senior disciples eagerly stepped forward, each brimming with ideas; applications piled up like snowflakes in the cave abode. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy devolved her authority to Lu Yang to handle the task, but he was overwhelmed by the sheer volume and passed it on to Yun Zhi.

Yun Zhi’s approval criteria were simple—as long as the activity wasn’t dangerous and didn’t tarnish the Dao-Seeking Sect’s reputation, it was permitted.

“Sect Leader Lu.”

Greetings, Sect Leader Lu.”

“Greetings, Sect Leader.”

All along the way, voices called out to Lu Yang. He nodded in response to every one of them. I must say, this feels pretty amazing.

He changed out of his cumbersome ceremonial robes.

“Acting Sect Leader, would you like to buy some books?” A senior male disciple, often on duty at the Great Mission Hall, beckoned to him.

Those from the Dao-Seeking Sect referred to Lu Yang as the Acting Sect Leader, while outsiders simply called him “Sect Leader.”

“Books? Are they not available in the scripture library? Lu Yang was puzzled.

“These are all good stuff you won’t find in the scripture library. Do you want to take a look?” the senior male disciple urged.

Slightly tempted, Lu Yang stopped at the stall, curious to see what kind of premium goods were on offer. “What do you have here?”

“Acting Sect Leader, although you are the sect leader’s disciple, you probably haven’t interacted with him much. Here, I have an autobiography written by the sect leader himself. Interested in buying a copy?”

“Shifu’s autobiography?” This was indeed something the scripture library wouldn’t have and a book Lu Yang was very tempted by.

“I’ll take one.”

“Fifty contribution points.

Lu Yang clicked his tongue. Fifty contribution points for a book is steep. But given how often I make meritorious contributions, I have plenty of contribution points. This is simply a drop in the bucket.

After transferring the contribution points, the senior male disciple handed him a book with a worn, curled cover.

The Evolution of Prison Conditions in the Great Xia Dynasty Over Two Millennia

“...This is Shifu’s autobiography?”

Lu Yang suddenly recalled that Yun Zhi had once mentioned this book. She said Shifu believes that one should leave their mark on the world, so he wrote this book based on his personal experiences.

Strictly speaking, the contents are far more reliable than his pingshu stories. It can be considered an autobiography.

Lu Yang’s heart ached. Outside, this book can be bought with just loose silver. Yet here in my own sect, it costs fifty contribution points.

To cheat even the Sect Leader!

“Don’t be angry, Acting Sect Leader. I’ll throw in another book for free,” the senior male disciple hastily added with his last shred of conscience.

“What book?”

“The sect leader has enemies everywhere. As his youngest disciple, you’re bound to run into them easily. I’ll give you a book with a list of his enemies. How’s that?”

“That’s more like it.”

Lu Yang took the book. Its title read: List of Great Xia Dynasty’s Fusion cultivators

“...So every Fusion cultivator is Shifu’s enemy?”

The senior male disciple waved his hand and flipped through the pages for Lu Yang. “It’s not that bad. Look, Acting Sect Leader, I’ve marked a few names in red.”

“These people are Shifu’s enemies?”

“Only these people aren’t the sect leader’s enemies.”

Lu Yang felt emotionally exhausted. I’ve become a disciple of a shifu who hasn’t taught me a single day, yet he has enemies all over the world.

“Take care, Acting Sect Leader. Come again!” The senior male disciple warmly saw him off.

“Senior Brother, may I ask if you still have that book from earlier?” Another buyer approached after Lu Yang left.

“Which one?” The senior male disciple squinted at his new customer.

“List of Great Xia Dynasty’s Fusion cultivators. I don’t think I’ve seen it outside.” The buyer looked about Lu Yang’s age.

Under the senior male disciple’s uncomfortable gaze, he bashfully scratched his head. “I’m Zhou Qingshi from the Monolith Sect. I figured if I ever meet a Fusion senior in the future, it’d be impolite not to recognize them, so I wanted to buy the book to study up on them.”

The senior male disciple beamed with joy, his suspicions dispelled. “Ah, I see! It’s fifty thousand spirit stones; take it or leave it.”

“F-five thousand?!” Zhou Qingshi gasped. But upon thinking of the book’s usefulness, he gritted his teeth and bought it.

The senior male disciple shot a meaningful glance at someone nearby, signaling to add Zhou Qingshi to the watchlist of suspicious individuals. He snorted coldly, “A Golden Core cultivator wanting to recognize every Fusion cultivator in Great Xia? Do you think you’re Junior Brother Lu?”

~~~

Lu Yang hadn’t gone far when he spotted a familiar face. “Palace Leader Luo, what are you doing here?”

Luo Hongxia had set up a temporary stall by the roadside. It was technically considered an illegal structure, but no one dared to call her out on it. She sat on a straw mat with a box placed before her.

She glanced up at Lu Yang. “Oh, it’s Sect Leader Lu. I’m fishing.”

“Fishing?” Lu Yang was baffled. There isn’t even water here. What is she fishing with?

Luo Hongxia didn’t explain, simply motioning for him to sit.

Once Lu Yang sat down, she said leisurely, “I assume you’ve heard the pingshu storytelling of Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect: Chronicles of Lu Yang? The contents are remarkably detailed and accurate. I wonder who could’ve spread it?”

Lu Yang could feel his back drenched in cold sweat. He immediately sold out his master. “That was all my shifu’s doing! He asked about the meeting in the name of the sect leader, so I told him what happened.”

“Hmph, I knew it was him!” Luo Hongxia sneered, revealing a vindictive smirk.

Before Lu Yang could say more, Luo Hongxia’s peer, the Sect Leader of the Mystic Sect, approached.

Spotting Luo Hongxia, the Mystic Sect Leader grinned devilishly. “Fellow Daoist Luo, I heard you got beaten up by Sect Leader Lu. Is that true?” A Golden Core cultivator defeating a Fusion cultivator? Anyone with an ass would know there’s more to the story, but that doesn’t stop me from mocking her. Too bad Qiu Jin’an and Yang Ding aren’t here, or I’d mock them too.

Just as Lu Yang was about to explain, Luo Hongxia waved him off. “It’s true. Sect Leader Lu can confirm it.”

Luo Hongxia’s frank admission caught the Mystic Sect Leader off guard. There’s something amiss with her reaction...

Luo Hongxia continued, “This involves ancient secrets. If you’re interested, I can tell you about it.”

“Ancient secrets?” The Mystic Sect Leader’s interest was piqued.

“There are too many people here. Let’s talk inside the box.” Luo Hongxia opened the lid.

The Mystic Sect Leader’s eye twitched, finding the box eerily familiar. “Isn’t that the Light-Retaining Treasure Box from your Moon Laurel Immortal Palace—“

Before he could finish, a blinding light erupted from the box, sucking him inside.

Inside the treasure box, the Mystic Sect Leader heard a cold chuckle behind him.

“Young fellow, I heard you wanted to know how we lost to Lu Yang?”

He turned to see Qiu Jin’an and Yang Ding grinning menacingly, while Master Jiesha wiped blood from his fists with a compassionate expression.

Qiu Jin’an and Yang Ding charged, and soon, the Mystic Sect Leader’s blood-curdling scream echoed through the box.

Outside, Lu Yang gulped and stared mouth agape as Luo Hongxia calmly closed the treasure box.

“This is the fishing I was talking about.”

Chapter 478: In His Embrace, Left and Right

“Hmm, there are quite a lot of people in this box—at least a dozen,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy murmured in surprise.

The moment Luo Hongxia opened the box, she glimpsed a dozen Fusion cultivators and one half-baked Transcendent Tribulation cultivator lying inside, all piled up like a mountain.

The silent old monk was bathed in blood, yet bore not a single wound. Qiu Jin’an and Yang Ding cracked their knuckles, eagerly awaiting their next prey to bite the bait.

“Come, hand over control of your body to this immortal. I shall take a closer look inside.”

Cold sweat poured down Lu Yang’s back as he vehemently protested with his life. “Immortal Fairy, our Dao-Seeking Sect has plenty of activities. There’s no need to fixate on this one. This wastes too much time.”

“Alright then,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy conceded, adopting her loyal minister’s suggestion graciously.

Lu Yang hastily bid goodbye to Luo Hongxia and sped away. Behind him, he heard voices filled with schadenfreude.

“Fellow Daoist Luo, I heard you were beaten by Sect Leader Lu—is it true? Where are Fellow Daoist Qiu and Fellow Daoist Yang...”

Lu Yang quickened his pace.

Soon, an unfamiliar sight captured his attention. “This is...”

Lu Yang saw a small tent packed with cultivators sitting atop a familiar array, clutching torn talismans with vacant stares, their minds clearly wandering elsewhere.

A wooden plaque beside the tent read: Dao-Seeking Sect: Origins

“Acting Sect Leader!” A familiar face popped up from behind the tent. It was Tao Yaoye, whom Lu Yang hadn’t seen in quite some time. Upon noticing him, she broke into a sweet smile.

“Congratulations on your promotion, Senior Brother Lu,” she teased.

Lu Yang showed a wry smile. “Spare me from the teasing, Junior Sister.”

Noting his embarrassment, Tao Yaoye changed topics. “Since many experts and prodigies will gather in the sect for the celebration, I seized the chance to promote the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage.”

Lu Yang nodded, though he had already guessed from the array on the ground.

“How’s the reception?”

“Not bad. It shouldn’t be difficult to promote this in the future.”

The Dreamlike Bubble Mirage was essentially an illusory domain, hardly novel to the cultivators attending the celebration. For them to praise it meant that not only was the concept unique, but the content was also interesting.

“What is the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage about this time?”

“The origins of our Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Lu Yang gaped. “You could dramatize something like our founding ancestor getting lost, asking for directions, and thus establishing the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

“I made slight adjustments.

“The founding ancestor, Innate Daoist Priest, was restless and had a monkey mind. At a loss, his cultivation became mired in stagnation. During meditation, an immortal appeared. When he asked where the pure land of ultimate bliss lay, the immortal told him to journey north, where he would find answers. Along the way, our founding ancestor vanquished demons, witnessed countless injustices in the world, and finally understood that the pure land resided within one’s heart. Thus, he founded the Dao-Seeking Sect in the mountains, symbolizing that amidst the unfairness in life and the obscure immortal path, one should seek the Dao within their heart.”

Lu Yang, “...”

So you only kept the founding ancestor’s name?

Well, at least it makes the Dao-Seeking Sect’s history more dignified. Surely the founding ancestor wouldn’t mind such trivial matters.

“Any challenges with the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage? Do you need me to approve additional funding for you?” Lu Yang flexed his authority.

Tao Yaoye hastily declined.

“Keep up the excellent work then. Jiayou!” He offered a few words of encouragement before leaving.

After passing a few stalls, he found Meng Jingzhou delivering a fervent speech.

“Fellow Daoists! Mortals chase romantic affairs, but for us cultivators, they’ll only squander our time. Bedroom affairs drain our vitality, impair our memory, and scatter our focus, severely hindering our cultivation progress.

“Moreover, why waste time on romantic relationships when you could be in seclusion and cultivating? Look at me! Do you see this refined power? It’s the result of forsaking romantic affairs! As the number one Golden Core cultivator representing the Dao-Seeking Sect, my success speaks for itself!

“You all know Sect Leader Lu, right? Don’t be fooled by how he’s the sect leader now. A few days ago, when we met in his cave abode with only one chair, he insisted I take a seat! Do you know what that means? It means even the sect leader yields his seat to me!”

The cultivators drawn by Meng Jingzhou’s speech gasped softly. This is truly impressive.

“I have sworn an oath to heaven that I shall not marry or engage in romantic affairs until I become an immortal!

“Do you wish to attain achievements like mine?!”

“Yes!” Several shills planted in the crowd shouted enthusiastically.

Meng Jingzhou nodded, visibly pleased. “I have a secret technique here that can eradicate all desires for romantic affairs. Any volunteers want to try it?”

No one responded, but after several seconds, one person raised their hand and stepped forward.

“I’ll give it a try.”

Meng Jingzhou’s face lit up with joy. Someone actually wants to be like me! He eagerly prepared to unleash his Single’s Curse Fist.

Li Haoran stepped onto the platform.

“Senior Brother Meng, could you let me try?”

Meng Jingzhou’s face darkened immediately. If I punch Li Haoran, I’m afraid I’ll have to make another trip to Wilderness Province.

Seeing Meng Jingzhou’s gloomy expression, Li Haoran felt a secret thrill of satisfaction. Back when I hadn’t formed my golden core yet, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou constantly hovered around me, claiming they were Golden Core “experts” and messing with my mental state. Today, I’ve finally gotten my revenge.

“Haoran, you’re here?” A gentle female voice sounded surprised as a fragrant breeze swept by. Su Yiren appeared and clung to Li Haoran’s arm.
