She had searched everywhere before finally finding him here. With the number of people at the celebration, using her spiritual consciousness to scan the crowd would have been impolite, so she had no choice but to search with her own eyes.

Li Haoran’s pupils contracted. He didn’t expect Su Yiren to track him down despite his hiding in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Noticing Li Haoran’s panicked expression, Lu Yang was secretly exhilarated. He was the one who had invited Su Yiren. After all, inviting a secluded Fusion cultivator to the sect’s celebration is perfectly reasonable.

“Mom, what are you doing here?” Qin Yanyan emerged from the crowd, pouting. Embracing each other in broad daylight—how improper!

Mom? The crowd had initially envied Li Haoran for attracting a beauty, but now, they looked at him with strange expressions.

“Is this what they call 'cross-generational friends?’” Man Gu mused. He was one of the planted shills in the audience earlier. He had only heard about Li Haoran’s fiancée and her child after he returned from Wilderness Province.

“Come, there are so many interesting things here. Let’s go explore!” With irresistible strength, Su Yiren dragged Li Haoran away without giving him a chance to refuse.

Qin Yanyan followed beside Li Haoran, shooting warning glances at the couple, though to little effect.

With both mother and daughter in his embrace, left and right, Li Haoran became the envy of passers-by.

Lu Yang watched the scene with immense satisfaction.

“Little Junior Brother.” Yun Zhi’s voice startled Lu Yang.

“Big Senior Sister, what’s the matter?”

Yun Zhi frowned slightly, seeming perplexed. “We invited many Fusion cultivators, but why does it feel like very few actually came?”

Lu Yang inwardly replied, Maybe you should take a look inside that box. They’re all probably lying down and resting.

“No idea.” Lu Yang played dumb. What else could I say? Suggest she charge into the box and go on a rampage?

“Then come with me to look for them.”

Chapter 479: Fox Borrowing the Tiger’s Might

Lu Yang seriously considered selling out Luo Hongxia. Walking alongside Big Senior Sister is super stressful.

With her tall stature, slender figure, peerless beauty, and icy demeanor, Yun Zhi possessed an undeniable allure to all genders. As she strode through the streets, passers-by couldn’t help but turn for a second glance.

Though only outsiders dared to look. After all, who in the Dao-Seeking Sect would dare to look at Big Senior Sister?

At nearly eighteen years old and with a height of 180 centimeters, Lu Yang was half a head taller than Yun Zhi, but he still felt like the shorter one beside her.

“Competitive eating contest! One thousand spirit stones registration fee, ten contestants per round!”

“Competitive eating contest?”[1] Lu Yang was slightly surprised. Cultivators can instantly refine the food they eat. How long would this whole thing work?

Then, he saw the mountain of fasting pills piled on the contest tables.

Lu Yang, “..."

“Pill lottery! One thousand spirit stones or ten contribution points per draw! Guaranteed premium pill every ten draws and cloud-patterned pill every hundred draws!” A senior male disciple from Pill Cauldron Peak enthusiastically hawked, catching Lu Yang’s attention.

Noticing that Yun Zhi seemed interested, he proposed, “I want to try a few draws. Would you like to join me, Big Senior Sister?”

Yun Zhi stared at Lu Yang frostily before agreeing, “Sure.”

Upon spotting the acting sect leader and Big Senior Sister, the senior male disciple from Pill Cauldron Peak was extra cordial. “Big Senior Sister, please sit! Acting Sect Leader, please sit too.”

“We’re here for the lottery.”

The senior male disciple revealed a troubled look. “Lottery? These pills of mine could never meet your esteemed standards...”

“No worries at all. It’s just for fun.” As an expert interpreter of Yun Zhi’s expressions, Lu Yang detected her interest in the activity. Naturally, he couldn’t dampen her enthusiasm.

“Let’s go for ten draws first.” Lu Yang paid a hundred contribution points without so much as a blink.

The senior male disciple produced a large pill furnace with an opening at its base. “Strike it ten times, and ten pills will come out.”

Lu Yang did as instructed. After ten slaps, ten pills tumbled out with a clatter. Nine were shoddy, their surfaces dull and uneven, while only one’s appearance stood out as flawless—the so-called premium pill.

“What kind of pills are these?” Lu Yang was familiar with common pills, but those from Pill Cauldron Peak were beyond his knowledge.

“These nine are Heaven-Earth Creation Pills, forged through the Dao of time and born of serendipity from heaven and earth. Even with my skill, replicating another batch would be near impossible. They are pills full of boundless potential.”

Lu Yang was slightly astonished, seeing the nine inferior pills in a new light.

Yun Zhi lifted her eyes to the senior male disciples and icily uttered three words,” Speak the truth.”

The senior male disciple shuddered, not daring to disobey her. “A while ago, when I was refining pills, I stepped out midway and lost track of time. By the time I returned, the batch was already ruined. Since there would be activities during the celebration, I figured I might as well sell them as lottery prizes.”

“Do you recall that one of my conditions for permitting you to host an activity was that it must not tarnish the sect’s reputation?”

“Rest assured, Big Senior Sister, I’ll tell outsiders that I’m a disciple of the Five-Elements Sect!” He thumped his chest in earnest assurance.

“Hmm?”

“N-n-no! I mean—I’ll pack up and leave right away.”

Yun Zhi raised a hand, stopping him. “No need to rush. I’d like to try my luck as well. Here’s a hundred contribution points; ten draws for me.”

Yun Zhi gave the pill furnace a light tap, imbued with covert force. The impact reverberated inside, striking nine additional times.

That made ten strikes in total.

Ten pills clattered out. Each was full and plump, and three of them were even wreathed in swirling pill-clouds.

Seven premium pills and three cloud-patterned pills.

Statistically, one would need three hundred raws to obtain three cloud-patterned pills.

“Decent luck.” The corners of Yun Zhi’s mouth rose in the faintest arc as she picked up one cloud-patterned pill for herself and handed the rest of the pills to Lu Yang.

She hadn’t used any spells; this was pure luck. And her luck had always been great.

The two continued their stroll, investigating the disappearances of the Fusion cultivators while indulging in the festive activities. Gradually, Lu Yang shed his earlier reserve.

A master and disciple happened to pass by, spotting Lu Yang and Yun Zhi.

“Shifu, Lu Yang’s age and cultivation are similar to mine. How is it that he became acting sect leader and was even qualified to preside over the rites?”

The young prodigy harbored a flicker of envy toward Lu Yang. Despite hailing from the Qi-Commanding Sect, one of the nine S-class sects, and having the sect leader as his shifu, he could attend the Dao-Seeking Sect’s celebration not solely due to his background—it was more so because he was a finalist. Although he and Lu Yang shared similar backgrounds, their standings were poles apart, and he couldn’t get over the disparity.

“Silence!” The Qi-Commanding Sect Leader hissed, admonishing his disciple.

The youth was startled. Shifu has always been amiable with me. Since when has he reprimanded me like this?

The Qi-Commanding Sect Leader couldn’t be bothered with his disciple’s reaction. Cold sweat was already trickling down his back as he stared fixedly at Lu Yang.

Though his focus wasn’t on Lu Yang, but on Yun Zhi beside him.

Although his status couldn’t be compared to the sect leaders of the Five Great Immortal Sects, as the sect leader of an old S-class sect, he still held great prestige and was privy to certain matters.

For instance, he had heard of a Dao-Seeking Sect disciple from centuries ago who single-handedly defeated the sect leaders of four Great Immortal Sects, including the long-renowned Master Jiesha.

Who’s Master Jiesha? He’s a paragon even among Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, surpassing his own sect’s old ancestor! For even Master Jiesha to have lost, one can only imagine that person’s power. And this was centuries ago. How much stronger has that disciple grown since? I don’t even dare to think about it.

“This is truly a main character of the Battle of the Great Era...” With talent so extraordinary, I’m afraid no one will be a match.

“Shifu...” Noticing his master’s terrified gaze and hearing his murmurs, the young prodigy followed the direction of his gaze and saw the high-profile Lu Yang.

Never have I heard Shifu give anyone such a high appraisal. Understanding dawned upon the young prodigy, and he regarded Lu Yang with reverence.

Yun Zhi sensed someone looking at her and glanced back. Recognizing the Qi-Commanding Sect Leader, she didn’t think much of it and turned away.

“Big Senior Sister, is something wrong?” Lu Yang asked, assuming she had discovered something.

Yun Zhi frowned slightly. I’ve indeed discovered something I don’t understand.

“Strange, why does it feel like there are suddenly many unfamiliar Fusion cultivators?”

For this celebration, the Dao-Seeking Sect had widely extended invitations to friends, with numerous Fusion cultivators from all over turning up. However, what perplexed her was how she had barely encountered familiar Fusion cultivators along the way; instead, most of the Fusion cultivators she had crossed paths with were new faces.

A few unfamiliar Fusion cultivators mixed in a crowd of Fusion cultivators would be hard to detect, but if a handful appeared abruptly, it would be glaringly obvious.

1. Fun fact: it’s called a “big stomach king” competition in Chinese. ☜

Chapter 480: Where Exactly Am I?

“Many unfamiliar Fusion cultivators?” Lu Yang’s head swarmed with question marks. He only knew a few Fusion cultivators, mostly those from his sect. Among the external Fusion cultivators invited to the celebration, he only recognized Su Yiren; the others were merely names to him, including the Qi-Commanding Sect Leader, who had just passed by.

His newly acquired List of Great Xia Dynasty’s Fusion cultivators contained profiles and portraits of various Fusion cultivators, but he had been too occupied with strolling the streets to peruse it yet.

Unlike the unreliable Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Yun Zhi’s words carried immense credibility, so Lu Yang had to take them seriously. “Could they be secluded Fusion cultivators?” Su Yiren is a secluded cultivator whose presence is so faint that barely anyone knows her.

Yun Zhi shook her head, dismissing the possibility. “I know most secluded Fusion cultivators. It’s highly improbable that all those I’ve never met would coincidentally gather here.”

Lu Yang frowned in contemplation. This is truly strange. Why have so many Fusion cultivators suddenly appeared? Are they friends or foes?

Foes? Anyone considering invading the Dao-Seeking Sect would need to have been kicked in the head by a donkey to entertain such idiocy.

Friends? Then why did they come uninvited?

Lu Yang couldn’t quite understand these Fusion cultivators’ line of thinking.

Yun Zhi suddenly added, “Not just Fusion cultivators. There are also three or four unfamiliar Transcendent Tribulation cultivators.”

Lu Yang started. This makes the matter much more serious.

“Shall we capture them for questioning?” Lu Yang proposed. At worst, if we catch the wrong people, I’ll apologize as acting sect leader.

“Sure.” Yun Zhi nodded. Lu Yang’s idea perfectly aligns with mine.

A wooden sign obstructed their path. It read: Please hold your breath before proceeding.

“This wooden sign wasn’t here when we passed earlier.” Lu Yang was puzzled. They had nearly completed a full round.

“Sixth Elder erected this sign.” It was clearly not Yun Zhi’s first time encountering a sign like this. She immediately recognized Sixth Elder’s handiwork.

Lu Yang understood. That explains everything. All celebration attendees are either prodigies or cultivation experts. Holding their breath requires just a thought, hardly any effort at all.

Sixth Elder’s arrival caused minimal disruption.

Soon, they saw Sixth Elder at a familiar location—precisely where Luo Hongxia had been fishing.

Luo Hongxia and Sixth Elder were bosom friends, seizing the celebration as an opportunity to converse. Although they couldn’t speak out loud, their relaxed demeanors suggested a pleasant exchange.

Lan Ting and Tao Yaoye followed their respective masters, also communicating with each other through their spiritual consciousness.

“Palace Leader Luo.”

“Fellow Daoist Yun.”

The two bowed in greeting.

“Lu Yang, it’s been a long time since we parted in Qing Province,” Lan Ting greeted warmly.

“Junior Sister Lan Ting, you know Junior Sister Tao?” Lu Yang noticed both of them beaming with beautiful smiles, seeming to get along well. Both have immortal physiques, so they likely have much in common to talk about.

“I’ve long heard from Shifu about Palace Leader Luo taking in a junior sister whose stellar talents rival my own. I finally get to meet her today.” Tao Yaoye took Lan Ting’s hand, subtly shifting her feet to keep a distance between her and Lu Yang.

Lan Ting echoed in a dulcet tone, “I felt an instant connection with Junior Sister Tao, like we’d known each other forever! Junior Sister Tao even wants to use my appearance in the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage.”

Tao Yaoye giggled, gently swaying Lan Ting’s arms. “I’ve always wanted to feature a beautiful cultivator in the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage. The moment I saw you today, Junior Sister Lan, I was amazed by your heaven-defying beauty. I can’t think of anyone more suited for the role.”

“What beauty? You’re far prettier than me, Junior Sister Tao. The only thing I can offer is my cultivation.”

Lu Yang found the atmosphere somewhat peculiar, but he couldn’t put his finger on it, so he decided to keep silent for the time being.

Yun Zhi noticed the Light-Retaining Treasure Box at Luo Hongxia’s feet and inquired, “Palace Leader Luo, may I know the purpose of bringing out the treasure box? Have all your affairs been concluded?”

Luo Hongxia pondered. Almost all the veteran cultivators I know in the cultivation world have been locked up within the box. There’s probably nothing else to do now.

“Yes, my business is concluded.”

“Could you lend it to me then?” The Light-Retaining Treasure Box is perfect for rounding up those unfamiliar Fusion and Transcendent Tribulation cultivators.

“Umm...” Luo Hongxia revealed a troubled expression. Although the Light-Retaining Treasure Box was a supreme treasure of the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace, borrowing supreme treasures between the Five Great Immortal Sects was common, so she hardly had grounds to refuse.

Moreover, she felt guilty. We have imprisoned numerous expert attendees within the treasure box on the Dao-Seeking Sect’s territory. If word gets out, it would affect the Dao-Seeking Sect’s dignity. Besides, with Yun Zhi here, it’s too late to release those people now.

Finding no plausible excuse, she reluctantly handed over the treasure.

“I’ll thank you in advance, Palace Luo Luo.” Yun Zhi bowed, curling a finger to levitate the box. “Little Junior Brother, let’s go.”

Hearing Yun Zhi call him, Lu Yang exhaled in relief, hastily bidding goodbye to the two women before running after her.

~~~

The Moon-Gazing True Lord crouched before a stall, contemplatively examining the wares.

Under the Imperial Preceptor’s orders, he was here to investigate the celebration, stumbling upon an unexpected windfall.

“Interested in this?” The stallkeeper was an elderly man who resembled an old farmer. He wore an unassuming smile as he picked up a book from his display. “I found this old book in a secret domain. It documents the existence of a Heavenly Court Creed member called the ‘Hundred Herbs Heavenly King.’ If it intrigues you, I’ll sell it to you for eight hundred thousand spirit stones!”

The Moon-Gazing True Lord was tempted. The Imperial Preceptor has been troubled by the sudden rise of the Heavenly Court Creed. To think I’ve chanced upon clues about them. This would be a great meritorious contribution.

For a Fusion cultivator, eight hundred thousand spirit stones weren’t considered expensive. Neither was he worried about counterfeits. After all, this is the Dao-Seeking Sect’s territory. How could they sell fakes? That would be a slap to the Dao-Seeking Sect’s face.

“I’ll buy it!” Without another word, the Moon-Gazing True Lord clinked his storage ring against the old man’s, transferring the payment.

Just as he reached for the book, a beam of light enveloped him, sucking him into the treasure box.

Thud. The old book slipped free, falling to the ground.

“Junior Niece Yun, what are you...” Grandpa Ba looked at Yun Zhi with mild astonishment.

“Big Senior Sister plans to question him,” Lu Yang obsequiously answered on her behalf.

~~~

The Moon-Gazing True Lord stared at his surroundings blankly, utterly bewildered about what had happened. I’d just purchased a book a moment ago. How did I end up here?

And why are there so many people here?

He noticed two formidable cultivators slowly approaching him with sinister grins, cracking their knuckles, while a benign-looking elderly monk emanated murderous intent.

Further away lay a group of battered mighty cultivators moaning in pain, their screams making him shudder.

Where exactly am I?

“I don’t recognize him. Who’s this?” Qiu Jin’an hesitated, having never met the Moon-Gazing True Lord.

“Who cares? Since Fellow Daoist Luo let him in, he must be here to mock us. Beating him can’t be wrong!” Yang Ding concluded after a simple analysis.

“Makes sense.”

Chapter 481: Why Are There So Many People in the Treasure Box?

“Grandpa Ba, this old book of yours...” Lu Yang’s expression turned peculiar. Having overheard the conversation earlier, he knew the old book documented information about the Hundred Herbs Heavenly King.

Isn’t the Hundred Herbs Heavenly King you yourself?

So you’re writing your autobiography?

Grandpa Ba wasn’t the least bit embarrassed, admitting in good taste. “After showing our Heavenly Court Creed’s might at the battle of Hanshui City, I figured we could seize this opportunity for some self-promotion.” He assumed the Dou Heavenly Sovereign who appeared at Hanshui City was Yun Zhi’s doing.

“My plan was to accidentally leak some information to the outside world, letting them know how mysterious and powerful our Heavenly Court Creed is.

“See this book? Looks ancient enough, right? I specifically borrowed a magical treasure related to temporal spells from Fifth Elder to age it artificially.” As one of the infamous Dao-Seeking Nine, Grandpa Ba operated meticulously, committing fully to his deceptions.

“Fifth Elder knows temporal spells?” Lu Yang was floored. Among those he knew, only himself, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, and the Epoch Immortal could cast temporal spells. Temporal spells were notoriously difficult to cultivate. Without sufficient comprehension, mastery would be impossible.

“Not at all; Fifth Elder isn’t that capable. He refined it by accident. It’s a cloth mat that alters the time of whatever it wraps. He treasures that thing dearly! If not for Big Bro and me stepping in together, he wouldn’t have lent it!” Grandpa Ba grumbled, displeased with Fifth Elder’s stinginess. He conveniently forgot that when he guarded the herb garden, he was even more miserly than Fifth Elder, acting like it was the end of the world if anyone plucked a herb or two.

“First Elder is in on this too?” How should he put it? Upon hearing the news, Lu Yang was not at all surprised.

In fact, he even found it perfectly natural.

“Come on, let’s capture all the unfamiliar ones.” Yun Zhi paid no mind to Grandpa Ba’s antics. His actions posed no danger, nor would they discredit the Dao-Seeking Sect, fitting the event guidelines.

Moreover, there were more pressing matters at hand. She resolved to capture all the suspects in one sweep and confine them within the treasure box to uncover their true intentions.

“Let’s go!” With Yun Zhi present, Lu Yang found his courage. As the acting agent of the acting sect leader,[1] apprehending a few Fusion cultivators meant nothing.

The senior sister and junior brother duo ran amok around the Dao-Seeking Sect with the treasure box, unceremoniously imprisoning all unfamiliar cultivators. Even Transcendent Tribulation cultivators weren’t exempt.

The Light-Retaining Treasure Box was a supreme treasure passed down a hundred thousand years within the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace. Continuously fortified by generations of sect leaders and grand elders, it was powerful enough to detain even Transcendent Tribulation cultivators—though they could escape easily afterward.

~~~

When the light beam enveloped the Black-White Venerable Lord, he assumed his cover was blown. His gaze turned vicious as he struggled with all his might, yet before the Light-Retaining Treasure Box, he had no choice but to surrender.

Once he was inside, he witnessed Great Xia cultivators beating his subordinates. Although the beatings weren’t harsh, they were extremely humiliating. His subordinates’ desperate struggles only provoked heavier blows in return. Seventeen or eighteen Great Yu Fusion cultivators lay battered on the ground; it was unclear whether they were alive or dead.

“Damn it! As I thought, we’ve been exposed!” Surely this can’t be how the Dao-Seeking Sect treats its guests.

Most of Great Xia’s notable experts are gathered here. Our intelligence must have leaked somehow, allowing the Dao-Seeking Sect to get a hold on us and set this trap with the treasure box to capture us in one fell swoop!

“What a clever scheme.” The Black-White Venerable Lord’s voice turned icy. The Imperial Preceptor was right—the Dao-Seeking Sect is truly an obstacle to Great Yu’s resurgence.

But so what? As an almighty Advanced Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, how could I be confined to this wretched box?

With a flip of his hands, two rotating black and white spheres materialized in his palms, containing boundless destructive power.

Just as Qiu Jin’an and Yang Ding were about to strike, they hastily retreated upon seeing the spheres. This is no Fusion cultivator!

The Black-White Venerable Lord sneered coldly. A few mere Fusion cultivators truly overestimate themselves—how dare they encircle this venerable lord?

Suddenly, his heart tightened in alarm.

An old man approached at a measured pace, brimming with compassion and sorrow for the world, his body aglow with resplendent Buddha light.

Another elder rose from the ground as three thousand li of purple qi surged from the east like silk ribbons, which he effortlessly pinched between his fingers. He was the One-Qi Venerable Lord, the Qi-Commanding Sect’s old ancestor.

Scattered wood pieces floated in the air and assembled into a wooden figure. It was the Puppet Venerable Lord, Grand Elder of the Puppet Master Sect.

One expert after another climbed up from the ground, emitting auras surpassing that of the Fusion Stage.

The Dao-Seeking Sect’s 120,000-year celebration naturally invited Transcendent Tribulation seniors. They had come to mock Master Jiesha, but they were unable to find him, so they sought out Luo Hongxia instead, only to be sucked into the treasure box and thrashed by Master Jiesha himself.

There were so few Transcendent Tribulation cultivators to begin with; the sudden appearance of an unfamiliar one naturally warranted a thorough investigation.

“Attack together!”

The Black-White Venerable Lord’s expression turned into despair. The Dao-Seeking Sect has indeed come prepared!

I’ve fallen into their trap!

~~~

“We’ve captured more or less all the suspects.” After making several rounds, Yun Zhi and Lu Yang only spotted familiar faces outside.

“Let’s go in and interrogate them.” Yun Zhi felt fairly confident. I have captured so many people. Even if one or two don’t speak the truth, surely not all will keep their mouths sealed?

The light beam enveloped the two, transporting them into the treasure box.

“Fellow Daoists, more have arrived! Charge!” Lu Baqian yelled upon seeing newcomers, rallying everyone to attack.

Spearheading the assault, he failed to notice others halting with terrified expressions, as if they were recalling unpleasant memories.

“Y-Yun Zhi?” Lu Baqian finally realized, skidding to a stop.

“Why are there so many people?” Yun Zhi was equally surprised, having expected only unfamiliar cultivators inside the box.

Lu Yang’s gaze darted about furtively, surveying the surroundings.

Unfamiliar cultivators were bound, including the three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators.

One of the three agreed to confess everything truthfully. “I’ll talk, I’ll tell you everything.

“We are Great Yu cultivators following the Imperial Preceptor’s orders to infiltrate the Dao-Seeking Sect during the celebration, assassinate Lu Yang, then annihilate the whole sect.

“Our comrades are all here, captured by you.”

Lu Yang’s expression turned odd, uncertain how to react. It’s somewhat expected that these unfamiliar faces are Great Yu cultivators. But why would they want to kill me for no reason?

Has my identity as the Heavenly Court Creed’s young creed leader been exposed?

“Fellow Daoists, why are you all here?” Yun Zhi was puzzled.

Lu Baqian stepped forth with an expression that read “we anticipated this” and explained, “It’s a long story. We received news about Great Yu cultivators infiltrating the Dao-Seeking Sect, so I gathered all fellow Daoists here to ambush them!”

“Yes yes yes, that’s precisely what happened.”

“We’ve been lying in wait forever before they finally turned up.”

Nods all around corroborated Lu Baqian’s account.

What else could they say? That they had traveled all this way to mock the four leaders of the Great Immortal Sects, only to be “fished” and beaten?

They couldn’t afford to bear such humiliation.

Evidently, they still believed Luo Hongxia had let the Great Yu cultivators in.

Out of respect for seniors, Yun Zhi didn’t expose their lies.

Nor did Qiu Jin’an and the others expose their lies. After all, they had already beaten them up, so they should leave them some dignity.

Hearing their conversation, the Great Yu cultivators were filled with deep regret.

We knew it! This was an ambush!

The Black-White Venerable Lord possessed the highest cultivation and remained indignant. Things have not yet reached a dead end. “So what if you got more people? Once our Imperial Preceptor acts, all of you are finished!”

1. I tried to use “acting” twice here because the term for agent or proxy uses the same first two characters as “acting sect leader.” ☜

Chapter 482: Half-Immortal

(Rewinding time a little...)

“So this is the Dao-Seeking Sect. Truly magnificent.” Ming Tai remarked in awe as he stood before the sect’s entrance.

“Ming Tai, we need to go.” Elder Sikong urged him to keep up.

The two passed through the bamboo forest and crossed streams to reach the heart of the Dao-Seeking Sect—the main venue of the celebration.

The River Spirit peeked his head out, scrutinizing every individual who entered the Dao-Seeking Sect to verify if they were qualified.

“This year’s celebration is livelier than past years,” the River Spirit murmured as prodigies and experts streamed in, his face breaking into a satisfied smile.

He was a stream spirit blessed by heaven and birth and gained a spark of sentience before being enlightened by the Innate Daoist Priest, developing true intelligence. Grateful to the Innate Daoist Priest, he voluntarily became the sect’s guardian spirit, witnessing its ups and downs.

However, the River Spirit didn’t notice a group of uninvited guests slipping in alongside Ming Tai and his shifu. Moving soundlessly through the bamboo forest without leaving any traces, it was as if they were never there; none detected their presence.

The Imperial Preceptor sneered coldly as he bypassed the River Spirit and led his entourage into the Dao-Seeking Sect. “I’ve long heard of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s formidable guardian spirit. I have finally seen it for myself today. It’s a pity you encountered me this time.”

Upon reaching the center of the Dao-Seeking Sect, the Imperial Preceptor dropped his disguise. There are too many cultivators here. Even if we can’t see them, we may bump into them. Continuing to conceal ourselves will instead work against us.

Spotting several Transcendent Tribulation cultivators along the way, the Imperial Preceptor was inwardly glad that he had brought enough people. Otherwise, with me alone, annihilating the Dao-Seeking Sect would genuinely not be that easy.

“Your Excellency, when shall we act?” the Black-White Venerable Lord transmitted an auditory message.

“No rush. The celebration has just started, and the Dao-Seeking Sect is on full alert now. Let’s first investigate thoroughly and scout out how many Fusion and Transcendent Tribulation cultivators are present. After calculating our relative strength, we will decide the optimal moment to strike.

“According to immortal sect standards, every sect has at least one Transcendent Tribulation cultivator and Transcendent Tribulation-equivalent methods. Surely the Dao-Seeking Sect wouldn’t deploy all their combat forces for this celebration. They would require people to guard their treasury and other key areas.

“That River Spirit earlier is likely their Transcendent Tribulation-equivalent method. Their true Transcendent Tribulation cultivators must be elsewhere. When we strike swiftly, they won’t react in time. Even if they rush over, it’ll be too late.”

Dong, dong, dong.

Twelve resonant bell tolls reverberated through the sect, signaling the celebration’s official commencement.

The group fell silent as they noticed their primary target ascend the altar to preside over the ceremonial rites.

“Such old rites. They seem to be derived from ancient times.” The Imperial Preceptor was mildly surprised. As cultivators from the early Great Yu era, only the Great Qian Dynasty separates us from the ancient era. Yet the Dao-Seeking Sect possesses such ancient ceremonial knowledge despite being founded in the late Great Yu era.

“This Dao-Seeking Sect has some substance,” the Black-White Venerable Lord commented impassively. He ranked second only to the Imperial Preceptor in their group.

Even if their rituals are ancient, that doesn’t prove anything; they might have simply copied them from some ancient text. After all, many ancient ruins remain unexplored until now.

“That utterly ordinary brat has repeatedly thwarted our Great Yu’s plans! He should be taught how the character for ‘death’ is written!”

As the ceremony concluded, the Imperial Preceptor’s brow smoothed, a smirk playing at his lips.

“Your Excellency, you...”

The Imperial Preceptor analyzed, “Haven’t you noticed? Compared to during the rites, the number of high-level cultivators has decreased. It looks like I’ve overestimated the Dao-Seeking Sect’s standing in Great Xia.

“These high-level cultivators likely attended the celebration rites out of obligation. Now that the ceremony has ended and the Dao-Seeking Sect’s subsequent segments like the various activities and the youth tournament finals are of no interest to them, they departed.”

The group’s faces lit up with excitement. With fewer high-level cultivators present, their operation would face significantly less resistance and pressure.

“Destiny truly favors Great Yu.” The Imperial Preceptor’s lips rose into a pleasant smile. With such favorable circumstances, the Dao-Seeking Sect’s destruction is inevitable.

He reminded the group, “However, we mustn’t grow complacent yet. Since we can’t use our spiritual consciousness here, fan out and gather intelligence about the sect. Report back to me afterward.” He pointed at the ground beneath his feet. “I’ll wait for you here.”

“Roger.”

The group dispersed, leaving the Imperial Preceptor standing alone.

“They won’t return that soon. I should gather some intelligence about the Dao-Seeking Sect myself as well.” Ever prudent, the Imperial Preceptor wanted to cross-verify the intelligence his subordinates collected with his own findings to ensure its reliability.

“The most bustling area here appears to be the commercial street. I’ll take a look there.” The Imperial Preceptor strolled toward the shopping district.

“This small, unassuming commercial street actually conceals numerous Fusion cultivators.” The Imperial Preceptor narrowed his eyes. With his profound cultivation, he instantly recognized that the seemingly nondescript restaurant owners and waiters were in fact formidable experts who could dominate entire regions in the outside world.

“Fusion cultivators alone won’t stir many waves.” I had once killed six Transcendent Tribulation cultivators alone, though they were all at the Basic Transcendent Tribulation Stage—still, that’s impressive. Fusion cultivators aren’t worth my attention.

“Guest, would you like some barbeque?” The three Alluring Ghosts, Little Five, Little Six, and Little Seven, enthusiastically drew in patrons at the shop entrance, their eye-catching presence impossible to miss.

As business boomed at the barbeque shop, Chefs Liu and Gao activated Three-Heads Six-Arms, drastically boosting their grilling efficiency.

“Make way, make way! Meat delivery coming through!” The owner of a slaughterhouse called out, urging customers to clear a path for him.

Despite preparing ample meat skewers in anticipation, the barbeque shop’s overwhelming popularity still nearly exhausted their supplies.

The Everlasting Immortal lounged with his legs crossed, grinning from ear to ear as he observed the prosperous sight. Today’s sales alone are ten days’ worth!

Lu Yang had temporarily changed the barbeque shop’s name to prevent external cultivators from remembering and spreading word of “One More Barbeque” outside, which would alert the Nine-Netherworlds Creed of a similar shop within the Dao-Seeking Sect and make fooling them more difficult.

Hearing Little Five’s calls, the Imperial Preceptor glanced up and started upon seeing the two barbeque chefs and the slaughterhouse owner.

Three tiger-henchman ghosts at the Fusion Stage? The Dao-Seeking Sect’s Transcendent Tribulation cultivator is here? Only a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator can refine Fusion tiger-henchman ghosts. Since tiger-henchman ghosts typically remain near their creator, the Dao-Seeking Sect’s Transcendent Tribulation cultivator must be hiding within this very shop.

“My luck is pretty good.” The Imperial Preceptor’s smile brimmed with confidence.

I had planned only to gather intelligence, yet I’ve now found a chance to eliminate a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator in advance.

His Incipient Dao Fruit was related to concealment, which was how he could bypass the River Spirit’s detection and lead his group into the Dao-Seeking Sect. This Incipient Dao Fruit can also ensure I get rid of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s Transcendent Tribulation cultivator without alerting anyone.

Entering the barbeque shop, he spotted the carefree Everlasting Immortal.

The Everlasting Immortal saw him too.

“Half-immortal?” the two blurted out at the same time.

Chapter 483: The Imperial Preceptor’s Incipient Dao Fruit

The Imperial Preceptor posed as a Fusion cultivator to outsiders. While this pretense might fool those at the Fusion or Transcendent Tribulation stages, it couldn’t deceive someone at the same cultivation realm.

Had he been serious about his disguise, his deception might have worked even against his peers. But I never imagined I’d encounter a half-immortal powerhouse in the Dao-Seeking Sect!

Tidal waves surged through the Imperial Preceptor’s heart. This is just one of the Five Great Immortal Sects—having a few Transcendent Tribulation cultivators would already be impressive enough. How could they also harbor a half-immortal powerhouse?!

The Everlasting Immortal studied the Imperial Preceptor with a grave expression.

Without special techniques, those at the same cultivation realm couldn’t discern one another’s true cultivation. When two cultivators met and couldn’t see through each other’s cultivation, two possibilities existed—the other party’s cultivation realm either surpassed theirs or stood at the same level.

With immortals being exceedingly rare in the world, the likelihood is minuscule. Therefore, this person must be a half-immortal. Those who possess Incipient Dao Fruits are considered half-immortals.

Is he a friend or a foe?

The Imperial Preceptor steeled his resolve. Although this person is a half-immortal, only his soul is left, which means his combat power is weakened. The best course of action is to end this swiftly.

He decisively produced an octagonal porcelain plate, a half-immortal magical treasure refined over three millennia. Shattering it upon the ground, the fragments formed an isolated space trapping the two of them while his Incipient Dao Fruit’s power cut off the Everlasting Immortal’s connection to the outside world.

~~~

“Business today was not bad. The Immortal should...” the sect leader remarked while skewering meat.

Suddenly, he paused.

Immortal? What immortal?

Scanning the shop, he saw continuous streams of customers, Chefs Liu and Gao overwhelmed with work, creed elders serving dishes and washing plates, and three alluring ghosts drawing in customers outside.

“Old Gao, Old Liu, do you feel like someone’s missing?”

Chefs Liu and Gao looked around blankly. “No? Isn’t everyone here?”

“Is that so?” The creed leader’s brows scrunched up before gradually smoothing.

“I remembered wrong then.”

~~~

“Enemy!”

The Everlasting Immortal was caught off guard when the Imperial Preceptor suddenly confined him in this hastily constructed small space. Judging by his stance, he clearly intends to kill me.

Does he really think I’m a pushover?

As the Everlasting Immortal released a piercing cry, golden filaments of light burst forth and rippled through space like highly suspended heavenly blades during tribulation punishments, severing all foundations of living beings.

“So what if you have heavenly blades? Destiny is on Great Yu’s side! Hundun-Chaos Sacred Lotus!” The Imperial Preceptor hissed.

A lotus shrouded in hundun chaos mist emerged from his forehead, its petals glowing with white halos that flowed like torrents, dissolving the golden threads as they illuminated all directions.

“Hundun-Chaos Sacred Lotus?” The Everlasting Immortal gaped. This is a top-tier Transcendent Tribulation sacred item. The hundun-chaos qi it emits can negate tribulation punishment. It's designed specifically for cultivators breaking through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. Such artifacts exist only in legends; I’ve never heard of anyone actually possessing one.

“You are somewhat knowledgeable. I excavated this from the Extreme North, the source of an entire hundun-chaos mountain range. This is a symbol of destiny’s favor.”

“Destiny my ass! Destiny favors our Everlasting Lineage!”

“The Everlasting Lineage?” The Imperial Preceptor frowned, having never heard of such a lineage before.

“Ignoramus! Our Everlasting Lineage stands supremely powerful, and I rank only third within it!” The Everlasting Immortal sneered coldly.

The Imperial Preceptor was flabbergasted. A half-immortal powerhouse is only third? What unfathomable figures must the top two be?

They must at least be half-immortals!

“Pillar Branding Torture!” The Imperial Preceptor fished out eight copper rods from his storage ring. As he planted them into the ground, they instantly expanded into towering bronze pillars that seemed to prop up the heavens.

“Bind!” The Imperial Preceptor pointed at the Everlasting Immortal, and countless iron chains erupted from the pillars.

The Everlasting Immortal tried to dodge but discovered an inseverable karmic bond had formed between himself and the chains. This is a sure-hit spell!

The chains bound the Everlasting Immortal, suspending him right at the center of the eight copper pillars. Lightning materialized directly above, its violent energy concentrated into a single devastating strike aimed at the Everlasting Immortal.

“Dream Butterfly Technique.” Closing his eyes, the Everlasting Immortal transformed into a swarm of immortal butterflies that slipped through the chains’ fetters before reforming atop the pillars, watching as the lightning bolt struck empty air.

“Ocean-Overturning Seal!” The Imperial Preceptor flipped his palm, unleashing an azure handprint that carried the briny scent of sea winds as it crashed toward the Everlasting Immortal.

During the Great Yu era, the Ocean-Overturning Seal had earned fearsome renown. A Transcendent Tribulation garrison general guarding the border of the East Sea had used it to repel millions of invading sea tribes with a single palm strike, instantly dyeing the ocean crimson.

And that was merely its power when cast by a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. If executed by a half-immortal, its might would increase exponentially.

“Great Carefree Palm!”

The collision between palm and seal produced a heaven-shaking explosion that scattered flesh and eroded souls.

The Imperial Preceptor lost an arm, his immortal blood forming a vast crimson sea as it dripped. With a cold snort, he consumed a great pill crafted from a thousand expensive medicinal ingredients. His injuries healed rapidly, his bones regenerated, his muscles reattached, and his skin closed over as his arm returned to normal.

“Physical wounds may heal quickly, but let me see what you’ll do about your soul injuries!” Observing the Everlasting Immortal’s fractured soul, the Imperial Preceptor was confident of victory and unleashed another Ocean-Overturning Seal to deliver the killing blow.

Soul injuries affected one’s foundation; even great pills could hardly mend them.

“Save your concern. Great Carefree Palm!”

When they exchanged blows, the Imperial Preceptor noticed something amiss. With such soul injuries, he should only be able to bring out seventy to eighty percent of his cultivation. How is he still in peak condition?

What the Imperial Preceptor did not realize was that, with the Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit, the notion of soul injuries simply did not exist—any damage to the soul would heal in an instant.

The two traded hundreds of blows in mere moments, their fierce techniques a blur that ordinary eyes could scarcely track.

The Imperial Preceptor coughed up blood. I’m actually at a disadvantage?! His strength far exceeds my expectations.

As the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s substitute, the Everlasting Immortal had always been formidable, but right from his debut, he was subdued by three venerable beings—Lu Yang, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, and Yun Zhi—and became their captive, stripping him of any chances to demonstrate his true capabilities.

“Very well, very well, I’ve underestimated you.” Realizing he couldn’t gain an advantage in direct combat, the Imperial Preceptor activated his Incipient Dao Fruit to break all karmic ties between himself and the Everlasting Immortal.

He gradually disappeared before the Everlasting Immortal’s eyes, as if he was merging into one with space.

The Everlasting Immortal was alarmed and extended his immortal consciousness, preparing for an attack.

Suddenly, his expression turned vacant.

“What was I doing?”

The Everlasting Immortal frowned. He sensed a gap in his memory; he had forgotten the events that had transpired.

The Imperial Preceptor watched coolly from the shadows, waiting for an opportunity to strike. He cultivated the Karma Dao Fruit, and it was currently at its incipient phase.

The Karma Dao Fruit granted the power to manipulate karma at will. Everything in the world was woven from karma—every meeting, every bond, every enmity was but a thread in this vast karmic web. Severing the karmic ties between people would cause both parties to forget each other.

The River Spirit overlooking the Imperial Preceptor’s group, the Everlasting Creed’s higher-ups forgetting the Everlasting Immortal, and the Everlasting Immortal forgetting the Imperial Preceptor during the Pillar Branding Torture were all effects of the Karma Incipient Dao Fruit.

The Imperial Preceptor had once slain six Transcendent Tribulation cultivators precisely because he made them forget his existence before eliminating them one by one!

Chapter 484: Self-Detonation

The Imperial Preceptor severed all karmic ties between himself and the Everlasting Immortal, making the latter forget his existence and unable to detect him.

“Luna True Fire.” Reciting inwardly, he exhaled a plume of flame specialized in dealing with souls. It could dispel souls and rivalled the Sun True Fire. After refining it, even half-immortals could hardly withstand its power.

The Sun True Fire relentlessly corroded the Everlasting Immortal’s soul like maggots clinging to rotting bones.

“I remember now!” In that moment when the Imperial Preceptor attacked the Everlasting Immortal, the karmic bond between them was reestablished, restoring the Everlasting Immortal’s memories.

Activating the Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit, his soul reconstituted itself, and the Luna True Fire was purged.

“As I thought, the Luna True Fire alone can’t kill you.” Despite anticipating this outcome, the Imperial Preceptor was still alarmed. He couldn’t discern the method his opponent had deployed to recover.

While there were countermeasures to the Luna True Fire, every one of them was troublesome. None was as effortless and straightforward as what the Everlasting Immortal had done.

“An Incipient Dao Fruit method—could it be related to souls?”

This battle proved far more challenging than the Imperial Preceptor had anticipated. Since the Everlasting Immortal was only left with his soul, the Imperial Preceptor assumed he would be an easy opponent. However, the Everlasting Immortal’s soul could reconstitute itself instantly, turning his supposed weakness into the toughest obstacle.

The Everlasting Immortal also mulled over the methods the Imperial Preceptor had displayed. Making me forget his existence—I’ve never heard of a rule-defying spell like this. Could this be the effect of his Incipient Dao Fruit?

Ordinary cultivators relied on spells and physiques. Upon reaching the Fusion and Transcendent Tribulation stages, “Rules” also came into play. “Rules” wielded at these stages easily crush mid- and low-level cultivators, but offer little advantage against peers of the same cultivation realm. Since everyone could use similar rules, no one truly held the upper hand.

However, things became substantially different once a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator condenses an Incipient Dao Fruit, which signified that the cultivator now possessed their unique rules. Every Incipient Dao Fruit functioned differently, and the differences between Dao Fruits, along with one’s comprehension of Dao Fruits, determined the gulf between half-immortals.

In battles between half-immortals, the priority was to figure out what the opponent’s Incipient Dao Fruit was.

“Tribulation-Breaking Everlasting Body!”

A ten-thousand-zhang-tall dharma body rose from the earth, its towering form nearly tearing the fabric of space as it stood between heaven and earth. It held the power to seize stars from the sky and was imbued with the everlasting trait of indestructibility.

The Imperial Preceptor activated his Karma Incipient Dao Fruit again, severing all connections between himself and the Everlasting Immortal.

“Damn it, it’s this trick again...” The Everlasting Immortal gnashed his teeth. If he failed to grasp the underlying principles of this technique, he would perpetually be at a disadvantage.

In a rush, he carved out a series of characters with his power, trying to explain everything that had occurred. Yet under the distortion of the Karma Incipient Dao Fruit, the words soon blurred and became indecipherable.

Mid-explanation, his gaze turned vacant, and he forgot the Imperial Preceptor’s existence once more.

Whoosh! A silver needle materialized from nowhere and traversed space, leaping into the dharma body to strike the Everlasting Immortal squarely in the forehead.

The Everlasting Immortal winced in pain. His body grew frail, and he could no longer maintain his Everlasting Body, causing it to come crashing down.

When the Imperial Preceptor appeared, the Everlasting Immortal regained his memories. “This is a Soul-Breaking Needle forged from the essence of gold and silver.” Every technique the Imperial Preceptor employed targeted the soul.

The Imperial Preceptor sneered. “So what if you know? The Soul-Breaking Needle can tear apart your three ethereal souls and seven corporeal souls. I’d like to see how you plan to reconstitute your soul this time!” That said, a pang of anguish tugged at him. Soul-Breaking Needles are extraordinarily difficult to forge; I’ve only crafted three. I used one during my succession ceremony to demonstrate my might. Now I’m down to the final one. It’s almost impossible to refine more.

The Soul-Breaking Needle’s effect was instantaneous. The Everlasting Immortal felt like his body was being torn asunder as immense energy gushed forth, threatening to burst his body from within.

Ten different souls drifted out; they were the Everlasting Immortal’s three ethereal souls and seven corporeal souls.

The Imperial Preceptor watched intently, wondering which part of his soul the Everlasting Immortal would prioritize in mending.

After three breaths, all ten soul fragments remained separate as they hovered in the air.

The Imperial Preceptor was assured of victory. Looks like scattering the souls was the right decision. He can’t reconstitute them anymore.

“Luna True Fire!” He aimed at one of the Everlasting Immortal’s three ethereal souls, preparing to eliminate them one by one.

Suddenly, this particular soul fragment opened an eye as the Everlasting Immortal’s voice sounded. “Why do I have to reconstitute? Detonate!”

The Imperial Preceptor’s pupils contracted, and a sense of foreboding swelled within him. I’ve never heard of any half-immortal who dares to detonate one of their three souls. Does he not want to live anymore?

The soul fragment exploded and slammed the Imperial Preceptor to the ground, causing the latter’s soul to be affected by the shockwaves.

“Did you think that was all?”

Another ethereal soul detonated, stirring up a soul storm. The gale howled as black mist permeated the skies, rendering all five senses and six perceptions useless in that moment.

“Again!”

Boom!

The third ethereal soul followed suit in an explosion.

The Everlasting Immortal’s cold voice echoed through the blasts of exploding souls. “Our Everlasting Lineage’s first-in-command was the head of the Five Ancient Immortals, unbeatable across the ages. Now reborn, our big boss shall ascend to the peak of Immortal Dao. I’d like to see which of our Dao Fruits is the stronger one!”

“Damn it!” The Imperial Preceptor hastily activated his Karma Incipient Dao Fruit, cutting off their karmic ties.

“Detonate again!” The Everlasting Immortal’s voice now emitted from one of the seven corporeal souls.

A chill ran down the Imperial Preceptor’s spine. I’ve already severed our karmic connections. The Everlasting Immortal shouldn’t remember me. Why is he still attacking?

Before he could derive the reason, a new round of soul explosions had begun.

Boom! Boom! Boom!

The seven corporeal souls detonated in rapid succession. Having never witnessed a scene, the Imperial Preceptor felt like a small boat tossed upon tempestuous waves and on the verge of capsizing any moment.

The Everlasting Immortal had already anticipated this move. Since any clue he attempted to leave behind would be forgotten and erased, he reckoned he might as well not leave behind any information about the Imperial Preceptor.

Before the Imperial Preceptor activated the Karma Incipient Dao Fruit, he left only one instruction for himself.

Self-detonate six out of seven corporeal souls.

After the nine cataclysmic explosions of three ethereal souls and six corporeal souls, the Imperial Preceptor’s soul became unsteady and flickering.

The Imperial Preceptor gasped for air in a sorry state. Despite wearing a precious defensive garment that could withstand even attacks from a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, the nine explosions had reduced it to rags, stripping it of its defensive function.

He glared at the last corporeal soul. With only one remaining, let’s see what you can do!

Then, the Imperial Preceptor watched helplessly as the Everlasting Immortal reconstituted his three ethereal souls and seven corporeal souls, returning to peak condition.

The Imperial Preceptor excelled in battles of attrition, and his signature strategy was first using his Karma Incipient Dao Fruit to make his opponent forget about him before ambushing them. Repeating this several times would exhaust even half-immortals.

But what he didn’t know was that the Everlasting Immortal feared battles of attrition the least!

~~~

The Black-White Venerable Lord surveyed Yun Zhi’s group as if they were already dead. “So what if you got more people? Once our Imperial Preceptor acts, all of you are finished!

“His Excellency possesses the Karma Incipient Dao Fruit and is a half-immortal powerhouse. Release me now, and he might spare your lives!” His tone was laced with threat.

So what if you have more Transcendent Tribulation cultivators? You’re nothing before the Incipient Dao Fruit!

Chapter 485: Is the Method You Mentioned Referring to Yourself?

“A wielder of an Incipient Dao Fruit—a half-immortal?!” Lu Baqian’s scalp prickled at the Black-White Venerable Lord’s threat.

Since stepping into the Transcendent Tribulation realm, he had officially entered its inner circles, gradually learning of the Transcendent Tribulation Stage’s formidable power and future cultivation direction.

For Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, the goal was to condense an Incipient Dao Fruit, which signified that one could control a rule that only belonged to themselves. Even if it was incomplete, it still placed its wielder above all other Transcendent Tribulation cultivators.

If the Black-White Venerable Lord wasn’t bluffing and Great Yu’s Imperial Preceptor was truly a half-immortal, the matter had become far more intractable.

The old ancestors of various S-class sects also realized the thorny problem.

Most Fusion cultivators understood little of Incipient Dao Fruits or half-immortals, but the ashen faces of their Transcendent Tribulation old ancestors were enough for them to recognize that the Imperial Preceptor was a trickier opponent than they had imagined.

Lu Baqian studied Acting Sect Leader Lu Yang’s expression and discovered that the latter seemed utterly unperturbed. Just as I thought, even if this junior has temporarily become the acting sect leader and is being groomed as the next sect leader, he’s still not qualified to access high-level matters such as Incipient Dao Fruits and half-immortals.

No wonder he looks so unruffled.

Meanwhile, Lu Yang was busy dealing with the chattering Everlasting Immortal Fairy to notice Lu Baqian’s gaze.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy scoffed loudly. “So what if he’s a half-immortal? I could crush one with a single punch! Back in ancient times, half-immortals knelt while listening to my lectures!” She didn’t find half-immortals worthy of her attention.

Sitting on a recliner, the hem of her dress fluttered as she swayed, revealing a glimpse of her ankles.

It’s not like half-immortals are immortals. There were so many half-immortals in the ancient era, but didn’t only the five of us become immortals?

“Second-In-Command, do you want an Incipient Dao Fruit? This immortal can give you one.”

“I thought only Transcendent Tribulation cultivators could condense Incipient Dao Fruits?” Lu Yang was surprised. This contradicts the information I’ve learned.

“What are you saying? With me here, I could just force one onto you,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy assured with absolute confidence.

Lu Yang firmly shook his head in refusal. I harbor ambitions of rebellion—I want to establish my own organization and break away from the Everlasting Lineage.

“A half-immortal... That’s indeed a bit troublesome,” Yun Zhi murmured softly. If a half-immortal hiding in the celebration suddenly struck, even subduing them immediately would still result in casualties.

“But there’s no need for concern,” Yun Zhi reassured the crowd. “The Dao-Seeking Sect has methods to counter a half-immortal’s ambush.”

“Does the Dao-Seeking Sect have a half-immortal?” Lu Baqian probed cautiously.

His question was met with Yun Zhi’s icy gaze.

Everyone drew sharp breaths. Judging by her reaction, even if the sect didn’t have a half-immortal, they undoubtedly possessed methods to deal with one.

“Shall we return to our sects and bring back supreme treasures to assist?” Qiu Jin’an asked. The Five Great Immortal Sects stood united in critical times.

Yun Zhi shook her head. “Each supreme treasure has its own purpose. There’s no need to bring them out of your sects recklessly.”

“Alright.”

If Yun Zhi says it’s unnecessary, then it truly is. Qiu Jin’an could tell she wasn’t speaking out of pride but because certainty was in her grasp.

“Then these Great Yu cultivators...”

Yun Zhi replied, “Lock them all in the treasure box for now. Seniors, you have contributed to suppressing them. After the celebration concludes, you shall be rewarded accordingly.” After all, they’ve helped to beat and interrogate them, sparing me much effort.

Everyone’s eyes gleamed with fervor. Attending the Dao-Seeking Sect’s celebration was the right choice—it’s worthwhile despite the beatings we endured.

The Great Yu cultivators themselves were worthless; their true value lay in the intelligence they held, particularly the locations of hidden treasures.

Archaic slumbering cultivators often concealed themselves and their treasures in separate locations. These were their entire fortune—capital for the upcoming Battle of the Great Era.

Among them were numerous extinct natural treasures, their worth beyond measure. Even if several first-class sects divided a single treasure trove, each would emerge with overflowing spoils.

The Dao-Seeking Sect had already reaped the benefits. Through Yun Zhi’s relentless interrogations and torture, she had extracted information on treasure spots from the likes of the Calamity Venerable Lord and the Azure Lightning Venerable Lord.

When Lu Yang returned from Hanshui City, he had met First Elder instead of Dai Bufan in the Great Mission Hall. This was because Yun Zhi had dispatched Dai Bufan to unearth those treasures.

After everyone filed out of the treasure box, they appeared on the bustling streets.

The prodigies here for the competition were left dumbfounded by the sight. These are eminent, untouchable figures. Why are they all coming out of a box?

Though these prodigies were talented, they were still far from earning renown equal to these eminent figures. This was especially so since among these prominent figures were not only Fusion cultivators but also the legendary Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, who were mostly out of the public eye; most cultivators would never meet one in their lifetime. On the other hand, a single misstep on these young prodigies’ paths would cut off their fate of ascending to the peak.

The prodigies whispered excitedly. “Look, isn’t that the One-Qi Venerable Lord from the Qi-Commanding Sect? Our sect once received his aid. We have portraits of him in the sect.”

“And that’s the Puppet Venerable Lord, the strongest Puppet Master! Legends say his puppet strings can manipulate people like marionettes.”

“That’s Sect Leader Lu Baqian, who has recently advanced to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.”

“Oh my Heavens, so many Transcendent Tribulation cultivators!”

“Do you see Sect Leader Lu? He’s actually conversing jovially with these figures as equals without being nervous at all!”

“As expected of the designated successor to the sect leader. If it were me, I’d be so nervous I’d be tongue-tied.”

“You don’t say!”

Lu Yang was naturally not nervous when speaking to Fusion and Transcendent Tribulation cultivators—he wasn’t even nervous when talking to immortals.

The One-Qi Venerable Lord suddenly realized something. “Wait, the treasure box contains three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators and over thirty Fusion cultivators. The treasure box alone can’t restrain them.”

The treasure box shook violently, as if its prisoners were ramming against the sides in a struggle to break free.

“No matter.” Yun Zhi bit her fingertip and traced a blood seal on the treasure box. Instantly, the tremors ceased, leaving the box still again.

The One-Qi Venerable Lord eyed Yun Zhi strangely, recalling the tragic scene of his debate with her. When you said the Dao-Seeking Sect has methods to counter a half-immortal, you weren’t referring to yourself, right?

Yun Zhi returned the treasure box to its owner, Luo Hongxia. “This box now contains three Great Yu Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. Please keep it safe, Palace Leader Luo.”

Luo Hongxia nearly lost her grip on the treasure box.

“Please rest assured, Fellow Daoist Luo,” someone comforted her. “Fellow Daoist Yun has already added a seal to the treasure box. It’ll absolutely be fine.”

“Yes yes yes, even if it isn’t fine, it’s no problem. We’re all here to assist you.”

The crowd pressed close around Luo Hongxia—or more specifically, around the box—wherein lay immeasurable riches.

Having settled matters, Yun Zhi extended her spiritual consciousness. She first scanned the Great Yu cultivators’ rendezvous point but found the Imperial Preceptor absent. A sweep of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s territory likewise yielded nothing.

“Big Senior Sister, have you found Great Yu’s Imperial Preceptor?”

Yun Zhi shook her head regretfully. “No. If he’s still in the sect, there are two possibilities: either his Incipient Dao Fruit is at work, or a temporary pocket space has been carved out.

“I will continue the search. Let the celebration proceed as planned.”

Chapter 487: Those Who Didn’t Break Through Mid-Battle Are Key Surveillance Targets

The Qi Training cultivators who had fought their way to the finals were but a single thought away from the Foundation Establishment Stage. Among them were many who could have broken through a month prior, yet they refused to, suppressing it until this very moment to break through mid-battle.

The first match featured two contenders: Chen Chenxi and Su Youdao.

Chen Chenxi broke through to the Foundation Establishment, believing victory was certain, only to realize his opponent had thought the same.

“These two juniors have some clever ideas, though who will prevail remains to be seen.”

The sect elders whispered among themselves, unable to predict the outcome. Since the two had similar cultivation and foundations, the tide could turn as long as the battle hadn’t concluded.

“Without question, victory will belong to our Heart-Locking disciple.” The Heart-Locking Sect Leader stepped forward to back Chen Chenxi, who hailed from the Heart-Locking Sect.

“Is that so? Are you looking down on our Void-Breaking Sect?” The Void-Breaking Sect Leader narrowed his eyes, backing their sect disciple, Su Youdao.

The Heart-Locking Sect Leader smiled like a gentle spring breeze. “I’m merely stating the facts. How is that looking down on you?”

“Shall we make a wager then?”

“What are the stakes?”

“The ownership of the Great Yu cultivators.”

“Sure, let’s bet then! What’s there to be scared of?!”

The two sect leaders were evenly matched in power, and their sects were of comparable strength. Having been at odds with each other, backing down now would only invite mockery for years to come.

The Qi Training battles proved far fiercer than anticipated. By unofficial counts, ninety-six percent of Great Perfection Qi Training prodigies chose to break through mid-combat, elevating the Qi Training category’s overall combat power.

In the end, victory went to a core disciple of the Qi-Commanding Sect.

“Note every Qi Training contestant who didn’t break through mid-battle. They’re key surveillance targets,” Jiang Qun ordered his subordinates. He suspected these individuals to be archaic cultivators who had dispersed their cultivation to cultivate anew.

“Understood.” The reply was received as an auditory message from the Luoshui Guard hiding in the shadows.

Having undergone special training, the Luoshui Guard excelled in stealth arts and agriculture. Detecting them was nigh impossible, though just yesterday, Jiang Qun and his Luoshui Guard were caught by the River Spirit upon arriving at the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Jiang Qun nodded in satisfaction, not expecting results so swiftly. “Speaking of which, I had hoped to pay my respects to you seniors yesterday but couldn’t locate you. Truly a pity. Where were all of you yesterday?”

He had reached before the celebration began. After the rites, he wanted to seek out the immortal sect leaders and only managed to find Luo Hongxia chatting with Sixth Elder. The two were using their spiritual consciousness to communicate, but Jiang Qun mistook it as they were casting flirtatious glances at each other and didn’t dare to disturb them.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy effortlessly categorized herself as one of the “seniors” and replied, “I received urgent intelligence that Great Yu cultivators plan to infiltrate our Dao-Seeking Sect and sabotage the ceremony.”

Qiu Jin’an seamlessly continued, “After receiving the news from Sect Leader Lu, we devised a plan. We’d conceal ourselves in the treasure box and wait for the Great Yu cultivators to walk into our trap.”

Jiang Qun was baffled. Why didn’t the Luoshui Guard receive this intelligence? And why hide in a treasure box?

Yang Ding added, “You might not be aware, dear nephew, but this treasure box is a supreme treasure of the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace. It possesses the power to beguile the mind, easily bewitching high-level cultivators and luring them into the box.”

“So mystical?” Jiang Qun gasped. I’ve never heard of a supreme treasure with such features. The Five Great Immortal Sects’ waters truly run deep.

“Then why wasn’t I beguiled?”

“Your cultivation is too low.”

Jiang Qun didn’t know what to say to that. “Then where are the Great Yu cultivators now?”

“Inside the treasure box.” Luo Hongxia patted it with an expression of quiet grievance. As the treasure box’s value increased, so did her status. On her way here, everyone urged her to guard it meticulously and shout for help if she encountered any danger; they would rush to her aid immediately.

A human borrowing a box’s power.[1]

“All of them have been caught?” Jiang Qun flushed with shame. He had taken pride in identifying a few suspected archaic cultivators who had dispersed their cultivation to cultivate anew, yet the Dao-Seeking Sect was already close to wiping out Great Yu’s forces.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded steadily. “More or less. Only the Imperial Preceptor remains; he’s supposedly a half-immortal powerhouse. We don’t know where he’s hiding, but Lass Yun has said to let her handle this.”

Jiang Qun had tensed up at hearing that the Imperial Preceptor was a half-immortal, but his heart settled down once he heard Yun Zhi would deal with the matter.

Wait... What did Sect Leader Lu just call Yun Zhi?

Jiang Qun’s heart quivered. No wonder Emperor Father exhorted me to foster good relations with Sect Leader Lu. His relationship with Yun Zhi is much closer than I’d imagined.

Master Jiesha stopped rolling his prayer beads and gazed at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and the others, secretly thankful he was cultivating the Mouth-Shut Chan Meditation.

Amitabha, a monk does not speak falsehoods.

The Basic and Intermediate Foundation Establishment matches also saw a number of prodigies choosing to break through mid-battle, though such cases were much fewer compared to the Qi Training category. After all, not all prodigies had reached Great Perfection.

The two winners hailed from sects that Lu Yang wasn’t familiar with, while the Everlasting Immortal Fairy hadn’t even heard of the sects’ names. One was a second-class sect, and the other was a third-class sect.

The Five Great Immortal Sects didn’t send representatives for the first three categories. Their disciples were minimally at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage. If the immortal sects must participate in the first three categories, they could only send in food ingredients.

“Did you note down those individuals?” Jiang Qun transmitted an auditory message to the unseen Luoshui Guard behind him.

“Yes, all noted.”

“Investigate their backgrounds later.”

Qiu Jin’an sidestepped, addressing the Luoshui Guard behind Jiang Qun kindly, “Fellow Daoist, why not reveal yourself? It’s not like everyone can’t see you ‘hiding’ here.

“And everyone can hear your spiritual consciousness communication too. Why not just speak aloud?”

Qiu Jin’an and the others could hear the exchange between Jiang Qun and the Luoshui Guard as clear as day. So what are you two acting all secretive for?

The Luoshui Guard helplessly showed himself.

Suspicious cultivators were filtered mainly by combat experience. Those seasoned in combat had a high chance of being reforged archaic cultivators, a smaller chance of being an expert pretending to be weak, and an even slimmer chance that their body had been taken over.

The lavish prizes could have tempted experts to feign weakness; the first and third scenarios were considered key surveillance targets.

It wasn’t that Great Xia bore hostility toward archaic cultivators. Dispersing one’s cultivation to cultivate anew wasn’t illegal. At most, they were unregistered individuals. Paying a fine and formally registering themselves would suffice.

However, most archaic cultivators refused to comply with Great Xia’s laws, bringing their old ways of murder and arson into the Great Xia Dynasty. This was why Great Xia had to crack down on these lawless old relics. If archaic cultivators behaved after waking from their slumber, Great Xia wouldn’t bother with them.

Actually, Lu Yang himself was very suspicious. His rich combat experience and ability to beat an old-timer like Master Jiesha defied logic.

But since he was Yun Zhi’s little junior brother, and considering Yun Zhi’s similar feats in the past, no one found anything wrong with Lu Yang.

1. This is a play on the idiom of “a dog relying on their master’s authority,” which means someone borrowing someone else’s authority to commit evil deeds. ☜

Chapter 488: Cultivation Techniques With the Same Names

Zhao Yuan stepped onto the arena stage with a cruel smirk on his lips. He was participating in the Advanced Foundation Establishment category.

Cultivators nowadays have it too easy, untempered by blood and flame. They break down in tears and forfeit the match the moment I display the slightest cruelty.

This was how I’d fought my way through the city-level and provincial-level competitions. Had the referees not intervened in time, those opponents would have died.

But openly killing people in the Dao-Seeking Sect’s territory does pose some difficulty. Forget it, since killing is off the table, I can frighten my opponents out of their wits and cripple their path to growth, eliminating a potential threat in the upcoming Battle of the Great Era.

My opponent this time is some so-called genius of the Dao-Seeking Sect?

It doesn’t matter. Regardless of who it is, all talent and efforts are meaningless in the face of absolute disparity in power.

“Greetings, Fellow Daoist. I am Wei Nanfei of the Dao-Seeking Sect.” Wei Nanfei was Lu Yang’s batchmate. He was poisoned by his stepmother in his childhood and was saved by Dai Bufan when he passed by.

“Rogue cultivator, Zhao Yuan,” Zhao Yuan replied perfunctorily as he sized up his opponent condescendingly.

If not for the tournament finals, this person wouldn’t be qualified to stand on the same stage as me. After all, I was an almighty Apex Fusion cultivator who had dispersed my cultivation to cultivate anew. This time, I’ll definitely climb a level higher and aim straight for the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

“After you, Fellow Daoist Zhao Yuan.”

Zhao Yuan lunged at Wei Nanfei, an emerald long saber materializing in his grip, its hilt adorned with a Dragon-Eye Stone the size of a pigeon’s egg.

“So fast!” Wei Nanfei gasped, barely sidestepping in time.

Zhao Yuan naturally pressed the assault, his wrist flicking to spin the long saber mid-air, cleaving it toward Wei Nanfei’s abdomen.

Clang! Wei Nanfei drew two axes from his waist, crossing them defensively before his stomach to intercept the attack.

~~~

“Why do these axes look so familiar...?” Man Gu mumbled, turning to Li Haoran beside him. “Junior Brother Li, do you recognize these two axes?”

Li Haoran was currently enjoying the happy fate of a man surrounded by several partners, with Su Yiren to his left and Qin Yanyan to his right, though his left hand had been crushed by Su Yiren more than once. Fortunately, his Limb Rebirth allowed his wounds to heal quickly, which he treated as practice for using his golden core.

“These are replicas of the Mountain-Splitting Axe. I forged them for Junior Brother Wei.”

“Mountain-Splitting Axe?” Man Gu found this name familiar too.

Li Haoran elaborated, “It’s one of the River Spirit’s three axes during our sect’s entrance trials—a mortal axe, a spirit artifact Mountain-Splitting Axe, and an immortal artifact Heaven-Splitting Axe. Junior Brother Wei liked the Mountain-Splitting Axe’s design and requested me to craft two.”

Man Gu finally understood.

~~~

Onstage, the battle had reached a climax, Wei Nanfei proving far more troublesome than Zhao Yuan had anticipated.

Although Zhao Yuan was confident of defeating Wei Nanfei, a battle like this wouldn’t cripple Wei Nanfei’s Dao heart. In the past, Zhao Yuan loved pretending to be weak and disguising himself as a genius to crush young prodigies’ Dao hearts.

“Time to use some real methods!” Zhao Yuan’s eyes glinted ruthlessly as he employed his trump card. His blood boiled beneath his flushed skin like a frenzied wild beast. The Dragon-Eye Stone embedded in his hilt emitted an eerie red glow, resembling an ancient dragon opening its eyes with an overwhelmingly oppressive aura.

The long saber came crashing down toward Wei Nanfei’s face. Despite fending it off with his axes, Wei Nanfei’s arms still trembled from the impact, barely withstanding the force.

~~~

“What cultivation technique is this?” Yang Ding’s brow furrowed. The Prison Suppression Sect’s study of cultivation techniques was limited, and he could only recognize that Zhao Yuan had executed a cultivation technique that unleashed a short burst of explosive strength.

“It should be a cultivation technique that burns one lifespan to increase their combat power temporarily,” Luo Hongxia analyzed. Few cultivators in the current era would touch such cultivation techniques.

“It’s the Incinerating Heaven Burning Blood Art,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy casually stated, showcasing her wealth of ancient knowledge.

Burning one’s lifespan to increase combat power was common in ancient times. The Five Ancient Immortals would play around by burning several years of their lifespans when they had nothing to do.

The Epoch Immortal had often burned his lifespan even before becoming an immortal, making him hard to deal with. After all, his original form was the Jianmu World Tree, whose existence spanned the entirety of human history or even longer, its lifespan bordering on the infinite.

“So it’s that one.” Although everyone didn’t know the technique, they had heard of its name before.

“Then it’ll be tough for your Dao-Seeking Sect disciple. I’m afraid he won’t defeat this Zhao Yuan.” The Eldest Prince Jiang Qun knitted his brow.

All signs pointed to Zhao Yuan most likely being an archaic cultivator.

“Worry not. Wei Nanfei also cultivates the Incinerating Heaven Burning Blood Art.”

“Also?” Qiu Jin’an was taken aback. No wonder you could recognize Zhao Yuan’s cultivation technique.

“Mmm, Lass Yun wrote it.”

~~~

Wei Nanfei opened his mouth, seeming like he was about to say something, but Zhao Yuan struck preemptively, preventing Wei Nanfei from speaking.

Want to surrender? No way!

Wei Nanfei helplessly shook his head at his opponent’s unreasonable conduct and could only activate his own cultivation technique.

Zhao Yuan’s power skyrocketed. Although he was still at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, his combat prowess could rival an Advanced Golden Core cultivator.

Kill!

Internally crowing, Zhao Yuan’s momentum rose, while Wei Nanfei deftly evaded his incisive assaults. Zhao Yuan was unrelenting, determined to etch permanent trauma in Wei Nanfei’s heart through this battle.

Kill, kill, kill!

The stronger Zhao Yuan became, the faster his lifespan burned.

“Wait, why is my lifespan burning this quickly?!” Zhao Yuan cried out in alarm. The Incinerating Heaven Burning Blood Art is my life-bound cultivation technique that I’ve practiced for a lifetime. It can’t possibly go wrong.

“It’s you!” Zhao Yuan glared daggers at Wei Nanfei.

Wei Nanfei sighed. “I tried to warn you just now that if you admitted defeat, I wouldn’t have used this move, but you insisted on stopping me from speaking. Since both you and I cultivate the Incinerating Heaven Burning Blood Art, why must we fight to the death?

“Most importantly, you can’t beat me.”

“Are you kidding me?! How is yours considered the Incinerating Heaven Burning Blood Art?!” Zhao Yuan roared in rage. Who are you trying to fool? Who could understand this cultivation technique better than I do? I’ve never heard of a cultivation technique that burns another’s lifespan!

“In any case, Big Senior Sister called this the Incinerating Heaven Burning Blood Art,” Wei Nanfei muttered, equally perplexed. When he was selecting a cultivation technique, the elder had presented two manuals to him, both bearing the name Incinerating Heaven Burning Blood Art.

The sole difference was that the former was excavated from an ancient cave domain, while the latter was written by Yun Zhi.

Wei Nanfei had chosen the latter without hesitation.

Zhao Yuan watched as his lifespan drained away uncontrollably, his attempts to stop it futile. He could only hastily concede defeat.

~~~

“What just happened?” Qiu Jin’an stared at the scene on stage in shock.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s face lit up with an excited glee. Just as she was about to spill Yun Zhi’s secrets and dark past, a teacup appeared beside her hand.

She turned around to see Yun Zhi standing behind her with a frosty demeanor and asking with concern, “Acting Sect Leader, drink some water to soothe your throat.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy broke out in a cold sweat and dared not speak further.

Yang Ding recalled certain rumors about how every disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect had to complete two missions annually, and how Yun Zhi had fulfilled hers by lying that she had discovered archaic cultivation techniques in cave domains. In reality, she had written all of those solely based on their names.

Furthermore, Yun Zhi’s versions of cultivation techniques with the same names always far surpassed the originals.
