Chapter 489: The Diabolic Path Doesn’t Have Such Cultivation Techniques

Cultivation techniques at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage were a highlight. Disciples from immortal sects clashed with opponents suspected to be archaic cultivators who had dispersed their cultivation to start anew, with both parties showcasing their mighty abilities. Wei Nanfei, in particular, stood out among immortal sect disciples; everyone was afraid of facing him in battle.

A Foundation Establishment cultivator only had a limited number of years to live. One had to be careful not to burn through their entire lifespan in a single match.

“Fortunately, the competition has age restrictions,” Meng Jingzhou remarked below the stage. The Dao-Seeking Sect has worthy successors.

“Why do you say that?”

“If a bunch of veteran Foundation Establishment cultivators were allowed on stage, wouldn’t they have to surrender on the spot?”

Bai Ming nodded. Indeed, even if the lifespans of the old Foundation Establishment cultivators are added together, it still wouldn’t match mine. Wei Nanfei’s cultivation technique inherently counters veteran cultivators.

“The cultivation technique does have its flaws—it can’t burn the lifespan of cultivators stronger than the user. But in this match, that’s hardly an issue.” Meng Jingzhou had some understanding of Wei Nanfei’s cultivation technique.

The Dao-Seeking Sect encouraged transparency in cultivation techniques, where disciples could freely research and discuss them together to promote mutual improvement. If someone didn’t disclose their cultivation techniques, it was usually out of embarrassment—for instance, when the cultivation technique left them unable to approach women.

~~~

“Is this a variant of the Incinerating Heaven Burning Blood Art? Interesting. It’s a pity I’ve cultivated the Turtle Breathing Technique. It seals off my lifespan and happens to counter him.”

Below the arena stage, a towering cultivator slowly opened his eyes. His gaze was frosty as ice, and a confident smirk played on his lips. To others, Wei Nanfei is a formidable opponent, but to me, he’s nothing special.

He’s merely been lucky to advance to the finals. If we had crossed paths earlier, how would he have gotten the chance to be here for the finals?

With that, he turned and left.

He was a cultivator belonging to the Basic Golden Core category.

~~~

“Burning others’ lifespans... That’s quite the idea. He’s got potential. Had he been born in my era, I might’ve taken him as a disciple. What a shame.”

Below the arena stage, a cultivator cloaked in black murmured to himself, pushing back his hood to reveal a face streaked with scars—slash marks, burns, frostbites—each a testament to his battles waged on the boundary between life and death.

These battles had honed his combat instincts to a powerful level, making it hard for him to find an equal among peers at the same cultivation realm.

With that, he turned and left.

He was a cultivator belonging to the Intermediate Golden Core category.

~~~

“Wei Nanfei, huh? Quite interesting. The Dao-Seeking Sect’s prodigies are really not to be looked down upon. But as for the burning of lifespan? That’s hardly a threat.”

Below the arena stage, a cultivator as lanky as a monkey narrowed his eyes, dissecting Wei Nanfei’s match frame by frame in his mind and strategizing countermeasures.

Having experienced numerous competitions, his combat experience was vast; he had already devised a countermeasure.

Then, he stepped onto the stage.

He was the referee.

~~~

Fang Sheng stood on the arena stage, waiting for Wei Nanfei to step onto the stage.

Soon, Wei Nanfei ascended the stage, trailed by a procession of chickens, ducks, and pigs.

Fang Sheng didn’t dare to be careless. These are no ordinary livestock—they possess cultivation.

Looks like Wei Nanfei is also a Beast Tamer.

“Wei Nanfei, Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“Fang Sheng, Changes Sect.”[1]

The two took their stances, the battle about to break out at any moment.

Fang Sheng had studied Wei Nanfei’s combat style, just as Wei Nanfei had analyzed Fang Sheng’s. Both concluded the other party was a formidable foe and that there was no room for complacency.

Hence, Wei Nanfei mobilized his full power from the outset. “Incinerating Heaven Burning Blood Art!”

Fang Sheng’s lips curled into a cold smirk. “Did you think I came unprepared? I’m not afraid to tell you that I consumed a pill before stepping up here—one that counters your cultivation technique. You can’t burn my lifespan!”

He possessed a few specially concocted pills, designed by a Pill Dao master to seal off his lifespan temporarily. It was originally meant to safeguard him from accidents during his slumber.

I didn’t expect it to come into use here.

Anticipating Wei Nanfei to have a moment of daze upon learning of this matter, Fang Sheng seized the opportunity to close the distance. “Spear Sweeps Eight Directions!”

Wei Nanfei’s axes gleamed with dazzling rays as he moved with lightning speed, his eyes sparkling. There was not a single bit of hesitation as he faced the attack head-on.

As their weapons clashed, a grating hum pierced the air.

“How’s that possible? Why do you still have such power?!” Fang Sheng was shocked and staggered backward, driving his spear into the ground to disperse the incoming force.

According to his observation of past matches, Fang Sheng could discern that Wei Nanfei could burn others’ lifespans to boost his own cultivation realm. This should be a power that Wei Nanfei can only wield when using his cultivation technique!

But my lifespan hasn’t been burned at all.

Wei Nanfei sneered. “Who said I was burning your lifespan? You think I bought all those ingredients from Hundred Fragrance Restaurant for nothing?”

Realization seemed to strike Fang Sheng, and his peripheral vision caught the lifeless forms of the aged livestock.

I’ve miscalculated!

In a world teeming with talents and heroes, Wei Nanfei had long predicted others would conceive of methods to counter him. Rather than let his opponents counter him, he figured he should switch his combat method first.

“Force Cleaves the Firmament!” Wei Nanfei swung his twin axes, his muscles bulging as he mustered his strength. He hacked at Fang Sheng until he was forced to backpedal repeatedly, soon reaching the edge of the arena.

This is bad! If I continue retreating, I’ll lose!

“Don’t think flashy cheap tricks can win you the match! True strength is everything!” Fang Sheng roared. A mist of spirit energy rose from his dantian, condensing into a full, plump golden core.

A mid-battle breakthrough!

According to his plan, breaking through half a month later would have been ideal. But now that things have come to this, I have no choice if I don’t want to lose.

I’m an almighty Apex Fusion cultivator who dispersed my cultivation to cultivate anew. How could I lose to a mere Foundation Establishment brat? My pride won’t allow this!

Besides, the tournament’s rewards will compensate for my premature breakthrough.

Fang Sheng retaliated with the full might of a Golden Core cultivator. Even if Wei Nanfei was unbeatable at his cultivation realm, he was now facing an opponent a major realm above him.

“Fighting a Golden Core cultivator is somewhat tough... But acting all proud over just a breakthrough? As if you’re the only one who could break through to the Golden Core Stage.” Wei Nanfei scoffed. If not for participating in this tournament, I could’ve broken through half a month ago.

“Condense.” Heat flared in his dantian as a warm energy flowed through him. A golden core, bright as the blazing sun, rose within.

Under Fang Sheng’s stunned gaze, Wei Nanfei flashed an amiable smile. “There, now we’re both at the Golden Core Stage.

“My golden core may not match up to Senior Brother Lu Yang’s, but it’s more than enough to deal with you!” He brought out various livestock—purchased from the Hundred Fragrance Restaurant—from his specially refined storage ring and began burning their lifespans.

Unsurprisingly, Wei Nanfei won.

~~~

On the judges’ platform, Qiu Jin’an rubbed his temples in pain.

He couldn’t help but feel that these archaic cultivators weren’t as powerful as he had imagined. They’re seasoned in combat, but they lack adaptability.

Isn’t burning livestock’s lifespan to boost your cultivation realm something one can easily think of? Why did it not cross their minds?

“Burning others’ lifespan to enhance one’s combat power—why does it sound an awful lot like a diabolic cultivation technique?” Yang Ding muttered, though the Everlasting Immortal Fairy still heard him.

As the acting sect leader, I have to protect the sect’s dignity.

“You can’t say that. Our Dao-Seeking Sect is a righteous sect certified by the court. How could we have diabolic cultivation techniques?

“Besides, the diabolic path doesn’t have such cultivation techniques.”

1. The sect’s name is likely inspired by the Yijing or Book of Changes. ☜

Chapter 490: Ming Tai’s Origins

“Basic Golden Core category, first round, the winner is the rogue cultivator, Zhuang Xuan,” the gaunt referee announced the conclusion of the first round of matches with an unexpected victor, whose name had been unheard of before this.

Regardless of whether one was a disciple of a major or minor sect, they received their cultivation resources from their respective sects.

On the other hand, rogue cultivators were different. They lacked cultivation resources—wealth, companions, techniques, and land. Without the guidance of elders, even the slightest mishap in their cultivation could lead them astray with irreversible consequences.

Thus, the cultivation realm and quality of a rogue cultivator far paled in comparison to that of cultivators from sects. To defeat numerous sect cultivators and stand out from the city-level and provincial-level competitions to reach the Dao-Seeking Sect, one could only imagine the difficulty of such a feat.

“Note him down. He’s a prime suspect,” Jiang Qun instructed the Luoshui guard.

As he flipped through Zhuang Xuan’s previous battle records, it was evident the man had blazed his way to the finals. In every match, he had ended the fight within five moves. Even in the first match of the finals, he had defeated his opponent in just five moves.

Terrifyingly strong.

“Understood.” The Luoshui guard had already filled most of the page with names.

“Next time we compete, I’ll definitely win!” The defeated cultivator brimmed with vigor, showing no signs of dejection despite his loss to Zhuang Xuan. Instead, he challenged him to a rematch another time.

Zhuang Xuan cast an icy glance at his opponent and softly uttered, “Boring.”

“You!” The defeated cultivator’s expression shifted, finding Zhuang Xuan overly arrogant.

Zhuang Xuan ignored his reaction and leaped off the stage, his eyelids drooping as he let out a bored yawn. If not for the tournament’s generous rewards, I wouldn’t have bothered humoring these children in playing house.

Winning feels meaningless; there’s simply no challenge.

Soon, Zhuang Xuan faced his second opponent, a courteous cultivator with a sword. His demeanor suggested he was a Confucian cultivator who cultivated the Gentleman Sword.

“I am Ming Tai from the Sword Tower. I look forward to your guidance.” Ming Tai grasped his sword with both hands, blade pointing downward, and bowed respectfully with a bashful smile.

Zhuang Xuan remained as disinterested as ever, looking half-asleep.

He didn’t have favorable impressions of polite cultivators. They have no bloodlust and fire in them. Playful sparring might suit them, but once they step onto the battlefield in a true life-or-death struggle, these people are always the first to die.

He had clashed with Confucian cultivators at the Fusion Stage several times before. He believed such cultivators belonged in court to debate about semantics and had no place on the front lines of war.

Suddenly, a flash of azure light sliced through the air.

Zhuang Xuan instinctively jerked his head back, though the light ray’s edge still grazed his neck. A cold breeze brushed past his skin, and a stinging sensation at his neck followed as a thin cut appeared, blood soon seeping out.

“He honed his mastery of the sword to such a degree at his cultivation stage?!” a participant gasped.

Some hadn’t watched Ming Tai’s first match, but witnessing his move now, they realized he was a formidable foe.

“A Basic Golden Core cultivator already possessing such mastery of Sword Dao? He can rival the old Taciturn scoundrel,” an elder of the cultivation world remarked. The Central Continent hasn’t seen a Sword Dao genius comparable to the old Taciturn scoundrel in ages.

”This Zhuang Xuan is also not simple. He hasn’t used his full power yet.” Another elder of the cultivation world nodded. Truly the Battle of the Great Era. The first few categories of matches could already broaden one’s horizons, but now, in the Basic Golden Core category, various prodigies are shining even brighter.

“This will be a clash between tigers and dragons,” a towering cultivator commented, his gaze as cold as glacial ice.

Having lost to Ming Tai in the first round, he had studied Zhuang Xuan’s combat style. If these two meet, it will no doubt ignite fierce sparks.

“What a pity, my Turtle Breathing Technique never got a chance to come into use!”

On the arena stage, a jade pendant slipped from Zhuang Xuan’s neck. The earlier slash from the azure light hadn’t just left a thin wound on his neck; it had also severed the jade pendant’s string.

Zhuang Xuan bent down, carefully retrieving the jade pendant. His voice was now low and raspy, carrying none of its former lethargy.

“Fellow Daoist Zhuang Xuan, are you finally taking this seriously?” Ming Tai’s eyes burned with eagerness as he stared at Zhuang Xuan.

Zhuang Xuan didn’t answer, speaking to himself or perhaps to Ming Tai.

“This jade pendant holds special significance. My shifu left it to me on his deathbed. He told me I was an orphan and that I was clutching it in my hand when he found me. It’s the only clue to my parents. I’ve kept it close all these years, never letting it touch the ground.

“You’re the first to make it fall to the ground.

“Do you know that a dragon has its reverse scale[1]; touch it...and you will die!”

A bestial snarl erupted from Zhuang Xuan’s throat, sending chills down people’s spines. His head snapped up, eyes locking onto Ming Tai with the gaze of a demon beast that had gone insane.

“His momentum...” The Qi-Commanding Sect Leader was slightly astonished. Zhuang Xuan’s current aura almost rivaled that of a Basic Nascent Soul cultivator. And yet, he was only at the Basic Golden Core Stage.

Zhuang Xuan lunged at Ming Tai in a frenzy, his body emanating a frightening black energy. People couldn’t identify the cultivation technique, but one thing was certain—no one wished to become his opponent.

Boom! A blast of sword qi hurled Zhuang Xuan off the stage.

“Whew, that was close. So close.” Ming Tai patted his chest, still shaken.

Once he regained his composure, he approached the stage’s edge, gazing down at the dazed Zhuang Xuan and bowing with his sword. “A strong momentum doesn’t equate to strong cultivation. I have learned much.”

Zhuang Xuan blinked, yet to process what had just happened. Shouldn’t I have been the one to lose control and rip Ming Tai apart? How did I end up losing?

~~~

“How did your Sword Tower recruit such a disciple?” Lu Baqian stared at Elder Sikong in shock.

Others might have missed it, but I, an almighty Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, saw it clearly. That sword strike encompassed the cosmos and the extreme changes of the universe. It looked nothing like what a Golden Core cultivator should have been capable of. Even Nascent Soul cultivators who could perform that slash would be hailed as a genius.

Elder Sikong relished the sight of the ever-boastful Lu Baqian wearing such an expression. It’s even more refreshing than eating ice cubes in summer. “Hehe, I’ve already said so. Ming Tai is the only one in our Sword Tower to have obtained the Supreme Lord’s legacy.”

~~~

“That was a fine sword strike. My Slashing Word Mantra is roughly at this level.” Confined in his mental space, Lu Yang peered through the small window left by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to observe the battle.

Ming Tai’s moves had truly been unexpected. If not for Ming Tai, I might have forgotten I’m a sword cultivator myself.

“This fellow doesn’t seem human,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy mused, eyeing Ming Tai briefly before losing interest.

Although she wasn’t interested, Lu Yang was, and he hastily followed up on what she meant.

“He seems like a sword spirit that has developed true spirit sentience and become a living being. Then, someone crafted a physical body for him, inviting him to inhabit it, fusing spirit and flesh to make him truly human.”

Lu Yang mulled over it. He had access to all the tournament participants’ records, which stated Ming Tai had earned the recognition of the Sword Tower’s Supreme Lord and inherited his legacy.

“Could he be the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s sword spirit?”

If so, everything falls into place.

1. The dragon’s reverse scale or inverted scale is something like a person’s taboo that must never be triggered, else they will fly into a rage. ☜

Chapter 491: Methods to Use the Rebirth Golden Core

“Can sword spirits also become souls?”

“Most sword spirits can’t, but the Sword Tower’s Supreme Lord is different. As a half-immortal, his sword spirit must have slain enemies for years and been steeped in immortal blood, thus possessing the spirit charm of Immortal Dao.

“Take that Qilin Immortality Herb as an example. Didn’t it gain spirit sentience and become a demon spirit after it was soaked in the Qilin Immortal’s blood?”

As the duo—one human and one ghost—rose in authority and clawed their way up to the position of acting sect leader, they uncovered some secrets, such as details about the Sword Tower’s Supreme Lord.

The title of “Supreme Lord” was reserved for half-immortals; the Everlasting Immortal could be called the Everlasting Supreme Lord.

No one knew what Incipient Dao Fruit the Sword Tower’s Supreme Lord possessed. The only certain information was that he had attempted to perfect the Incipient Dao Fruit and seized the opportunity to become an immortal, only to end in failure and be reduced to ashes.

With no suitable successor to inherit his legacy and the repeated setbacks of the Sword Tower, the Sword Tower fell to its current status as a first-class sect. If Ming Tai was indeed the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s sword spirit, it made sense for him to inherit the legacy.

“You should know that the higher one’s cultivation, the harder it is to conceive offspring, and it’s all the more so for half-immortal Dao partners.”

Lu Yang nodded. He was aware of this. Most of the current imperial princes and princesses were born when the Xia Emperor was young. It wasn’t that the Xia Emperor was too old and feeble to procreate now, but his cultivation had simply become too high to produce offspring.

Of course, it’s also possible he really can’t procreate anymore.

“Some half-immortal couples resort to blending their immortal blood. With luck, something akin to a sword spirit will be born from the blood mixture. Given time, it would develop sentience and become a soul—in other words, their child.

“That’s why high-level cultivators must fight with extra caution and avoid drawing blood.”

“Why?”

“Just imagine two half-immortals in battle, fighting tooth and nail, spilling blood, sweat, and tears, yet still locked in a stalemate. Finally, they agree to resume fighting the next day.

“Once the next day arrives, lo and behold, their blood has become a demon spirit. Now, the two have a child together. What do you think they should do then?”

Lu Yang, “...”

That makes a lot of sense.

“In ancient times, half-immortal battles were fought with restraint and a sense of propriety. Bloodshed was avoided whenever possible. If blood was spilled, it had to be cleaned immediately after the battle to prevent complications. Otherwise, accountability would become messy.

“Moreover, this procreation method was controversial. For instance, the Qilin Immortal’s family adamantly refused to adopt it.”

~~~

On the arena stage, the two combatants stood ready.

“Li Haoran, Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“Zhao Po, Corpse-Driving Sect.”

They exchanged bows with proper etiquette.

“Senior Brother Li, after you,” Zhao Po said with a grave expression. I’m up against a senior brother from the Dao-Seeking Sect; I mustn’t be careless.

After all, I’ve witnessed Lu Yang’s terrifying prowess firsthand. And Wei Nanfei, the lifespan driver...

But I’m no longer the same person. After receiving pointers from the sect leader, my power has soared, and my walking corpse has undergone a metamorphosis.

“After you, Junior Brother Zhao.”

Zhao Po didn’t turn down the gesture, attacking simultaneously with his walking corpse.

The walking corpse was like tempered steel and iron bones, unafraid of pain. It charged at Li Haoran like a moving mountain range.

Li Haoran clapped his hands together and repelled the walking corpse, but the impact also left his arms numb.

Before Li Haoran’s pain could be alleviated, he saw Zhao Po brandish a Copper Coin Sword. Every coin lit up, igniting a golden aura that shot to the sky—part sword qi and part flame—its offensive power astounding.

“Cleave!” The golden aura condensed into a mass of sword qi that pierced the air with a thunderous crackle, dazzling like meteor trails.

Li Haoran valiantly met the Copper Coin Sword head-on with a single palm.

The moment they collided, something unusual occurred. A thin membrane appeared to separate the palm and golden sword qi. It was composed of countless irregular fragments, light and delicate yet hard to pierce, warding off the golden sword qi attack.

“Refined space?” Luo Hongxia recognized Li Haoran’s artifact-refining methods.

Brilliant artifact-refining masters could refine space for their own use, integrating it into their weapons, but this was far beyond the capabilities of a Basic Golden Core cultivator.

Fifth Elder watched Li Haoran with a pleased smile that almost turned his eyes into crescents.

Li Haoran hadn’t advanced his cultivation recently because he had been comprehending this artifact-refining method.

Zhao Po was less familiar with the world and hadn’t seen such methods, faltering momentarily.

But Li Haroan gave him no chance to react. He shattered the spatial membrane, then flicked his two fingers on the Copper Coin Sword with a hidden rhythm. Every tap weakened the Copper Coin Sword’s power. After three consecutive strikes, the sword qi’s radiance dimmed entirely.

Zhao Po’s pupils contracted. I can’t activate the Copper Coin Sword anymore?!

“Junior Brother Zhao, this Copper Coin Sword is newly acquired, right? It hasn’t been fully refined yet. Remember to use a weapon that truly belongs to you the next time you fight,” Li Haoran said leisurely, temporarily severing the connection between the Copper Coin Sword and Zhao Po.

This was also a useful method employed by artifact-refining masters.

Zhao Po gritted this time. Desperate times call for desperate measures—I have to use risky methods.

He bit his wrist and poured his blood over the walking corpse. The walking corpse’s pores stretched open, absorbing the blood. Beneath its pallid skin, blood now flowed, as if the walking corpse had come back to life.

“Attack together!” The walking corpse charged like a raging elephant, while Zhao Po soared like a diving hawk.

Normally, two fighters teaming up against one would lack coordination due to inexperience. But it was different for Zhao Po and his walking corpse. He shared a close bond with his walking corpse, resulting in flawless synergy between them.

The walking corpse fought like a Martial Dao master. Each punch and kick was packed with fearsome strength, resembling the swing of a saber and the crash of an axe. Every blow carried deadly peril, like bolts of lightning exploding across the arena.

Meanwhile, Zhao Po was midair as he wielded a peachwood sword and talismans, targeting gaps in Li Haoran’s defenses.

The duo overwhelmed Li Haoran, driving him into a disadvantageous position.

Zhao Po and his walking corpse hit Li Haoran’s chest simultaneously, sending him hurtling backward. He panted heavily. This kind of assault drains me and the walking corpse immensely. I need to end the fight swiftly.

Clap, clap, clap. Lone applause rang out from below the stage. Be it Zhao Po or the audience below the stage, they turned to the voice in bewilderment.

The person clapping looked exactly the same as Li Haoran.

It was actually Li Haoran!

But how could that be? Wasn’t Li Haroan still on the stage?”

Only the sect leaders and elders of major factions smiled, as if they had seen through something.

“Junior Brother Zhao, well fought. As I thought, a mere clone isn’t enough to defeat you.”

“Clone?” Zhao Po frowned, still not understanding how Li Haroan had done it. Is it like Senior Brother Lu Yang’s wooden clones?

Li Haoran explained unhurriedly, “My golden core is called the Rebirth Core. As the name suggests, it can regenerate severed limbs. A head grows if decapitated, and legs grow if amputated.

“Then if I chop off every body part, wouldn’t they assemble into a new complete body?” Zhao Po’s pupils shrank. A method like this exists?!

“Afterward, I consulted Senior Brother Man about Corpse-Driving Techniques. I could use the Corpse-Driving Technique to control my ‘corpse.’ Although my combat power can’t compare to my main body, it makes up seventy to eighty percent.”

A smile as gentle as the spring breeze played at Li Haoran’s lips. “Since my clone can’t defeat you, what will you do if both my clone and I strike together?”

Zhao Po’s heart sank. The clone alone is already so much trouble. If we ask Senior Brother Li’s main body to step in, can we still fight?

Other Basic Golden Core cultivators shifted uneasily. The combat prowess Li Haoran had displayed was undeniable and intractable. And this was just the clone. With the clone and main body joining forces, who could stand against them?

The gaunt referee glanced at Li Haoran below the stage and announced the competition results. “As per tournament rules, if one party steps off the stage after the match begins, they’re considered to have lost.”

“Zhao Po wins.”

Li Haoran’s smile froze.

Chapter 492: The Heavenly Court Creed Makes Its Entrance

As a sword spirit who had gained sentience, Ming Tai’s talent in Sword Dao rivaled Lu Yang’s. In the Basic Golden Core category, he swept through the matches with invincible dominance, with only prodigies from immortal sect disciples and suspected reforged cultivators managing to push him into tough battles. However, even these prodigies fell before his exquisite swordsmanship. Although his cultivation was still low, he already possessed a faint hint of the might of “One Sword Breaks All Spells.”

Winner of the Basic Golden Core category: Ming Tai.

Standing on the arena stage, his hand was raised to his chest level as he bashfully waved at Elder Sikong. Bathed in sunlight, his figure gleamed as though he was cast from gold.

“Looking at Ming Tai is like looking at Lu Yang’s shadow,” Meng Jingzhou remarked, the rim of his eyes red as he reminisced about their glorious days with palpable sorrow—a testament to the deep bond between Lu Yang and him.

“What a pity. Lu Yang was such a good man, how could he just...” Meng Jingzhou choked up, weeping uncontrollably.

Bai Ming was rendered speechless for a while until he kindly offered, “How about you keep crying, and I’ll go up the stage for you instead?” The Intermediate Golden Core matches had already begun, and Meng Jingzhou was the first contestant.

Wiping away his tears, Meng Jingzhou steeled himself. “No need. Since Lu Yang can’t compete, I’ll carry on his will and press forward undaunted. If his spirit is watching from the heavens, I believe he’d have wanted this.” With that, he strode onto the stage, every step bearing immense weight as though he shouldered a solemn duty.

At the judges’ stands, Lu Yang pondered whether he could abuse his authority to declare Meng Jingzhou instantly defeated.

“Meng Jingzhou, Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“Ye Mengyin, Allure Sect.”

Meng Jingzhou’s opponent, Ye Mengyin, was a true lineage disciple of the Allure Sect.

Ye Mengyin was clad in pristine, flowing robes. Her translucent skin sparkled like snow, and her aura resembled an immortal spirit’s. She was a fairy-like beauty chased by countless admirers in the outside world.

Her allure arts were the cream of the crop among her peers in the sect. A mere smile or frown of hers could stir the deepest desires in a man’s heart. Even women with weak resolve might succumb.

As she introduced herself, her coquettish voice could melt listeners’ bones with its sweetness. “Senior Brother, please be gentle. This humble girl can’t endure too much force.”

Ye Mengyin gazed pitifully at Meng Jingzhou while secretly casting her allure arts. In the city-level and provincial-level matches, these few words had been enough to bewitch her opponents into surrendering voluntarily.

“Why don’t you concede defeat? I don’t discriminate by gender when fighting.” Meng Jingzhou grinned at her. His eyes remained clear, showing no signs of being bewitched.

Be it facing men, women, or Lu Yang, I never hold back.

Ye Mengyin was stunned. Since my debut, I’ve never encountered a cultivator at the same realm who’s unaffected by my allure arts. Even prodigies had to divert their attention to resist; none were immune to it like Meng Jingzhou.

As expected of someone from the Dao-Seeking Sect. He indeed has some skills.

Before the finals, she had strolled through the commercial street and participated in the activities. That was when she heard Meng Jingzhou’s preaching: “Cultivators should stay single; females are all rouge-colored skeletons.”

She had simply shrugged it off, certain it was because Meng Jingzhou hadn’t met her yet. After all, the Allure Sect’s cultivators had records of bewitching even monastery monks back to secular life.

Retrieving a guqin from her storage ring, Ye Mengyin plucked its strings. The melody flowed like a caressing breeze, so tender that even cultivators in the audience were entranced.

She was a rare sound cultivator.

Combined with allure arts and her first-grade golden core—Scorching Desire Golden Core—none at her realm could rival her!

...Except Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, Tao Yaoye, Man Gu, Lan Ting, Bai Ming, Yan Tianzhi...

“Heaven-Shaking Six Forms!” Meng Jingzhou roared, drowning out the sound of the guqin as he charged forward, golden fists igniting sparks as they brushed through the air.

The two Single’s Golden Cores spun within him, nullifying all allure arts.

Only the music posed a threat, slowing his movements. However, as a physique cultivator, his body was so robust that even Lu Yang avoided frontal clashes. Control of this extent was but a drizzle to him, its effect negligible.

Ye Mengyin never imagined her proud moves wouldn’t work on Meng Jingzhou. Before she could react, a sandbag-like fist smashed into her face, the impact alone sounding painful as she crumpled to the ground.

Meng Jingzhou won.

“Are you alright, sister?” Meng Jingzhou kindly helped her up. During the match, we were merciless opponents; after the match, we’re fellow Daoists supporting each other.

Ye Mengyin gazed at Meng Jingzhou with tender affection. It’s my first time encountering such a powerful male cultivator. All male cultivators I’ve met in the past would grovel before me, terrified I’d see through them.

Only Meng Jingzhou remained utterly indifferent.

She said, “When I began my cultivation, I swore in my sect’s name—whoever can defeat me, I will marry them.”

“That sounds inappropriate...” Meng Jingzhou chuckled awkwardly. My peach-blossom romantic luck arrived so abruptly.

Ye Mengyin shook her head gently. “There’s nothing inappropriate about that. Our sect also has a rule—no disciple may marry a Dao-Seeking Sect disciple or someone from the Meng Family.

“Shifu said marrying into either would easily bring trouble upon our sect.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

What did my family ever do to you? Go ask around the imperial city—the Meng Family is widely known! Sure, it may not be for the right reasons, but it’s not like we have sunk to the Dao-Seeking Sect’s level!

Whatever, I shall not think so much. A win’s a win.

Off to a victorious start, he cheerfully descended the arena stage and boasted to Bai Ming and the others. “You saw my fight earlier, right? One punch, and down she went.”

“Impressive, impressive! I’m always cautious when fighting female cultivators, afraid I might strike the wrong spot and be mistaken as a lecher. Looks like I need to learn from Senior Brother Meng.” Bai Ming applauded, having gleaned many insights from Meng Jingzhou.

I’d cared too much about saving face in the past—that truly wasn’t the way.

“Amazing,” Yan Tianzhi summarized succinctly.

The matches continued, and Bai Ming and Lan Ting managed to advance, their prowess clearly surpassing their peers by a large margin.

“Seems the winner of this category will be among us four,” Meng Jingzhou declared.

“Don’t conclude so hastily.” Bai Ming shook his head and pointed at the cultivator currently standing on the stage.

“All of you have seen the matches of earlier categories. Some contestants are comparable to our cultivators from immortal sects; the Intermediate Golden Core category is no exception.

“See that cultivator on the stage? He’s from our Yun Province. He already stood out in the provincial-level matches, demonstrating outstanding combat talent, adaptability, and solid foundations. He practically has no shortcomings. Even his mental power—the hardest to cultivate—doesn’t lag behind. His golden core is likely a first-grade golden core, the Devouring Golden Core, that drains opponents’ spirit energy in battle.”

As they discussed in whispers, a sonorous laughter rang from above.

Under everyone’s gaze, a young man descended from the skies, landing on the arena stage and halting the match.

“With such a lively scene, how could our Heavenly Court Creed be absent?”

Upon the clouds stood several more figures, each emanating terrifying auras.

Chapter 493: Young Creed Leader Lu

“Heavenly Court Creed?”

The gathered guests gasped in unison upon hearing the young man announce his identity.

If the hottest topic among low-level cultivators these past two months had been speculating tournament victors, then high-level cultivators were consumed by endless discussions of Dou Heavenly Sovereign, who had showed up during the Hanshui City battle and proclaimed to be the Heavenly Court Creed’s Supreme Grand Heavenly Sovereign.

This was the first immortal to have appeared in public since the Four Ancient Immortals. Be it Great Qian, Great Yu, or even Great Xia, all had legends of immortals keeping watch within the forbidden grounds of the imperial palace, yet none had ever seen them.

The appearance of Dou Heavenly Sovereign had sent shockwaves through the outside world. Whether it was those at the Fusion or the Transcendent Tribulation stages, all were debating about the identity of Dou Heavenly Sovereign and the nature of the Heavenly Court Creed. Theories abounded, but no consensus had yet to be reached.

Some claimed the Heavenly Court Creed was an ancient organization that had only recently awakened. Others posited that it had existed since ancient times, lurking in the shadows of history all this time and manipulating the rise and fall of dynasties as the mastermind behind the scenes.

No one expected the Heavenly Court Creed to appear uninvited at the imperial court’s tournament and the 120,000-year celebration of the Dao-Seeking Sect with such brazen audacity. The more perceptive ones had already detected the thick scent of gunpowder in this bold move.

The Heavenly Court Creed has come with ill intentions.

“Who are you?” As the acting sect leader, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy demanded sharply by controlling Lu Yang’s body. Her tone carried an undercurrent of decisive, lethal intent.

The Heavenly Court Creed youth stood calmly on the arena stage, showing no fear despite being surrounded by belligerent experts. Instead, he cupped his fists and spoke clearly. “You must be the rising star, Sect Leader Lu Yang—renowned at a young age with solid foundations. If you had competed, you would have easily clinched first place. What a coincidence—we share the same family name. My surname is also Lu, and I’m our creed’s young creed leader.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy narrowed her eyes, ignoring his flattery as her voice turned frosty. “So it’s Young Creed Leader Lu. May I ask why you have come to our Dao-Seeking Sect and disrupted our tournament? And what business do those few individuals in the sky have here?”

Dark clouds loomed above the arena stage, upon which stood five solemn figures as imposing as ghost gods.

“I am the Heavenly Court Creed’s protector, Nether World Heavenly King.” Ominous black energy emanated from him as if he had awakened from an ancient tomb, resurrected with the grievances of the dead to bring ceaseless calamity to the world.

“I am the Heavenly Court Creed’s protector, Hundred Herbs Heavenly King.” The scent of medicinal herbs wafted from him. One whiff was enough to discern it was extraordinary and could only result from prolonged exposure to Little Herb Kings.

“I am the Heavenly Court Creed’s protector, Unbreakable Heavenly King.” He resembled the arhats with golden bodies in Buddhist sects’ lore, or perhaps he was the inspiration for those arhats! His physique was powerful without a single weak point—the pinnacle of a physique cultivator.

“I am the Heavenly Court Creed’s protector, Myriad Treasures Heavenly King.” Strings of magical treasures hung at his waist, and the most conspicuous was a top-tier magical treasure that even Transcendent Tribulation cultivators covet. It contained an artifact spirit refined from a Transcendent Tribulation soul—utterly terrifying!

“I am the Heavenly Court Creed’s protector, Golden Flame Heavenly King.” Golden flames occasionally surged around him—not one of the 108 True Fires but seemingly a fusion of them all, elevating true fire to unprecedented heights.

The five figures stood like insurmountable mountains, their auras aged as if they hailed from ancient times. Despite their ancient aura, anyone could see these heavenly kings were in their prime, far from being old and perhaps not even at their peak yet.

“I feel like these five haven’t reached the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. Why are our old ancestors not intercepting them?” The Qi-Commanding Sect Leader whispered, particularly sensitive to auras.

The One-Qi Venerable Lord’s glare scared the Qi-Commanding Sect Leader. The latter immediately knew he had misspoken and kept silent.

Only then did the One-Qi Venerable Lord explain through an auditory message. “You think you’re smarter than all the Transcendent Tribulation cultivators present?”

“Please enlighten me, old ancestor.”

“Are you aware that one must pass the River Spirit’s trial before they can enter the Dao-Seeking Sect? The River Spirit’s methods rival a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator’s. Anyone who slipped past definitely wasn’t relying on methods at the Fusion Stage.

“Do you think the Heavenly Court Creed figures that have shown themselves are the only members here? In my opinion, at least one half-immortal from the Heavenly Court Creed is lurking in the shadows.

“Moreover, the Dao-Seeking Sect mentioned they have methods to deal with half-immortals, yet they haven’t acted. I’m afraid it’s the worst-case scenario—Dou Heavenly Sovereign is also here, perhaps right under our noses, unnoticed by everyone!”

The Qi-Commanding Sect Leader shuddered, a chill running down his spine.

“Pardon our discourtesy,” rumbled the Nether World Heavenly King, who appeared to be the leader of the heavenly kings.

As the five heavenly kings descended, the crowd scattered in fear and hastily cleared a space, none daring to approach them. Under their terrifying aura waves, some prodigies could barely remain standing.

Young Creed Leader Lu smiled as if he was oblivious to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s hostility. “Ever since I’ve awakened from my slumber since ancient times, I have yet to meet my match at the same cultivation realm. By chance, I heard of the tournament at your esteemed sect, so I came to join in the excitement. Please forgive us for coming uninvited, Sect Leader Lu.”

Slumber since ancient times? The crowd was stunned again by this revelation. The Heavenly Court Creed indeed hails from the ancient era!

Glancing at the two prodigies on stage, Young Creed Leader Lu added, “These two are at the Intermediate Golden Core Stage, and coincidentally, so am I. Let me face them as my opponents. Should I lose, our creed will leave, but if I win, it will prove my strength, and we shall stay. Would that be acceptable?”

“One against two? You certainly talk big, Young Creed Leader Lu.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy snorted. “But refusing your challenge would tarnish Great Xia’s magnanimous reputation. Fine, if you win this match, you shall be granted a spot in the tournament. However, if you lose, get out of the Dao-Seeking Sect at once!” Toward the end, her tone became laced with killing intent.

The prodigies in the audience inwardly cheered, wishing they could applaud. Young Creed Leader Lu is arrogant and overbearing, speaking as if we prodigies were beneath him. However, in the face of such a formidable Heavenly Court Creed, Sect Leader Lu shows no fear and even threatens them.

This courage alone surpasses all of us!

“Well said, Sect Leader Lu! I, Qiu Jin’an, agree with Sect Leader Lu. Since antiquity, winners reign, losers flee. If you lose, crawl back wherever you came from!”

The leaders of the Five Great Immortal Sects and the Eldest Prince stepped forth to support the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

Seeing these six major factions of the righteous faction join hands against a common foe, the crowd clenched their fists in exhilaration.

Only Meng Jingzhou stared at the so-called Young Creed Leader Lu with dead-fish eyes throughout this whole time.

The Eldest Prince was on tenterhooks. It’s my first time doing something like this. I didn’t give myself away, did I?

Anyway, why do those from the Five Great Immortal Sects seem so practiced at this?

Chapter 494: When There Is No History, Create It

“This Young Creed Leader Lu is a formidable opponent.” Bai Ming remarked.

He and the others wore grave expressions. Fixing their gazes on the flashy young creed leader on the stage, they tensed in preparation.

“Not someone to take lightly.” Yan Tianzhi also felt the pressure emanating from both Young Creed Leader Lu and the Heavenly Court Creed behind him.

The collective stance of the Five Great Immortal Sects and the imperial court spoke volumes about the Heavenly Court Creed’s terrifying influence.

Lan Ting’s eyes flickered with bewilderment. I can’t help but find something disturbingly familiar about this Young Creed Leader Lu’s mannerisms.

Lu Yang’s opponents were Mo Wenli, a true lineage disciple of the Thunder-Fire Sect, a first-class sect, and Su Mo, a remarkable genius among rogue cultivators. Both broke into cold sweats as they watched Lu Yang’s relaxed demeanor.

“No holding back; we attack together!” Su Mo commanded Mo Wenli in a deep voice. For someone as proud as he was, joining forces with another was a disgrace. But we’re against the young creed leader of the Heavenly Court Creed. If I want to win this, I must swallow my pride.

Mo Wenli frowned. He’s merely a fellow hyped up to be a remarkable genius by rogue cultivators—what right does he have to order me about?

“Follow my lead if you want to win!” Su Mo’s brow knitted, radiating authority despite not raising his voice. This junior really doesn’t know what’s good for him.

Mo Wenli shivered involuntarily, startled by Su Mo. He felt as if he had seen his shifu in Su Mo. “You’d better have a plan,” he conceded grudgingly.

Seeing Mo Wenli’s compliance, Su Mo’s expression softened lightly, and he transmitted an auditory message. “As the art of war states: delay breeds uncertainty—end battles swiftly.

“Your thunder spells should be at a level ready for combat. If sword spells rank first in offense, thunder spells rank second. I’ll restrain him with my golden core’s abilities while you charge up your attack from behind and strike with full power!”

Mo Wenli replied, “Alright. But are you certain your golden core can restrain him?”

Su Mo didn’t answer. I dispersed my cultivation to cultivate anew, condensing my Devouring Golden Core through painstaking efforts. It can devour an opponent’s spirit energy; anyone encountering such a situation would panic momentarily.

In battles at the Golden Core Stage, a moment of panic can decide the outcome.

Su Mo’s calves grew as straight as an arrow, propelling him toward Young Creed Leader Lu with a speed that surpassed Mo Wenli’s.

The moment they engaged, Su Mo recognized how intractable his opponent was. He has rich combat experience and strong adaptability. I’d be delusional to think I can gain an advantage with my combat experience alone.

Why does he have such vast combat experience? This doesn’t seem to have been accumulated through battles against peers but through battles against multiple higher-level opponents.

Of course, he’s the young creed leader of the Heavenly Court Creed. He must have had experts feeding him moves to accumulate such terrifying combat experience.

But so what? I only need to restrain him!

“Devour!” Su Mo recited inwardly, summoning his golden core. The Devouring Golden Core spun madly, and every time it came into contact with Young Creed Leader Lu, it would siphon some of his spirit energy away.

This move always works.

However, just as he activated his golden core, he saw Young Creed Leader Lu parting his lips.

Soon, he understood why.

I’m devouring his spirit energy, but he’s also devouring my spirit energy, achieving a strange and delicate equilibrium!

How is this possible?!

Could he also have a Devouring Golden Core?!

Su Mo clenched his teeth. Now that things have come to this, I can’t be bothered that much. He sensed the mighty lightning power surging behind him—Mo Wenli had finished charging up his lightning spell.

“Get out of the way!” Mo Wenli forced out through gritted teeth. The lightning’s power was so heavy that his arms shook simply from propping it up.

Su Mo barely dodged aside as the devastating burst of lightning power exploded behind him. Sparks flew everywhere, resembling silver serpents dancing wildly with raging energy.

Boom! The silver-serpent lightning swallowed Young Creed Leader Lu.

Before Su Mo and Mo Wenli could rejoice, a sharp hiss cut through the air as sword light flashed, splitting the mass of lightning in twain. The lightning burst apart, and a figure wielding a sword emerged from the explosion, completely unruffled.

“The power’s not bad, but unfortunately, it’s too scattered. Had you concentrated it to a single point, even I might have found it troublesome,” Young Creed Leader Lu evaluated offhandedly.

This Young Creed Leader Lu is a sword cultivator, number one in offense!

While Mo Wenli stood frozen in shock, Su Mo reacted first, deftly evading to the side. There’s no time to be dazed on the battlefield!

Just as he was about to warn Mo Wenli, another sword light streaked past, and before any words could leave his mouth, Su Mo found himself already off the stage.

“One down.”

The sword’s tip dragged across the stage strewn with debris, producing irregular screeches that sent chills down Su Mo’s spine.

However, rage quickly replaced his fear. I am an almighty reforged cultivator with two thousand years of cultivation experience. I’m meant to ascend to greater heights. How could I be a prey at others’ mercy?

I will teach this young man how terrifying a reforged cultivator can be when he gets serious!

~~~

“Winner: Heavenly Court Creed.” The referee announced the result of the match.

On the arena stage, Young Creed Leader Lu sheathed his sword with impeccable grace and posture, then lifted his gaze to the judges’ platform. “So, am I qualified to continue participating in the tournament?”

“This sect leader keeps his word. You may continue. Though I do have one question.”

“Please speak, Sect Leader Lu.”

“When Su Mo activated his Devouring Golden Core to devour your spirit energy, you also devoured his spirit energy. Could that have been the Taotie Tribe’s life-bound mighty ability—the most ancient and primordial version of Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth?”

Young Creed Leader Lu stared at Sect Leader Lu in surprise, not expecting the latter to recognize it. “Impressive discernment, Sect Leader Lu.”

Qiu Jin’an interjected at the right moment. “What distinguishes this most ancient version from its modern counterpart?”

Young Creed Leader Lu remained silent, waiting for Sect Leader Lu’s answer instead.

Sect Leader Lu’s voice boomed across the venue. “As all of you probably know, I have also cultivated Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth. During my studies, I uncovered an ancient secret of the Taotie Tribe.

“In the ancient era, the Taotie race was brutal beyond measure. While most demon beasts feed on living beings by instinct, the Taotie Tribe never did so. Instead, they devoured the spirit energy in the world, feeding on the earth and stars. Hence, they were called the ferocious beasts of heaven and earth!

“And how did they manage to devour all that? It was none other than the most ancient Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth!

“The primitive version proved too cruel, provoking crusades from other races. Succumbing to the pressure, the Taotie race modified it into its current form. Though it still claims to devour all things, its might pales in comparison to what it used to be!

“Even the Taotie Tribe today doesn’t know the most ancient version of Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth. I didn’t expect Young Creed Leader Lu to be capable of this move. It seems that the legends are real—the Heavenly Court Creed was indeed the biggest faction in ancient times.”

Gasps swept through the audience as they processed this shocking revelation about the Taotie Tribe’s hidden history.

~~~

Inside the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy kicked her dainty feet in excitement, her pink pearl-like toes wiggling in excitement.

“Well? Well? Did I act well?”

“Perfect! That’s exactly the feeling I wanted!”

Chapter 495: The Power of Bonds!

The moment Su Mo and Mo Wenli stepped down from the arena stage, they saw a figure rushing toward them in evident panic.

It turned out to be the Thunder-Fire Sect Leader. Approaching Su Mo with concern, he asked, “Shifu, are you alright?”

“Shifu?” Mo Wenli was utterly baffled, unable to understand what was happening.

“This is my shifu and your grand-shifu,” the Thunder-Fire Sect Leader explained through an auditory message.

“Grand-Shifu? But didn’t you say he was dead?” Mo Wenli was nonplussed, recalling that his earlier attitude toward Su Mo hadn’t been particularly respectful.

“That was just our official story to the outside world. In truth, your grand-shifu is a reforged cultivator aiming for the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. He had several enemies in his early years, so after dispersing his cultivation to cultivate anew, he kept a low profile in fear of retaliation. That’s why we announced to the world that he was dead.”

“And you didn’t tell me even when I was about to fight Grand-Shifu...” Mo Wenli gave the Thunder-Fire Sect Leader a reproachful look. Had the Heavenly Court Creed not intervened, we might have actually come to blows.

The Thunder-Fire Sect Leader scolded, “Isn’t it because you can’t keep secrets?! I was afraid you’d give it away during the match. And that Young Creed Leader Lu was right—look at how sloppy your lightning spells are, splitting apart like forked piss! You’re going into seclusion when we return, and you won’t come out until you’ve achieved some results!”

Mo Wenli’s face turned ashen.

“Now, now, no need to frighten a junior,” Su Mo interjected, playing peacemaker. “Little Mo is pretty strong. It’s just that his opponent this time was stronger. Tell you what, I’ll give you some pointers when we return.” He was actually quite pleased with Mo Wenli, viewing him as promising material.

The Thunder-Fire Sect Leader stared at him with an unreadable look. “You weren’t like this with me back in the day.”

~~~

Below the arena stage, the five heavenly kings exuded an aura that warned others to keep their distance. Though spectators didn’t dare approach, they couldn’t suppress their curiosity.

“Those five heavenly kings are so frightening! Just getting near them makes me shiver.”

“You don’t say! They’re from a major ancient faction, and you know how chaotic those times were; human lives were as worthless as grass. Who knows how many lives these heavenly kings have taken!”

“Shh! Don’t let them hear you!”

“We’re using voice transmission. They can’t hear us, right?”

“Better safe than sorry. Who’s to say there weren’t secret spells to eavesdrop in ancient times? Look at how palpable these five people’s killing intent is. They’re definitely the vindictive type. If they take notice of you, do you think you’ll still have peaceful days ahead?”

“But you seem to have said more outrageous things than we did.”

~~~

The five heavenly king protectors stood as motionless as stone statues, their minds free of distractions while they watched everything indifferently, devoid of joy or sorrow.

First Elder transmitted an auditory message gleefully. “You know, the acting sect leader’s idea is not bad. By leveraging our home advantage to stage a grand debut for the Heavenly Court Creed, our reputation is now established. The diabolic creeds and archaic cultivators are bound to take the bait.” He had seen the shock, fear, and panic on everyone’s faces during their flashy entrance, and he found it immensely satisfying.

“Say, do you think we’d get exposed?” Grandpa Ba asked nervously. As satisfying and thrilling as it was, he feared the truth might come to light. This time was different from their usual cons, where they deceived those of the same cultivation realm. Now, they were trying to dupe even Transcendent Tribulation seniors.

If we get exposed, going out of the sect in the future will be perilous. They didn’t fear anyone at the Fusion Stage, for none could defeat them, but if a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator stepped in, they could only pray their shifu would arrive in time to save them.

Third Elder thought his second brother’s worries were unwarranted. “No chance of that. Junior Niece Yun gave us her word; she assured us there’s no way we’ll be exposed.

”Besides, even if we do get exposed, it’s not a problem. I’ve prepared a backup plan.”

The other four were astonished. Since when did Old Three prepare a backup plan?

“What backup plan?”

“I bought insurance for all five of us at the merchant guild. Even if something happens, we’ll get a hefty sum of spirit stones... But never mind that, my disciple is taking the stage now.”

“Meng Jingzhou, Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“Long Huo, Longteng Village!”

Longteng Village was a unique entity. It was both an administrative unit of Great Xia and part of the aristocratic Long Family’s influence.

Eight thousand years ago, an expert surnamed Long settled in a desolate part of Ji Province with his wife, concubine, and servants. No one knew his origins; it was as if he had appeared out of nowhere. Some claimed he came from the East Sea and was a dragon-human.

The expert sired several sons and daughters before passing away, leaving behind an enormous amount of cultivation resources. His descendants remained upon this land, continuing to thrive and carrying forth his bloodline.

Thanks to the resources left by that expert and the considerable talent of his children, the family did not squander their inheritance. Over generations, outsiders began calling them the Ji Province Long Family, and they became an ancestral clan.

Gradually, the area took shape. When local officials inspected the site and deemed that it met the criteria for a village, they reported it up the chain of command. The higher-ups designated it as a village and respected the Long Family’s wishes, naming it Longteng Village.

The village chief of Longteng Village was always the current patriarch of the Long Family for every generation. Long Huo was the son of the previous patriarch. Although he was suppressed by the current patriarch in his youth, as he demonstrated outstanding talent and became Longteng Village’s most gifted cultivator, even the current patriarch could no longer oppress him.

Long Huo activated his golden core—a first-grade water-type golden core—covering his body with a thin film of water that could block attacks to some degree.

“Roving Dragon Strike!”

Like a roaming dragon, Long Huo darted across the arena at terrifying speed, leaving afterimages in his wake. Even one’s spiritual consciousness struggled to pinpoint his location. He circled behind Meng Jingzhou and seized the moment when his opponent had yet to react, targeting his neck with a knifehand strike.

“Got you!” His heart leaped with triumph. My opponent had been careless.

To his shock, however, Meng Jingzhou dodged the ambush with just a slight shift of his body.

“What?!” There’s no way he could have seen me coming.

Meng Jingzhou yawned in boredom. This opponent is nothing special.

Refusing to give up, Long Huo unleashed the Roving Dragon Strike again, launching relentless assaults from all directions, but Meng Jingzhou evaded them all with ease.

~~~

Below the stage, Young Creed Leader Lu clapped, his eyes alight with excitement as if he had found an opponent he had long yearned for. “Terrific! As expected of a disciple representing the Dao-Seeking Sect. Unless I’m mistaken, he has reached the ‘No-Self Forget-Self’ realm of physique cultivation. Even among ancient prodigies, none accomplished this at the Intermediate Golden Core Stage!”

The Unbreakable Heavenly King nodded. “It looks like he has only recently entered this realm. At this level, his body automatically dodges low-threat attacks without conscious thought.” Since “low-threat” didn’t mean no threat, one would naturally still dodge the attacks.

With Young Creed Leader Lu’s explanation, the prodigies below the stage finally understood how formidable a physique cultivator Meng Jingzhou was.

Meng Jingzhou nodded in satisfaction. This kid Lu Yang isn’t so bad after all.

He executed the Heaven-Shaking Six Forms and took a sudden step forward. With a burst of power, he dealt a threefold fist force that sent Long Huo flying.

Long Huo desperately dissipated the fist force, staggering backward until he stabilized himself just half a chi from the arena’s edge.

Meng Jingzhou’s expression was one of mild astonishment. “Not bad, you could withstand that punch! Again!”

No longer holding back, Meng Jingzhou ceaselessly unleashed Heaven-Shaking Six Forms, driving Long Huo back. However, each time he thought he had knocked Long Huo off the stage, Long Huo unexpectedly withstood the blow.

Even so, Long Huo gradually buckled under the barrage of intense assaults.

“You can’t win. Just admit defeat.”

Should I really admit defeat? Aware of the gulf between them, Long Huo closed his eyes unwillingly. After fighting so long, I’m also exhausted. Continuing will be futile; the outcome is already set.

Is the gap between me and a true prodigy really this vast?

“Long Huo-gege,[1] you can do it! Jiayou!”

“Long Huo, don’t give up!”

“You’re the man who defeated me to represent our village. You can’t lose here!”

Images of his companions flashed through Long Huo’s mind—his childhood sweetheart, his close friends, the patriarch’s son who was both a rival and an ally...

“I mustn’t admit defeat!” I bear the village’s hopes, fighting as the Long Family’s representative. How could I admit defeat here?!

The referee walked over and glanced at Long Huo, who lay sprawled on the ground.

“His life is already flashing before his eyes?

“Winner of this match: Meng Jingzhou.”

1. Gege is a term of endearment used to address an older male, typically by a female. ☜

Chapter 496: Removing the Seal!

Long Huo’s mouth was stuffed with several life-saving pills before being carried off by the referee.

Meng Jingzhou emerged victorious.

A cooling sensation spread through Long Huo’s throat as the pills took effect. He gradually regained consciousness, his mind blank for a while before the realization of his defeat hit him.

“You alright? You fought well.” Meng Jingzhou extended a hand and pulled Long Huo to his feet.

Long Huo shook his head with a bitter smile. “A loss is a loss. I’m not one who can’t accept defeat.”

Worried that Long Huo might lose heart after this defeat, Meng Jingzhou kindly said, “I’ll be waiting for you to beat me next time.”

After a moment of silence, Long Huo nodded. “Alright.”

After their brief exchange, Long Huo descended from the arena stage to find the village chief—a stern middle-aged man—waiting for him.

“Village Chief...I’ve failed the village’s expectations.”

The village chief’s lips curved into a faint smile as he patted Long Huo’s shoulder. “You did remarkably well just to hold your own. Meng Jingzhou is no ordinary opponent. He’s both the eldest young master of the Meng Family and a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect. The Meng Family is the number one ancestral clan, and the Dao-Seeking Sect is the number one major sect. These two identities are enough to wipe the floor with all peers.

“Also, look who’s here.”

Long Huo looked up to see the village chief step aside, revealing two beautiful figures—his childhood sweetheart and a godsister who treated him like her own younger brother.

“Long Huo-gege, you already did great!” His childhood sweetheart was a vivacious young girl brimming with energy.

“Long Huo, you fought splendidly. My daily guidance hasn’t gone to waste.” His godsister had a striking figure and a bearing that commanded authority.

“Everyone...” Tears welled up in Long Huo’s eyes as he sobbed uncontrollably, vowing to train even harder upon returning and never let them down again.

Not far away, Meng Jingzhou watched the scene silently. Can we have a rematch? I’d like to hit this fellow with my Single’s Curse Fist.

~~~

Under countless gazes, Young Creed Leader Lu’s second match was about to begin.

“Young Creed Leader, Heavenly Court Creed.”

“Kong Hao, Waterfall Sect.”

The second-class sect, Waterfall Sect, had shallow foundations; its sect leader was only at the Void Refinement Stage. Even among second-class sects, it was an obscure and unremarkable existence.

Bai Ming had researched several opponents beforehand. “This Kong Hao isn’t simple. He appears quiet, like a scholarly cultivator, but fights like an untamed beast. Even before the battle begins, his frenzied demeanor instills some fear in his opponents.”

~~~

The Waterfall Sect Leader stroked his beard, watching Kong Hao with satisfaction. Thanks to Kong Hao, I’m qualified to attend this celebration and meet so many prominent figures.

“This kid Kong Hao has indeed been concealing his strength.”

Kong Hao was reticent and rarely spoke with others, keeping a low profile. However, during sect tournaments, he would always narrowly seize first place, seeming to be only slightly better than the runner-up. Yet, no matter how the second-place cultivator tried, they could never defeat Kong Hao.

The Waterfall Sect Leader had suspected Kong Hao was concealing his ability, but he never imagined it would be to this extent.

~~~

Young Creed Leader Lu drew his treasured sword, temporarily borrowed from the sect’s treasury.

The Qingming Sword and Mingyue Sword had already appeared at the Qing Province Grand Ceremony, so using them again as the young creed leader would reveal his true identity. Hence, Lu Yang leveraged his wide connections, having the Everlasting Immortal Fairy step in to borrow a sword from the treasury.

Facing Kong Hao, Lu Yang’s brow furrowed slightly. This person gives me an unusually dangerous feeling. Even great reforged cultivators haven’t made me feel this way.

“Hidden dragons and crouching tigers—hidden talents huh...”

Kong Hao knew his opponent was formidable. Only by fighting with my full power do I stand a chance.

Placing two fingers to his lips, he exhaled a frigid breath, and the arena’s temperature gradually dropped. Lu Yang lifted his foot slightly, finding his movements sluggish as if he was mired in a swamp.

“Ice cultivation techniques are quite rare...” Lu Yang suddenly noticed something amiss. “Wait, it’s not just cold air. It’s laced with poison!” Mistaking it for mere frigid air and circulating one’s energy to dispel it would only accelerate the poisonous air’s absorption, eventually leaving one vulnerable.

“But it doesn't matter.” As a frequent visitor to Pill Cauldron Peak, Lu Yang had built resistance to common poisons and wouldn’t be affected in a short time. With a light spin of his sword, he cleared the surrounding area of both the frigid air and the poisonous air.

Lu Yang’s various spells and techniques were too distinctive, allowing anyone to recognize him at a glance. Thus, he could only employ sword techniques when he acted as Young Creed Leader Lu. Fortunately, due to his Sword Spirit Root, his swordsmanship was exceptional.

Seizing the moment while Lu Yang cleared the air, Kong Hao growled deeply, his muscles bulging like a frenzied beast. Yet, his eyes remained cold and clear, showing he kept in control. He charged forward, his nails elongating into claws of demon beasts as they clashed against the sword. Surprisingly, they didn’t break.

Lu Yang narrowed his eyes. The solid foundation Kong Hao displays isn’t something a second-class sect could nurture. This can’t be simply explained by extraordinary talent.

The audience gasped softly as the two clashed fiercely on stage. Unlike the first match’s swift conclusion, this battle appeared evenly matched.

Only Fusion cultivators could discern that Young Creed Leader Lu held the upper hand all along. While they seemed to be trading blows for blows, Young Creed Leader Lu had been leading Kong Hao by the nose the entire time.

Lu Yang thought, This alone isn’t enough to threaten me. He decided to unleash his full power.

With a twist of his wrist, his sword tip traced an arc through the air, and sword qi as thin as ox hair erupted from every pore, converging along the blade. Sword qi raged like misty clouds and a vast ocean, sweeping across all directions as if it was devouring heaven and earth.

Kong Hao took this strike head-on. Even blocking with both arms proved futile. His limbs dripped blood as his aura waves instantly withered, and he panted heavily from severe injuries.

“Brat, about to lose?” A voice echoed in his mind. It was deep and slow, hinting at the speaker’s colossal nature.

“None of your business.” That last sword strike made Kong Hao realize the chasm between him and Lu Yang. This is an innate disparity in talent—no amount of effort can bridge the gap.

Through the metal bars in his mind, he stared at the colossal entity.

The colossal entity scoffed at his egotism. “Mind your tone, you conceited brat. Without me, how could you be where you are today?

“I’ve been inside you since you were born. I know exactly how stubborn you are. You act humble, but when have you ever admitted defeat? Your desire to win surpasses anyone’s; otherwise, I wouldn’t have bothered with you.”

Long Huo demanded, “What do you want?”

“Power—that’s what you lack. I’ll lend it to you.”

Kong Hao stared at the colossal entity silently. Indeed, even a sliver of this power could let me turn the tide. But I’ll need to break a layer of seal if I want to use that power.

Should I?

The colossal entity grinned, its massive beast-eyes reflecting Kong Hao’s conflicted visage. Once you taste my power and realize how quickly it makes you stronger, you will willingly break seal after seal—until I’m free.

Kong Hao gritted his teeth. This colossal entity is right. I don’t want to lose. I want to be the champion.

One layer. I’ll just remove one layer. I won’t touch the remaining eight layers.

The colossal entity laughed silently. After the first seal came undone, an ominous power seeped through the metal bars and clung to Kong Hao.

“Hmm?”

Outside, Lu Yang watched in astonishment as a sinister power surging with cruelty and bloodlust gushed forth from Kong Hao endlessly.

Kong Hao’s body transformed. His wounds healed at a visible pace, and his gravely wounded body completely recovered in seconds. His pupils slit like a frenzied lion or ferocious tiger, and a layer of beastly fur sprouted across his skin, though it was indistinguishable whether they had grown naturally or were formed from spirit qi.

Kong Hao’s roar shook the heavens.

Lu Yang’s hair stood on end. This was the source of danger I’d sensed!

However, he soon found Kong Hao’s state familiar. It’s like he is temporarily possessed and borrowing a power that doesn’t belong to him.

Watching Kong Hao warily, Lu Yang raised his hand slowly and activated his trump card.

“Referee, I’m reporting him for cheating.”

Chapter 497: Lu Yang’s Three Trump Cards

Lu Yang had three trump cards he would never use lightly.

First was Yun Zhi’s Animal Form Fist—to summon his Big Senior Sister.

Second was the Spirit Medium method—to invite the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to possess him.

Third was the Unbeatable Golden Core—capable of formulating winning strategies.

Employing any one of these would prove devastating to opponents of the same cultivation realm. Lu Yang would only reveal one of these trump cards when facing overwhelmingly powerful foes or when opponents resorted to underhanded tactics first.

Kong Hao was considered the latter.

The power he displays clearly doesn’t belong to him. It’s likely from a powerful soul entity inside him. Lu Yang was all too familiar with this tactic. After all, I also have one inside me.

There’s no way to fight now.

That powerful soul entity had to be minimally at the Fusion Stage. How was Lu Yang supposed to stand a chance against that?

He decisively used his Unbeatable Golden Core, which provided a straightforward solution he had anticipated—reporting it to the referee.

“So this is what you call a genius? Relying on external power to fight me?” Young Creed Leader Lu sneered. “If none of you intervene, I too possess magical treasures bestowed by the creed leader and my shifu; even Transcendent Tribulation cultivators can’t withstand a strike from them.

“I refrained from using them precisely because they are overpowered. But if Kong Hao’s not violating the rules, I won’t bother holding back either.”

The referee froze momentarily upon hearing Lu Yang’s report. Despite his extensive experience, he had never encountered someone borrowing power from another soul within them to battle. Only after Lu Yang’s explanation did he recognize that Kong Hao’s power didn’t belong to him.

This undoubtedly constitutes a violation of the rules.

“Loser: Kong Hao.”

Just as Kong Hao prepared to wield his newfound power, the referee’s declaration of the match’s result made him leave the stage dejectedly.

Instead of the Waterfall Sect Leader receiving him, various Transcendent Tribulation old ancestors immediately surrounded him.

“Make way! Let me examine who’s inside this child.”

“Since I created the Body Takeover Technique, I’m an expert in this field—I should go first.”

“My cultivation is the highest here. Let me do it.”

The Waterfall Sect Leader tried to approach, but these venerable figures had already jostled him to the back.

“This aura resembles the Four Perils,” the One-Qi Venerable Lord observed, particularly sensitive to auras. “Young fellow, don’t resist. I’ll go and take a look at your spirit platform.” With that, a miniature figure emerged from his spirit platform and flew into Kong Hao’s spirit platform.

“Ho, it’s a big fellow.”

Kong Hao’s spirit platform was much more spacious than his peers. This wasn’t the outcome of his cultivation and training, but rather the result of the colossal entity inside him forcibly expanding it.

Metal bars divided his spirit platform. The smaller section was Kong Hao’s activity space, while the larger section was where the colossal entity was sealed.

Nine layers of unbreakable seals reinforced the metal bars. The colossal entity glared at the One-Qi Venerable Lord, its beastly eyes betraying almost imperceptible traces of terror.

The colossal entity was a male lion the size of a hill, with a pristinely white flowing mane that resembled snowflakes, two upward-curving tusks that gleamed like broad sabers, and a tail matching its body length.

“So it’s an old taowu.” The One-Qi Venerable Lord sneered. This old taowu isn’t an ordinary one; it has Transcendent Tribulation cultivation. It’s more than qualified to be the Taowu Tribe’s leader. I wonder why it’s sealed here.

“If it isn’t Ji Xiong! I thought you were killed after failing the contest to become the tribe’s patriarch, yet here you are.”

As more Transcendent Tribulation cultivators entered Kong Hao’s spirit platform, someone quickly identified the old taowu’s identity.

Kong Hao had never met this many Transcendent Tribulation cultivators in his lifetime. Learning about the old taowu’s cultivation and identity shook his heart. I’d assume the Fusion Stage at best. To think it’s the absolutely terrifying Transcendent Tribulation Stage!

He was an orphan. Ever since he could remember, the old taowu had been sealed inside him by someone unknown. Fearful of attracting covetous experts, Kong Hao had hidden the old taowu’s existence and joined the Waterfall Sect, which was unremarkable even among second-class sects.

Yet despite all that, this matter was still exposed. How would these experts treat me now?

They couldn’t count on receiving honest answers from the old taowu. The Transcendent Tribulation cultivators roughly pieced together the truth by questioning Kong Hao about what he knew and combining it with their own intelligence about the old taowu.

After failing in the contest for the tribe’s leadership, the old taowu was hunted down. Its physical form destroyed and spirit wounded, it fled to Great Xia’s territory, where an Apex Fusion cultivator adept at sealing spells imprisoned it within Kong Hao’s body.

Judging by the nature of the seals, that Apex Fusion cultivator’s attitude toward Kong Hao was probably benevolent. However, as Kong Hao’s strength grew, he could gradually remove the layers of seals to access the old taowu’s power.

“You have two paths before you.” The One-Qi Venerable Lord guided Kong Hao. “Remove the seals, and we’ll capture the old taowu and compensate you accordingly with natural treasures and spiritual pills. You can consider it a purchase. This is the safest option.”

While the old taowu was an intractable opponent at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, so was everyone present. Together, they could easily overwhelm it, and the old taowu could only endure a thrashing wordlessly.

“Alternatively, you will keep the old taowu sealed. As you grow stronger, the seals will peel off layer by layer. But through this process, there’s the risk of you suffering a backlash.

“Which will you choose?”

~~~

While the group of Transcendent Tribulation cultivators examined the old taowu like some rare specimen, the tournament progressed with everything in order.

Lan Ting, afraid of Meng Jingzhou’s Single’s Curse Fist, fought hesitantly and was defeated.

Meng Jingzhou secured a place in the finals.

Yan Tianzhi followed his shifu’s instructions to go all out against the Five-Elements Sect’s Bai Ming and won, advancing to the semifinals.

“Yan Tianzhi, Prison Suppression Sect.”

“Young Creed Leader, Heavenly Court Creed.”

Lu Yang and Yan Tianzhi faced each other in the semifinals.

Yan Tianzhi’s back shimmered with the battle tattoos of a Taotie and a Qinglong (Azure Dragon), the phantom forms of these two great demon beasts flickering with oppressive pressure.

This was the Prison Suppression Sect’s unique battle tattoo cultivation method, created by their founding ancestor.

Lu Yang applauded at the two battle tattoos. “At last, an interesting opponent! I’ve long heard how exceptional the Prison Suppression Sect’s battle tattoo system is; even our creed leader praises it endlessly. Now that I’ve seen it today, it’s indeed so.

“In the ancient era, we humans had the custom of painting decorative patterns on our faces. If they were drawn properly, one could obtain boundless power. It was humanity’s first countermeasure against severe floods and monstrous beasts. Our creed leader assumed this art had been lost to time, not expecting someone in this new era to build upon these decorative patterns and develop the battle tattoo cultivation method.

“He said the creator of this cultivation method is an extraordinary genius. It’s a pity he was born at the wrong time in the transitional period between Great Yu and Great Xia. Had he lived in ancient times, he could have contended for a Dao Fruit and attained a glorious future that would reverberate through the ages!”

Lu Yang sighed wistfully, as if he was recalling the creed leader’s appraisal of the Prison Suppression Sect’s founding ancestor.

~~~

At the judges’ platform, Qiu Jin’an and Luo Hongxia stared at Yang Ding in disbelief.

This isn’t part of the script! This kid Lu Yang is practically praising your Prison Suppression Sect’s founder to the high heavens!

Yang Ding scratched his head sheepishly. “Well, it’s a good opportunity to promote our Prison Suppression Sect.”

Chapter 498: Suppress

Qiu Jin’an flew into a rage. Yang Ding, you’ve always been a pretty honest fellow. Since when did you learn to scheme in the shadows?

Why hadn’t I thought of this myself?!

Our Five-Elements Sect also needs promotion, and what better opportunity than having the Heavenly Court Creed adulate us? Yet I’d let this golden chance slip!

The Taciturn Daoist Priest had been tirelessly spinning tales to add to the Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect every day. Nowadays, one could hear pingshu performances of the Dao-Seeking Sect in any teahouse, and the Dao-Seeking Sect’s fame had skyrocketed.

Qiu Jin’an wished he could do the same, but unfortunately, the Five-Elements Sect lacked talents like the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

Luo Hongxia remained unperturbed. As a semi-secluded sect of female cultivators, the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace’s reputation already surpassed the Five-Elements Sect and the Prison Suppression Sect even without active promotion.

“Sect Leader Lu, is it too late to promote our Five-Elements Sect too? We can discuss the remuneration,” Qiu Jin’an asked the Everlasting Immortal Fairy beside him.

In the cultivation world, it was widely accepted that the ancient era marked the pinnacle of power, and everyone wanted to associate themselves with this golden age. With the Heavenly Court Creed around, a few casual remarks could let them establish some connection to the ancient era.
