However, Lu Yang was the one who had negotiated the collaboration details; the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was clueless in this regard.

She transmitted an auditory message to Lu Yang, who was still occupied with the battle on stage. After a brief contemplation, he responded, “Although I could praise the Five-Elements now and say something like ‘as expected of the sect embodying the power of heaven and earth’s five elements’ or ‘what an extraordinary genius the founding ancestor was,’ the timing would feel forced and damage the credibility of our Heavenly Court Creed. Tell Sect Leader Qiu we’ll collaborate with the Five-Elements Sect next time.”

“Oh.”

~~~

On stage, Lu Yang was locked in an intense battle with Yan Tianzhi.

In the last round, Yan Tianzhi fought with everything he had to defeat Bai Ming for the sake of publicity. To have defeated Bai Ming proved he had something going for him.

The Taotie and Qinglong (Azure Dragon) were major races among demons. Originally, Golden Core cultivators could bear only a single battle tattoo. However, Yan Tianzhi’s physique was highly compatible with the battle tattoo cultivation method. After returning from the Qing Province Grand Ceremony, he entered seclusion, bathed in the Dragon-Transformation Pool, and comprehended an additional Qinglong battle tattoo.

Although he had yet to fully master the new Qinglong battle tattoo, which was newer than the Taotie one, he still placed considerable pressure on Lu Yang.

“These battle tattoos are really troublesome.” Lu Yang gritted his teeth. This wasn’t some scripted line for an advertisement; he genuinely meant it.

Yan Tianzhi’s fighting style was brutal and fierce, relying on close-quarters combat. As Lu Yang wasn’t a physique cultivator, going head-to-head with Yan Tianzhi would put him at a disadvantage.

Based on classifications of cultivation methods, Lu Yang was considered a spell cultivator and a sword cultivator.

If only I could switch places with Meng Jingzhou—let him fight Yan Tianzhi while I face Lan Ting. That way, both of us are guaranteed to advance to the next stage.

Behind Yan Tianzhi, several orbs of water materialized. The Qinglong battle tattoo was imbued with the power of the Qinglong to command water.

The water spears tapered at both ends, sharpening into water needles that shot toward Lu Yang.

“Stunning Swan!” Lu Yang randomly threw out a name for the sword technique, though in truth, it was simply the “Slashing Word Mantra.”

At this level of cultivation, sword moves were fundamentally similar, with the main difference being their names. Although Ming Tai displayed extraordinary swordsmanship that dominated the Basic Golden Core category, all of it could still be traced back to the basic sword moves Lu Yang had mastered, such as the “Slashing Word Mantra,” “Breaking Word Mantra,” and “Pointing Word Mantra.”

So long as one didn’t execute distinctive moves such as “One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords,” “Ten Thousand Swords Return to One,” or “Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate,” most sword cultivators’ moves were more or less variations of the same foundations. Comprehension of Sword Dao was the determining factor in the strength of rudimentary sword moves.

The Slashing Word Mantra cut through the water needles, which dissolved into mist upon contacting the sword qi and spread across the arena.

“Opening Heaven!” Lu Yang made up another name on the spot. The sword qi unleashed was majestic and imposing, balanced and steady, and radiated the indomitable might of an army.

Originally, Yan Tianzhi had been planning to close the distance under the cover of the mist, but his hair stood on end as an overwhelming sense of danger gripped him. This is not something I can block with my body alone.

“Shield Ghost!” A ghost king brandished its shield menacingly as it appeared in front of Yan Tianzhi and met Lu Yang’s blade in a soundless clash, yet the impact sent ripples of shockwaves that dispersed the mist enveloping the arena.

The Shield Ghost was Yan Tianzhi’s first battle tattoo. It possessed no offensive power, but in exchange, its defense was nigh impenetrable by those at the same level.

Yan Tianzhi’s pupils constricted as he noticed fine cracks splitting across the Shield Ghost. It’s actually struggling to withstand this sword strike?

As expected of an ancient genius—truly formidable.

He still wasn’t aware of Lu Yang’s identity.

“Return!” Yan Tianzhi recalled Shield Ghost, which transformed back into the battle tattoo and branded itself on his arm. The damage sustained by the tattoo was transferred partially to his flesh, and blood immediately began to seep out.

Luckily, it’s only proportional damage. If all of the damage had been transferred, my arm would have been pierced clean by the sword qi.

Yan Tianzhi summoned his Taotie and Qinglong battle tattoos again, preparing to launch another assault.

Lu Yang scratched his cheek and sheathed his sword. “This could go on forever. Might as well try the new move I just learned.

“Suppress!”

A gigantic golden statue materialized overhead and crashed down, trapping Yan Tianzhi before he could attack.

Bang!

Yan Tianzhi was caught off guard by the sudden appearance of the statue. His head slammed into the inner wall of the statue, causing a sizable bump to form on his forehead.

The two major battle tattoos charged at the statue, but it was as immovable as a mountain, barely shaking from the impact. Instead, the reverberations from the collision left Yan Tianzhi’s ears ringing and his hearing momentarily lost.

“What is this?!”

Even the knowledgeable spectators couldn’t recognize this move.

“Seems like the Buddhist sects’ Sixteen-Foot Golden Body.”

“Don’t spout nonsense. No one’s Sixteen-Foot Golden Body manifests that far from the caster. It’s got to be a lost ancient technique.”

“Didn’t you hear him say ‘suppress?’ This might be the long-lost Law Follows Words from ancient times!”

“What?!”

Yan Tianzhi tried tunneling beneath the statue and slipping out from below, but the arena had been reinforced with such immense power that even a Divine Transfiguration battle wouldn’t leave a scratch.

His last hope was dashed.

Lu Yang naturally could move his own golden body. Seizing the chance while Yan Tianzhi was still dazed, he kicked the statue and sent it, along with Yan Tianzhi, tumbling off the stage.

Lu Yang emerged victorious.

Young Creed Leader Lu fought his way through countless opponents and finally reached the finals, facing his lifelong nemesis—Meng Jingzhou.

After Lu Yang meditated to replenish his spirit energy, the finals commenced.

Meng Jingzhou couldn’t wait any longer and jumped onto the stage eagerly. With a sinister chortle, he cracked his knuckles. “Hehe, it’s finally my turn.”

After training with Qiu Jin’an, he finally had the opportunity to fully showcase his skills and put the unruly Lu Yang in his place. So what if you’re the acting sect leader? When it’s time to get your butt kicked, there’s no escaping!

“Meng Jingzhou, Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“Young Creed Leader, Heavenly Court Creed.”

“Let’s talk it over,” Lu Yang transmitted an auditory message. “Help me put on a show this time, and I’ll return the favor next time.” We’re fellow disciples after all. It’s best to avoid fighting if we can to preserve unity.

“You think I won’t beat you just because you said so? Tell you what, I’m dead set on beating you today!” Meng Jingzhou wasn’t about to let go of this opportunity.

Lu Yang sighed and switched tactics. “Then, as acting sect leader, I order you to admit defeat.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

“How about we talk it over again?”

Chapter 499: Full-On Acting

Due to Lu Yang’s tyrannical abuse of authority, Meng Jingzhou was cowed into agreeing to the terms—this time, he would play along and let Lu Yang shine, and next time, Lu Yang would return the favor.

The two greatest prodigies of their generation clashed. Although it was all an act, neither held back in the slightest. The spectators below were all cultivators seasoned in combat. If the two pulled their punches, the ruse would easily be exposed. Thus, they fought with everything they had.

Their battle was a storm of strength, speed, and reflexes. Even other prodigies on the same stage could only gape in disbelief. Compared to these two, winning the provincial-level competition and representing an entire province seemed to mean nothing. A massive gulf still existed between prodigies.

Even those reforged cultivators felt a chill in their hearts. Despite their painstaking efforts to disperse their cultivation and cultivate anew, they still couldn’t measure up to true prodigies.

The Battle of the Great Era is truly terrifying!

Lu Yang’s swordsmanship was so exquisite that even Ming Tai felt ashamed of his own inferiority. Meng Jingzhou’s fist techniques embodied the true essence of Third Elder’s teachings, bringing the strengths of a physique cultivator to their fullest potential. Every part of his body had been tempered to perfection, where even the Transcendent Tribulation old ancestors could find no fault.

“The Meng bloodline is truly fearsome...” an old ancestor murmured in awe.

Despite the Meng Family’s notoriety for troublemaking in the imperial capital, their position as the number one ancestral clan remained unshakable, all thanks to their indisputable, overwhelming strength. Even these Transcendent Tribulation old ancestors couldn’t help but feel a prickle of dread at the Meng Family’s power. Yet what they had witnessed was still far from the Meng Family’s full might.

Meng Jingzhou’s grand fist seals encompassed yang energy that could suppress demons and ghosts, shake heaven and earth, and conquer all obstacles; even ferocious beasts would cower before their brilliance.

Lu Yang’s sword qi surged forth like rivers breaching their dikes as they slashed through the fist seals.

The fierce battle was so evenly matched that the watching prodigies couldn’t help but clench their sweaty fists, their eyes fixed on every moment unfolding atop the stage. Only by focusing completely could they hope to keep up with the two combatants’ movements. These were true peers, and everything they learned from them would be immensely beneficial to their growth in combat.

Cough! A moment of negligence left Meng Jingzhou grazed by a sword qi. His qi and blood leaked out, putting him at a disadvantage.

Lu Yang pressed the advantage, allowing him no chance for respite.

“Meng Jingzhou, don’t give up!” someone shouted out their inner voice.

Meng Jingzhou represented the prodigies of their era—their hope. They couldn’t bear to see the Heavenly Court Creed win.

“Defeat this Young Creed Leader Lu!”

“Show them that this is now Great Xia’s era, not their ancient era of tyranny!”

The cheers reached Meng Jingzhou’s ears one by one, but unfortunately, against such consummate acting, they were meaningless.

“Heaven-Shaking Six Forms!” As if he was galvanized, Meng Jingzhou prepared to go all out, his veins bulging and his eyes bloodshot.

Lu Yang drew two fingers along his blade, offering his blood as a sacrifice to unleash his ultimate move. “Void-Breaking Sword Spell!”

Boom! The two drained every last bit of their spirit energy in this decisive showdown, kicking up a whirlwind of dust that swept across the arena.

Whoosh! A figure was sent flying, coughing blood, and grievously wounded.

“It’s the Heavenly Court Creed who got sent flying!” Someone yelled elatedly. This so-called Young Creed Leader Lu is finally gravely wounded. It’s the first time something like this has happened!

Lu Yang knelt on one knee with his sword planted into the ground, dazed from the enormous impact.

But before the crowd could rejoice, the dust dispersed, revealing Meng Jingzhou sprawled on the ground, blood pooling around him. His breathing was faint, and his injuries were far worse than Lu Yang’s!

Meng Jingzhou’s fingers twitched. He struggled to open his eyes, attempting to rise several times, but his limbs refused to obey.

Unwilling as he was, he could only give up on getting back to his feet.

In contrast, although Lu Yang knelt wounded on the ground, he still had enough strength to smile and speak.

The outcome was decided.

The referee gritted his teeth. Letting an ancient person claim victory is a humiliation for Great Xia, but as a referee, I can’t show favoritism.

“I declare...Meng Jingzhou...defeated.” The last word quivered on his lips, forced out only after a long, reluctant pause.

The referee checked on Meng Jingzhou’s condition and exhaled in relief. Thankfully, his injuries are severe but not life-threatening; they won’t affect his foundation.

The five heavenly kings leaped onto the stage, supporting their young creed leader.

“Young Creed Leader, are you alright?”

“Cough, cough... I’ll live. What a thrilling battle!” Lu Yang grinned, blood trickling from the corner of his mouth.

The Golden Flame Heavenly King hurriedly produced a small medicinal vial. When it became uncorked, a fragrant medicinal aroma suffused the air. He tipped out two golden pills, feeding them to Lu Yang. The latter immediately sat cross-legged to meditate, and his wounds and spirit energy began to recover rapidly.

~~~

Meng Jingzhou had lost.

The prodigy representing the current era of Intermediate Golden Core cultivators had lost.

Many couldn’t accept this reality.

So close! He was just a hair’s breadth away from victory!

Seventh Elder’s pills were highly effective. Lu Yang was soon fully healed. Under the five heavenly kings’ escort, he rose to his feet and gazed up to see the austere faces of the Five Great Immortal Sects’ leaders and the Eldest Prince Jiang Qun. “It looks like the prodigies of this era do have some skill. Not bad in combat. It’s a pity it’s just some skill—nothing more.”

The crowd erupted in outrage. That’s too cocky! What do you mean by “nothing more?” Everyone saw that the difference between you two was paper-thin. A single tiny detail could have tipped the scales. Given another match, who could say who would win?!

“Young Creed Leader Lu, your words dismiss the prodigies of this era too lightly,” Sect Leader Lu said with a meaningful look, his tone laden with warning. “You should know there’s always someone greater out there. This world doesn’t belong to your Heavenly Court Creed.”

Young Creed Leader Lu sneered, as if he was mocking Sect Leader Lu’s ignorance. “Someone greater out there? That’s just the excuse mediocrities use after losing. In terms of talent, who could surpass me?”

The Nether World Heavenly King gazed down at the crowd in contempt. “Had the ancient immortals not suppressed our young creed leader, he would have become an immortal in ancient times. How could he have waited until now?”

Young Creed Leader Lu shot the solemn Nether World Heavenly King a sidelong glance and waved his hand impatiently. “Enough, Protector Nether World. I’m in good spirits for once. Let’s not talk about these unhappy matters.”

“Yes.” The Nether World Heavenly King made no further comments and stepped back like a clay statue.

The crowd inhaled sharply, their astonishment beyond words. Is this Young Creed Leader Lu so talented that even immortals envied him?

Just how heaven-defying must his talent be?

There were only clear records of the Four Ancient Immortals, though no accounts had ever described their talents. In other words, Young Creed Leader Lu’s talent was without precedent in all of history.

“It’s just empty boasts. Since you’re so confident, Young Creed Leader Lu, why don’t you spar with me?” To everyone’s surprise, Sect Leader Lu jumped down from the judges' platform, landing steadily on the arena.

Young Creed Leader Lu toyed with his fingers. “Speaking of which, Sect Leader Lu, you’re also at the Intermediate Golden Core Stage. You could be considered an opponent. But I don’t like your tone.”

Their gazes locked, sparks practically flying between them. The five heavenly kings tactfully withdrew to avoid disrupting their young creed leader’s good mood.

“Bring it on then?”

“Bring it on!”

Chapter 500: Sect Leader Lu Against Young Creed Leader Lu

The battle between Lu Yang and Lu Yang raged with ferocious intensity.

Sect Leader Lu was well-versed in spell techniques, wielding elemental spells with effortless grace. He had even touched upon the pinnacles of temporal and spatial spells, and his seamless fusion of spells and fists had sent the leaders of the four Great Immortal Sects fleeing in disarray.

On the other hand, Young Creed Leader Lu specialized in sword spells. Despite his youth, his comprehension of the Sword Dao already far surpassed peers of the same cultivation realm, rivaling even those at the Nascent Soul Stage.

“Who will win? It’s said that this Sect Leader Lu is incredibly gifted in spells and even created several unique ones. Few in history have invented their own spells at this cultivation realm.”

“At the Qing Province Grand Ceremony, he fought two opponents at once, defeating both Bai Ming and Lan Ting. Yet, no one could discern the true nature of his golden core.”

“It’s hard to say who will win. Didn’t you hear Young Creed Leader Lu? He is so talented that even immortals had to suppress him!”

Lu Yang was truly an unparalleled expert. His every movement commanded the undivided attention of the crowd.

The leaders of the four Great Immortal Sects and the Eldest Imperial Prince Jiang Qun watched especially closely, curious to see how Lu Yang would fight himself.

The moment Sect Leader Lu jumped down from the arena stage, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy relinquished control of his body, allowing Lu Yang to control both bodies in battle.

“Lu Yang, fight well! You must defeat that fellow on the other side. You’re representing our Dao-Seeking Sect in this battle!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy cheered from Sect Leader Lu’s mental space before darting over to Young Creed Leader Lu’s mental space.

“Crush that guy from the Dao-Seeking Sect on the other side. We must make a name for our Heavenly Court Creed!”

“...Immortal Fairy, if you have nothing better to do, you can just rest.”

“Oh. Alright.”

During the period when the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was acting sect leader and used Lu Yang’s body to cultivate, his cultivation had indeed grown significantly, especially his mental power, which had ascended to new heights.

In the past, controlling two bodies demanded his full concentration, leaving no room for distraction. But now, he could control two bodies while still having enough energy to placate the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

To the outside world, Sect Leader Lu and Young Creed Leader Lu were locked in a fierce stalemate, each gaining and losing ground in turn.

Sect Leader Lu spat out the Three Flavor True Fire, which split into three distinct streams, each with its own flavor. The three flames lashed like tongues, licking the air and raising the temperature.

Young Creed Leader Lu flicked his wrist, shooting three sharp sword qi. “Three Sparrows Take Flight!”

Boom! Boom! Boom!

The sword qi and true fires collided in violent explosions, the resulting heat waves stinging the two combatants’ faces.

Sect Leader Lu employed Shrinking Earth, attempting an ambush from below, yet Young Creed Leader Lu seemed clairvoyant, evading right before Sect Leader Lu suddenly darted out from the ground.

Sect Leader Lu studied Young Creed Leader Lu solemnly. “Clairvoyance and a clear sword heart. I heard my shifu once say that only those devoted to the sword and obsessed with it can achieve such clarity. Your comprehension of the Sword Dao has already reached this level?”

Young Creed Leader Lu smirked, wiping a streak of blood from his cheek. Despite predicting the attack and dodging in advance, he was still a beat slower and was grazed on the face.

“You’re no less simple yourself. You created a brand new true fire by modeling after the Three Esse True Fire, and that underground movement spell earlier resembled Earth Escape, yet not entirely so. Did you create that too?

“A Golden Core cultivator inventing two elemental spells...such a feat was unheard of even in the ancient era!”

Suddenly, Sect Leader Lu shrank to a mere three inches tall. Wreathed in Three Flavor True Fire, he darted across the ground at blinding speed and unleashed the Arhat Fist. Despite his diminutive size, the sheer pressure behind each blow forced Young Creed Leader Lu to parry with his sword rather than risk engaging head-on.

The miniature Sect Leader Lu’s fist techniques packed astonishing power, accompanied by sound waves of Buddhist chants filled with compassion for the world. His tiny knuckles landed on the sword with clear, bell-like clangs.

Young Creed Leader Lu’s swordsmanship was also not to be trifled with. The sword tip thrust toward Sect Leader Lu three times in rapid succession. Each strike came within a hair’s breadth, and Sect Leader Lu narrowly dodged them all.

A hundred exchanges later, neither had gained the upper hand.

Every move was fatal, and any misstep could lead to defeat. However, both reacted with lightning reflexes, countering and retaliating in the shortest time possible.

The prodigies in the audience watched with bated breath, their eyes fixed on the intricate contest of offense and fence on stage, unwilling to miss a single detail. By now, they had forgotten their allegiances; all they cared about was what shocking moves the two combatants would showcase next.

A hundred and twenty exchanges later, the two disengaged simultaneously, gasping for breath as they replenished their spirit energy. The relentless battle had depleted their spirit energy.

“They say sword cultivators are capable of One Sword Breaks All Spells. I didn’t believe it in the past, but I’ve seen it for myself today.” Sect Leader Lu scrutinized Young Creed Leader Lu’s expression, searching for an opening.

“You flatter me, Sect Leader Lu. I once believed that I could go anywhere in this vast world with my sword, that none of those prodigies were worth a fraction of my sword’s might. Now that I’ve faced you, I’ve learned that there’s still someone obstructing my path to immortal ascension!”

The Hundred Herbs Heavenly King watched the scene before his eyes and involuntarily muttered just loud enough for those around him to hear, “The young creed leader has never praised anyone like this before.”

The four other heavenly kings nodded. “The young creed leader is a proud person. Only our creed leader and Dou Heavenly Sovereign can make him lower his head in respect. I never thought he’d finally encounter a rival he’s long yearned for. Truly rare.”

“A pity we left in haste. Had we brought the four holy sons, this battle might have unfolded differently.”

Four holy sons?

The onlookers ruminated over it. Could the Heavenly Court Creed harbor four other peerless geniuses apart from this young creed leader?

The four holy sons were none other than Meng Jingzhou, Tao Yaoye, Man Gu, and Li Haoran. Qin Yanyan was technically also a member of the Heavenly Court Creed, but her current identity was the reincarnation of Qin Haoran.

Lu Yang fought with himself for another eighty exchanges without an apparent victor before halting.

“Satisfying! I’ve never fought a cultivator at the same realm to my heart’s content!” Young Creed Leader Lu threw his head back and laughed uproariously, wild and unrestrained. He no longer looked at Sect Leader Lu condescendingly.

Sect Leader Lu replied with a smile. “Should we continue? I’m afraid we may fight until dawn without an outcome. There’s little point in further combat. Why don’t we call it quits?”

After a brief pause, Young Creed Leader Lu agreed.

“Let’s end it here then. I’ve underestimated the prodigies of the current era. With you around, I’m sure the upcoming Battle of the Great Era won’t be dull!”

Sect Leader Lu remained as courteous as ever. “To come uninvited is discourteous. Heavenly Court Creed, please leave.”

Young Creed Leader Lu was not annoyed despite being chased away. With a wave of his hand, he turned to leave. “Five protectors, we depart.”

“Yes!”

The Heavenly Court Creed had arrived on clouds, and on clouds they departed, flying out of the Dao-Seeking Sect under countless gazes.

~~~

Backstage, while resting to tend to his wounds, Meng Jingzhou simmered with indignation upon witnessing the scene. “Damn it, I got the short end of the stick!”

“Brother Meng, what’s wrong?” Man Gu asked.

Aside from Li Haoran, the other three heavenly sons of the Heavenly Court Creed were hiding backstage.

As Man Gu’s and Tao Yaoye’s acting skills were lacking, they could easily expose themselves if they appeared in public, so they had been watching from backstage all this time.

“That brat Lu Yang got to show off twice! Yet he only promised he’d help me do it once!”

Chapter 501: The Celebration Concludes

Sect Leader Lu and Young Creed Leader Lu’s fight ended in a draw, greatly lifting the spirits of the gathered prodigies and sweeping away the pent-up frustration in their chests.

On the other hand, the reforged cultivators wore grave expressions. With remarkable geniuses from the ancient Heavenly Court ahead and the modern era’s prodigies behind, they found themselves caught in between. That meant they had little hope of securing a place in the upcoming Battle of the Great Era.

On the viewing platform, Qiu Jin’an withdrew his gaze, exhaling slowly as he reflected on the battle. “The younger generation is indeed formidable.”

Jiang Qun asked curiously, “Are you talking about how Sect Leader Lu already possesses such combat power despite his young age?”

“No, I’m talking about how he’s an even better swindler than that old Taciturn scoundrel. When the old Taciturn scoundrel was his age, his deception skills were still puerile, though, admittedly, so was I, falling for his tricks again and again.

“Lu Yang is different. His deception skills are flawless. He’s not just fooling a few people—he’s fooling the entire world.”

Jiang Qun, “...”

He was grateful to have been born later than the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s era. Otherwise, how miserable would I have been?

Qiu Jin’an continued, “Still, this kid Lu Yang has one redeeming quality—he only scams outsiders, never his own people. I should have Bai Ming spend more time with Lu Yang. This boy’s talented and sharp-witted, but compared to Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, he’s lacking too much.”

Yang Ding concurred. “Tianzhi is worse. He’s too single-minded. He should also learn from Lu Yang.”

Luo Hongxia, however, would never let her dear disciple get close to Lu Yang. Who knows what horrors would await?

Master Jiesha likewise dared not let his disciple associate closely with Lu Yang. Monks do not speak of falsehoods. I can’t risk my disciple getting led astray by Lu Yang.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy merrily reclaimed control of Lu Yang’s body and returned to her seat in the center of the judges.

“Everyone’s busy? Shall we resume the competition?”

The tournament was only halfway through, with several more categories to go.

The matches progressed smoothly—Advanced Golden Core Stage, Basic Nascent Soul Stage... Occasionally, an astounding cultivator would appear, not due to astonishing combat power but their shocking ideas.

The Luoshui Guard and immortal sects discreetly observed these individuals, identifying potential reforged cultivators, experts pretending to be weak, or anomalies like Kong Hao, who had an old taowu sealed within him. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy and the immortal sect leaders also discussed suspicious cultivators.

As the tournament neared its end, a list was compiled, and the imperial court took over, investigating the backgrounds of the individuals flagged.

After ten thrilling days of competition, the tournament concluded, marking the end of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s celebration.

“At last, it’s over.” Lu Yang heaved a sigh of relief. He had handled everything for this celebration, while the Everlasting Immortal Fairy hadn’t helped in the slightest.

“Second-In-Command, well done!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was not stingy with verbal praise.

Lu Yang dared not take credit, replying humbly, “It was all thanks to your brilliant delegation in working one person to the bone.”

Jiang Qun called out to Lu Yang. “Sect Leader Lu, when you visit the imperial capital in the future, you must come to my estate. I’ll warmly welcome you!” He recognized Lu Yang as a talent—a significant help when the time came to evade the throne.

Not to mention, Sect Leader Lu casually referred to Yun Zhi as “Lass Yun.” I don’t even dare to think further about their relationship.

~~~

With the celebration over, only the final segment—division of spoils—was underway.

Amid the crowd, Luo Hongxia carefully whipped out a tightly wrapped treasure box. “Be gentle; don’t damage the box. This is my immortal palace’s supreme pressure, not your makeup case.”

As Luo Hongxia activated the treasure box, beams of light shot out and transported everyone into the box.

Inside, the Great Yu cultivators were still desperately pounding against the barriers. Three Transcendent Tribulation joined forces, their attacks earth-shaking, yet their efforts were futile against the treasure box sealed by a single drop of Yun Zhi’s blood.

“Don’t be scared, everyone! The Imperial Preceptor is still outside. By now, he has probably already launched an attack. He’ll surely save us!” The Black-White Venerable Lord rallied the group.

Calculating the time in his head, the celebration’s conclusion was the perfect opportunity for the Imperial Preceptor to strike. “Look, the seal is breaking!” The Black-White Venerable Lord pointed at a nearby light, his shout reigniting hope among the Great Yu cultivators.

However, when the seal was lifted, what awaited them was a flood of Great Xia cultivators pouring in like dumplings into a pot.

“My Heart-Locking Sect contributed greatly to the capture. We deserve one of the Great Yu cultivators!”

“Hey hey hey, Old Li, did you forget you lost all your Great Yu cultivators to my Void-Breaking Sect during the tournament?”

“Don’t spout nonsense. Gambling’s illegal. Who gambled with you?”

“...Do you have no shame?”

“Listen to me, everyone. Let’s sit down and discuss how to divide the Great Yu cultivators.” As a new Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, Lu Baqian stepped forward to maintain order.

With everyone’s interests at stake, the argument grew heated until Lu Baqian diverted their attention.

After everyone taught Lu Baqian a lesson, the One-Qi Venerable Lord finally stepped in to restore order for the big picture.

Lu Yang yawned repeatedly as he listened to their discussion, paying no attention to the final outcome. He only noted that the strongest Great Yu cultivator, the Black-White Venerable Lord, was assigned to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

As for the rest, they can keep arguing.

“By the way, Venerable Lord, have you decided how to deal with the old taowu?” Lu Yang asked the One-Qi Venerable Lord before leaving the box. As his identity was Young Creed Leader Lu at the time, he hadn’t been in a position to inquire about Kong Hao.

“Kong Hao insisted on maintaining the seal, hoping to coexist peacefully with the old taowu. He believes he can eventually reform the old taowu and become friends with it.”

“Well, I suppose that’s also an option.” Lu Yang couldn’t help but feel uneasy for Kong Hao.

The old taowu can’t hold a candle to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. The Immortal Fairy is beautiful, kind, beloved by all, harmless, and won’t turn on her own people, while an old demon like that taowu might scheme against Kong Hao any time.

But this is Kong Hao’s choice, after all. It’s not for me to interfere.

Yun Zhi dragged the Black-White Venerable Lord by the collar as she departed the treasure box with Lu Yang.

“Speaking of which, where did the Imperial Preceptor go?” After exiting, Lu Yang suddenly realized the Imperial Preceptor had never appeared, and even Yun Zhi hadn’t located him. He had remained vigilant, expecting him to act during the finale, yet nothing happened.

Lu Yang mused, “Strange, did he sense something amiss and flee?” This Imperial Preceptor is really a slippery one.

“Hmm? The barbeque shop?” Lu Yang looked up to find himself outside the barbeque shop.

Chefs Liu and Gao were tidying up the grill, Little Five, Little Six, and Little Seven cleared the dishes, while the creed leader was sweeping and mopping.

He had hoped for a simple meal, but seeing they were closing shop, he decided against asking them to reopen.

“Lu Yang’s here! Come in, come in!” The creed leader ushered him inside enthusiastically.

In the Dao-Seeking Sect, Lu Yang is our backer. Why am I so cordial to Lu Yang? Is it because he’s Yun Zhi’s Little Junior Brother? But I can’t help but feel like there’s another reason...

Who had warned me to treat Lu Yang with the utmost courtesy, even more than I would him?

Who was it again?

Noticing the creed leader’s daze, Lu Yang asked curiously, “Is something wrong?”

Snapping back to his senses, the creed leader realized his lapse. “Oh, it’s nothing. Please sit.”

Lu Yang glanced around, feeling like someone was missing. “Where’s the Everlasting Immortal? At the breeding farm?”

“Who?”
